# MOONSHELL ISLAND

# ==================================================

Sea: East Blue Classification: Original Island World Type: One Piece
Parallel World

------------------------------------------------------------------------

# OVERVIEW

Moonshell Island is a tranquil island famous for its brilliant white
beaches and rare moon-colored shells that wash ashore during certain
tides. The island thrives on fishing, shellcraft, and coastal trade
while remaining relatively untouched by large-scale conflict.

------------------------------------------------------------------------

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Small

Terrain

-   White Sand Beaches

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\EB-012_LOGUETOWN.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# LOGUETOWN
# ==================================================

Sea: East Blue
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Loguetown is the largest commercial city in East Blue and serves as the primary gateway to Reverse Mountain and the Grand Line. Nearly every captain sailing toward the Grand Line eventually visits Loguetown to resupply, recruit crew members, repair ships, and prepare for the dangerous voyage ahead.

Because of its strategic location, Loguetown maintains one of East Blue's strongest Marine presences. Merchants, bounty hunters, pirates, craftsmen, scholars, and travelers from every Blue can be found within its busy streets.

Although considered one of the safest major cities in East Blue, criminal organizations constantly attempt to exploit its enormous flow of commerce.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Large

Approximate Diameter

145 km

Travel Time by Foot

3–4 Days

Highest Elevation

Execution Hill

Terrain Distribution

30% Urban

25% Forest

20% Plains

15% Hills

10% Coastline

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Warm Maritime

Spring

Comfortable temperatures with occasional rain.

Summer

Hot and humid.

Autumn

Strong sea winds.

Ideal sailing conditions.

Winter

Cool but rarely cold.

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources

- Fresh Water
- Hardwood
- Fish
- Clay
- Limestone

Rare Resources

- High-quality Ship Timber
- Navigation Minerals

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Central City

Political and commercial center.

---

## Harbor District

Merchant docks, warehouses and shipyards.

---

## Market Quarter

Largest marketplace in East Blue.

---

## Marine District

Marine Headquarters and military facilities.

---

## Old Town

Historic residential district.

---

## Execution Hill

Historic landmark overlooking the city.

---

# SETTLEMENTS

Loguetown is the largest urban settlement in East Blue. Unlike most islands that revolve around a single village, the city is divided into specialized districts connected by wide roads, canals, and public plazas.

---

## Central City

Type

Capital District

Population

Approximately 31,000

Description

The administrative heart of Loguetown. Government offices, banks, public institutions, and large merchant companies operate here.

Major Facilities

- City Hall
- Central Plaza
- Public Library
- General Hospital
- Banking House
- Commercial Court
- Grand Hotel

Primary Occupations

- Government Officials
- Merchants
- Lawyers
- Bankers
- Doctors
- Scholars

---

## Harbor District

Type

Commercial Port

Population

Approximately 12,000

Description

The busiest harbor in East Blue. Hundreds of vessels enter and leave each week carrying cargo destined for every Blue and the Grand Line.

Major Facilities

- Cargo Docks
- Dry Dock
- Customs Office
- Shipyards
- Warehouses
- Fish Market
- Marine Inspection Pier

Primary Occupations

- Sailors
- Dock Workers
- Shipwrights
- Merchants
- Warehouse Workers

---

## Market Quarter

Type

Commercial District

Population

Approximately 8,500

Description

An enormous marketplace selling nearly every legal product available within East Blue.

Popular Businesses

- Weapon Shops
- Clothing Stores
- Bookstores
- Restaurants
- Medical Suppliers
- Navigation Equipment
- Blacksmiths

---

## Old Town

Type

Residential District

Population

Approximately 11,000

Description

The oldest neighborhood in Loguetown.

Stone streets, historical buildings and family-owned businesses preserve the city's early history.

---

## Marine District

Type

Military Zone

Population

Approximately 2,800

Description

Restricted military district containing the city's Marine headquarters and training facilities.

Civilian access is limited.

---

# HARBORS

Loguetown possesses the busiest harbor network in East Blue.

---

International Trade

# GOVERNMENT

## Political System

Loguetown is administered by a civilian city government under the authority of the World Government.

Daily administration is managed by the Mayor and City Council while Marine authorities retain jurisdiction over piracy, international crime, and maritime security.

Departments

- Commerce
- Infrastructure
- Finance
- Public Health
- Harbor Administration
- Public Safety
- Education

---

# LAW ENFORCEMENT

## City Guard

The City Guard maintains law and order within civilian districts.

Responsibilities

- Patrol Streets
- Investigate Crimes
- Traffic Control
- Public Safety
- Festival Security

The City Guard cooperates closely with Marine investigators during major criminal cases.

---

# MARINE PRESENCE

- City Guard
- Harbor Authority
- Merchant Guild
- Medical Association
- Customs Office

Joint operations are common due to the city's strategic importance.

---

# ECONOMY

## Economic Profile

Loguetown possesses the largest economy in East Blue.

Its strategic location before Reverse Mountain allows it to serve as the final resupply point for ships preparing to enter the Grand Line.

Economic Stability

★★★★★

Belly

Very High

- Government Services

Loguetown connects East Blue with every other major sea through merchant fleets.

Ships regularly depart toward

- Shells Town
- Orange Town
- Syrup Village
- Baratie

Influence

★★★★★

---

# BANKING

Loguetown possesses East Blue's largest banking district.

Services

- Currency Exchange
- Merchant Loans
- Trade Financing
- Safe Deposits
- Letters of Credit

Large commercial transactions are almost entirely paper-based rather than cash.

---

# CRIME

Overall Crime Level

Moderate

Although heavily protected by Marines, the enormous population attracts organized crime.

Common Crimes

- Pickpocketing
- Counterfeit Currency
- Cargo Theft
- Smuggling
- Illegal Gambling
- Fraud

Violent crime remains relatively uncommon within the city center.

---

# ORGANIZED CRIME

Several criminal groups secretly compete for influence over harbor commerce.

Activities include

- Smuggling
- Money Laundering
- Illegal Auctions
- Forged Documents
- Black-market Shipping

Most organizations avoid direct confrontation with Marines.

---

# BLACK MARKET

Despite strict Marine enforcement, an underground market continues to operate within hidden warehouses.

Common Contraband

- Illegal Weapons
- Stolen Cargo
- Forged Identification
- Counterfeit Belly
- Smuggled Medicine

Transactions usually occur at night through intermediaries.

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Pirate Threat Level

High Outside Harbor

Low Inside Harbor

Many pirate crews visit Loguetown to purchase supplies before entering the Grand Line.

Most avoid causing trouble inside the city due to the overwhelming Marine presence.

Typical Crew Size

10–40 Pirates

Average Bounty

8,000,000–25,000,000 Belly

Devil Fruit users remain uncommon but appear more frequently than elsewhere in East Blue.

---

## Common Pirate Activities

- Purchasing Supplies
- Recruiting Crew Members
- Selling Loot
- Gathering Intelligence
- Secret Meetings
- Smuggling

---

# SECURITY LEVEL

Marine Headquarters

★★★★★

Central City

★★★★★

Market Quarter

★★★★☆

Harbor District

★★★★☆

★★★☆☆

Outer Warehouses

★★★☆☆

Hidden Alleys

★★☆☆☆

Abandoned Dockyards

★★☆☆☆
---

# CULTURE

## General Culture

Loguetown is often called **"The City of Beginnings and Endings."**

For many people, it is the final destination of a peaceful life.

For adventurers, pirates, Marines, and merchants, it is the first step toward the Grand Line.

Because thousands of travelers arrive every month, the city has developed one of the most diverse cultures in East Blue.

Residents are accustomed to meeting people from every sea and generally judge others by their actions rather than their origins.

---

## Hospitality

Visitors are welcomed regardless of occupation, provided they obey local laws.

Restaurants, inns, taverns, and bathhouses remain open late into the night due to the constant flow of travelers.

---

## Social Classes

### Government Officials

Responsible for administration and public services.

---

### Merchants

One of the wealthiest and most influential groups.

Many own shipping companies operating throughout East Blue.

---

### Craftsmen

Highly respected.

Especially

- Shipwrights
- Blacksmiths
- Navigators
- Cartographers

---

### Sailors

Merchant sailors form a large portion of the city's workforce.

---

### Dock Workers

Responsible for loading and unloading cargo around the clock.

---

# EDUCATION

Public education is available throughout the city.

Core Subjects

- Reading
- Writing
- Mathematics
- Geography
- Navigation
- Maritime Law
- History
- Commerce

Private academies also offer advanced education for navigation, engineering, and finance.

---

# RELIGION

No official religion exists.

Many residents instead observe traditional ceremonies honoring

- The Sea
- Ancestors
- Safe Voyages

Small shrines are scattered throughout the city.

---

# FESTIVALS

## Founder's Festival

Celebrates the establishment of Loguetown.

Activities

- Fireworks
- Music
- Merchant Fair
- Street Performances

---

## Harbor Festival

Held each summer.

Includes

- Ship Parade
- Sailing Competition
- Seafood Market
- Navigation Contest

---

## Voyage Blessing Day

Before the beginning of the major sailing season, priests, navigators, and harbor officials bless departing ships.

---

# RUMORS

Game Masters may introduce these naturally.

1. A merchant recently purchased an ancient sea chart for an enormous fortune.

2. Strange lights have been seen beneath the abandoned eastern docks.

3. Someone has been forging Marine documents.

4. Several cargo ships disappeared shortly after leaving Loguetown.

5. A hidden warehouse secretly stores stolen Grand Line goods.

6. Pirates are searching for an unknown artifact hidden somewhere in the city.

7. An underground tunnel supposedly connects the harbor to Old Town.

8. A wealthy collector quietly purchases historical relics every month.

9. A mysterious navigator predicts storms with impossible accuracy.

10. An abandoned lighthouse still shines on moonless nights.

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|-----------|
|1|Marine patrol requests identification.|
|2|Merchant offers temporary work.|
|3|Street performer gathers a large crowd.|
|4|Lost child asks for help.|
|5|Cargo accident blocks the street.|
|6|Bounty hunters question local witnesses.|
|7|Heavy rain floods nearby roads.|
|8|Traveling doctor treats injured sailors.|
|9|Warehouse workers discover suspicious cargo.|
|10|A cloaked stranger quietly follows the party.|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

Escort an important merchant convoy preparing to enter the Grand Line.

Investigate counterfeit Belly coins circulating throughout the markets.

Discover who is financing an expanding smuggling network.

Search abandoned warehouses for missing government cargo.

Protect a famous navigator targeted by pirates.

Investigate strange disappearances around the eastern docks.

Recover confidential Marine documents before they reach criminals.

Locate an underground tunnel used by organized crime.

Stop illegal weapon shipments hidden among merchant cargo.

Uncover the truth behind a forgotten historical landmark.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## Forgotten Warehouse

An abandoned warehouse beneath the Harbor District.

Contains sealed cargo dating back decades.

---

## Underground Smuggling Tunnel

Secret passage connecting Old Town with hidden harbor caves.

Still partially operational.

---

## Lighthouse Archive

A forgotten archive beneath the city's oldest lighthouse.

Contains navigation records more than one hundred years old.

---

## Hidden Naval Bunker

An emergency military facility constructed beneath the Marine Headquarters.

Only senior officers know of its existence.

---

# SECRETS

Several respected merchants secretly cooperate with smugglers to avoid customs inspections.

A forgotten tunnel beneath Loguetown predates the city's modern construction.

One senior government official has accepted bribes from organized crime for years.

Ancient navigation records hidden beneath the lighthouse describe sea routes that no longer appear on modern maps.

A criminal syndicate plans to establish a permanent black-market auction inside the Harbor District.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

5–10 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Beginning to Intermediate Characters

Core Themes

- Maritime Adventure
- Trade
- Justice
- Crime Investigation
- Politics
- Exploration

## GM Guidance

Loguetown should feel like a living metropolis where hundreds of independent stories unfold every day.

Merchant prices, Marine patrols, public opinion, criminal activity, and trade volume should evolve naturally in response to player actions.

Because it is the final major stop before the Grand Line, Loguetown is an excellent location for:

- Recruiting crew members
- Purchasing equipment
- Gathering intelligence
- Introducing rival crews
- Beginning long-term story arcs
- Establishing recurring NPCs

Player choices made here can have lasting consequences that echo throughout the rest of the campaign.

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\ECONOMY.md
# =====================================================

# EAST BLUE ECONOMY

## Main Exports
- Fish
- Fruit
- Timber
- Grain
- Salt
- Iron

## Imports
- Medicine
- Luxury Goods
- Navigation Equipment
- Weapons

## Currency
Standard Belly economy.

## Trade
Merchant shipping is frequent between major islands.


# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\HISTORY.md
# =====================================================

# EAST BLUE HISTORY

## Parallel World Rule

Canon geography is preserved.
All historical figures are original characters.

---

## Early Era

Fishing settlements gradually expanded into trading ports.

---

## Trade Expansion

Merchant routes linked the major islands and encouraged Marine deployment.

---

## Age of Piracy

Local pirate crews emerged, targeting merchant shipping rather than conquering territory.

---

## Modern Era

East Blue is considered peaceful compared to the Grand Line but still experiences piracy, corruption, smuggling and political conflicts.

---

## GM Usage

History should influence politics, local traditions and rumors without forcing player outcomes.


# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\MARINE.md
# =====================================================

# EAST BLUE MARINES

## Purpose
The East Blue Marine Branch is responsible for maintaining order, suppressing piracy, protecting merchant traffic, enforcing World Government law, and responding to emergencies.

---

## Organization

### Regional Headquarters
Coordinates operations across East Blue.

### Local Bases
Located near major ports and populated islands.

### Outposts
Small stations responsible for nearby villages and shipping lanes.

---

## Responsibilities

- Patrol sea lanes
- Escort merchant vessels
- Investigate crimes
- Arrest pirates and bandits
- Disaster relief
- Protect World Government facilities

---

## Patrol Levels

| Level | Description |
|---|---|
| I | Harbor Patrol |
| II | Coastal Patrol |
| III | Open Sea Patrol |
| IV | Anti-Pirate Operation |
| V | Emergency Mobilization |

---

## Standard Fleet

### Patrol Boat
Crew: 10–30

### Medium Warship
Crew: 50–120

### Large Battleship
Crew: 150+

---

## Response Priority

1. Civilian distress
2. Pirate attack
3. Marine base emergency
4. Government request
5. Routine patrol

---

## Investigation Procedure

1. Receive report
2. Verify evidence
3. Dispatch patrol
4. Capture suspects
5. Submit report
6. Update bounty if necessary

---

## Relationships

### Civilians
Generally positive.

### Merchants
Strong cooperation.

### Pirates
Hostile.

---

## Corruption

Although Marine doctrine values justice, individual officers may abuse authority. Such corruption should remain local and become story hooks rather than the norm.

---

## GM Guidelines

Use Marines as an active organization rather than stationary NPCs.

- Patrols move between islands.
- Reports spread through Den Den Mushi.
- Pirate actions increase patrol frequency.
- Helping Marines improves reputation.


# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\PIRATES.md
# =====================================================

# EAST BLUE PIRATES

## Overview
Most pirate crews are inexperienced and operate locally.

## Typical Crew
- Crew Size: 5–30
- Average Bounty: 3–20 Million
- Devil Fruit Users: Rare
- Haki Users: Extremely Rare

## Activities
- Cargo theft
- Smuggling
- Port extortion
- Kidnapping
- Treasure hunting

## GM Notes
East Blue pirates should feel dangerous to civilians but not world-level threats.


# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\ROUTES.md
# =====================================================

# EAST BLUE ROUTES

## Major Civilian Route
Dawn Island → Shells Town → Orange Town → Syrup Village → Baratie → Loguetown

## Marine Routes
Frequent patrol loops connect Marine bases.

## Dangerous Areas
- Hidden reefs
- Pirate ambush zones
- Seasonal fog


# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\RUMORS.md
# =====================================================

# EAST BLUE RUMORS

Possible rumors for Game Masters:

1. A ghost ship has appeared offshore.
2. Pirates seek an old treasure map.
3. A Marine officer is accepting bribes.
4. A Devil Fruit washed onto a remote beach.
5. Sea Kings have been spotted unusually close to shore.
6. A merchant convoy disappeared without a trace.


# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\EAST_BLUE\SEA_INFORMATION.md
# =====================================================

# EAST BLUE SEA INFORMATION

## Overview
East Blue is the calmest of the Four Blues. Navigation is simple, weather is stable, piracy exists but is generally limited to small crews, and Marine influence is strong.

## Sea Characteristics
- Navigation Difficulty: Low
- Weather Stability: High
- Sea King Activity: Rare
- Average Wave Height: 1–5 m
- Visibility: Excellent

## Navigation
Uses compass, stars, sea charts and coastline. Log Pose is unnecessary.

## Common Wildlife
- Tuna
- Marlin
- Flying Fish
- Dolphins
- Sea Turtles
- Sharks

## Strategic Role
East Blue supplies food, timber, fish and recruits to the World Government and Marine forces.

## GM Notes
Ideal starting sea for beginner campaigns focused on exploration, local piracy and character growth.

# ISLAND_GENERATOR.md

> PROJECT ASTER ENGINE

# PURPOSE

ไฟล์นี้กำหนดมาตรฐานในการสร้างเกาะใหม่ (Original Island)

เกาะใหม่ทุกเกาะต้องให้ความรู้สึกว่าเป็นส่วนหนึ่งของจักรวาล One Piece

ห้ามสร้างเกาะที่ขัดกับกฎของโลก

ทุกเกาะต้องมีเหตุผลในการดำรงอยู่

---

# CORE PRINCIPLES

เมื่อสร้างเกาะใหม่

Game Master ต้องยึดหลักดังต่อไปนี้

- โลกมาก่อนเนื้อเรื่อง
- เกาะต้องมีเหตุผลในการดำรงอยู่
- ทุกเกาะมีเศรษฐกิจ
- ทุกเกาะมีวัฒนธรรม
- ทุกเกาะมีความขัดแย้ง
- ทุกเกาะมีความลับ
- ทุกเกาะสามารถเปลี่ยนแปลงได้

☐ มี Quest

☐ มีความลับ

☐ มีผลกระทบต่อโลก

☐ ผู้เล่นสามารถเปลี่ยนแปลงเกาะได้

---

# PARALLEL WORLD RULE

PROJECT ASTER ENGINE

ใช้เกาะ Canon เป็นแกนหลัก

และเพิ่ม Original Islands เข้าไปทั่วโลก

สัดส่วนแนะนำ

- Canon Islands : 70%

- Original Islands : 30%

เกาะ Original ต้องสามารถเชื่อมต่อกับภูมิศาสตร์ของ One Piece ได้อย่างสมเหตุสมผล

# ISLAND_TEMPLATE.md

> PROJECT ASTER ENGINE
> ONE PIECE PARALLEL WORLD RPG
> Folder : 01_WORLD/ISLANDS

---

# PURPOSE

ไฟล์นี้กำหนดมาตรฐานในการสร้างเกาะทั้งหมดภายใน PROJECT ASTER ENGINE

ทุกเกาะ ไม่ว่าจะเป็นเกาะจาก Canon หรือเกาะ Original ต้องใช้โครงสร้างเดียวกัน

เป้าหมายคือ

- ให้ข้อมูลเป็นมาตรฐานเดียวกัน
- ให้ AI สามารถอ่านและใช้งานได้ทันที
- ให้ผู้เล่นเดินทางไปเกาะใดก็ได้รับประสบการณ์ที่สอดคล้องกัน
- รองรับการสร้างเกาะใหม่ได้ไม่จำกัด

# CONNECTIONS

ความสัมพันธ์กับจักรพรรดิ

ความสัมพันธ์กับ Cross Guild

# PLAYER IMPACT

สิ่งที่ผู้เล่นสามารถเปลี่ยนแปลงได้

ตัวอย่าง

- เปลี่ยนผู้ปกครอง
- ปลดปล่อยเกาะ
- ทำลายเศรษฐกิจ
- สร้างชื่อเสียง
- ทำให้เกิดสงคราม
- ช่วยเหลือประชาชน
- ทำลายองค์กรอาชญากรรม

ทุกการกระทำของผู้เล่น

ต้องถูกบันทึกลง

09_LOGS

และส่งผลต่อ

NEWS_SYSTEM

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\NEW_WORLD\NEW WORLD CORE SYSTEM.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# NEW WORLD CORE SYSTEM (ONE PIECE RPG ENGINE)
# ==================================================
# ECONOMY / MARINES / PIRATES / GLOBAL POWER BALANCE
# ==================================================

Sea: New World  
Scope: World Core Simulation Layer (Meta System)

---

# 1. WORLD ECONOMY SYSTEM

## CORE MODEL: “MULTI-POWER CIRCULATION ECONOMY”

The New World economy is not free-market.  
It is controlled by **power blocs + territory control + maritime routes**.

---

## ECONOMIC CURRENCIES

### 1. BELLY (Standard Currency)
- Used in civilian markets
- Weak influence in New World politics

---

### 2. BOUNTY VALUE (INFLUENCE CURRENCY)
- Represents global threat level
- Can be “traded” by bounty hunters / pirates
- Impacts reputation and alliances

---

### 3. BLACK MARKET CREDITS
- Illegal currency
- Used in Hachinosu / underground networks
- Not traceable by World Government systems

---

### 4. STRATEGIC RESOURCES (NON-MONEY VALUE)
- Seastone (Kairoseki)
- Devil Fruits
- Ancient Weapons data
- Log Poses / Eternal Logs
- Weapon-grade metals

---

## ECONOMIC FLOW RULES

- Trade routes = controlled by military/pirate dominance
- Supply chains = vulnerable to war interruption
- Prices = fluctuate based on island stability index

---

## ECONOMIC STABILITY INDEX (0–100)

0–30 → Stable trade  
31–60 → Regional disruption  
61–80 → War economy  
81–100 → Collapse / black market dominance  

---

# 2. WORLD GOVERNMENT & MARINE SYSTEM

## CORE STRUCTURE: “GLOBAL MILITARY ADMINISTRATION”

---

## HIERARCHY

### 1. WORLD GOVERNMENT (TOP AUTHORITY)
- Controls laws, islands, and alliances
- Manages global political order
- Oversees Marine operations

---

### 2. MARINE HEADQUARTERS
- Main military enforcement branch
- Handles Yonko-level threats
- Executes global justice operations

---

### 3. MARINE BASE SYSTEM

- **Base Branches (Blue Seas)**
- **Grand Line Bases**
- **New World Fortified Bases**

---

## MARINE UNIT SYSTEM

### 1. STANDARD SOLDIERS
- Patrol and escort missions
- Low-tier combat capability

---

### 2. OFFICERS (LIEUTENANT – CAPTAIN)
- Island-level enforcement
- Anti-pirate operations

---

### 3. VICE ADMIRALS
- Regional disaster response units
- Anti-Yonko support force

---

### 4. ADMIRALS (TOP COMBAT FORCE)
- Natural disaster-level combat power
- Strategic war execution

---

### 5. SSG / SPECIAL SCIENTIFIC UNITS
- Advanced weapon systems
- Pacifista-type deployments
- Experimental combat technology

---

## MARINE OPERATIONS RULESET

- Pirates classified by bounty level
- Islands monitored by threat index
- War escalation requires approval chain

---

# 3. PIRATE SYSTEM

## CORE MODEL: “FREEDOM-BASED POWER STRUCTURE”

---

## PIRATE TIERS

### 1. CREW-LEVEL PIRATES
- Small groups
- Survival-focused

---

### 2. SUPER NOVA LEVEL
- Rising dangerous crews
- Territory disruption capability

---

### 3. YONKO CREW SYSTEM
- Multi-island control
- Fleet-based empire structure

---

### 4. YONKO (EMPIRE CORE)
- Controls large sea regions
- Political + military + economic dominance

---

## PIRATE ECONOMY

- Loot-based income
- Territory taxation (illegal)
- Black market trade
- Bounty hunting counter-system

---

## PIRATE WAR RULES

- No formal law
- Alliances are temporary
- Betrayal is expected system behavior
- Strength defines legitimacy

---

# 4. GLOBAL POWER STRUCTURE

## CORE TRI-POWER BALANCE

### 1. WORLD GOVERNMENT
- Law / control / suppression

---

### 2. PIRATES
- Chaos / freedom / expansion

---

### 3. REVOLUTIONARY ARMY
- Anti-system force
- Destabilizes global control

---

## BALANCE INDEX SYSTEM

Each faction has global influence rating:

0–100 POWER INDEX per faction

- 0–30 → Weak influence
- 31–60 → Regional control
- 61–80 → Global pressure force
- 81–100 → System-defining entity

---

# 5. REVOLUTIONARY ARMY SYSTEM

## CORE ROLE: “SYSTEM DISRUPTION FACTION”

---

## STRUCTURE

### 1. LEADER CORE
- Strategic global operations

---

### 2. ARMY COMMANDERS
- Regional uprising leaders

---

### 3. INFILTRATION UNITS
- Spy networks inside governments

---

## OPERATIONS

- Government destabilization
- Island liberation campaigns
- Information warfare
- Supply chain sabotage

---

# 6. SEA CONTROL SYSTEM

## CORE MECHANIC: “SEA ZONE DOMINANCE”

---

## SEA TIERS

### EAST BLUE
- Weakest system control

---

### GRAND LINE (PARADISE)
- Moderate chaos + structure

---

### NEW WORLD
- Full faction war zone
- Yonko-level dominance rules apply

---

## NEW WORLD RULES

- No safe travel guarantees
- Weather + geography unstable
- Territory changes dynamically
- Power determines survival

---

# 7. GLOBAL WAR DYNAMICS

## WAR TYPES

### 1. ECONOMIC WAR
- Trade disruption
- Black market control battles

---

### 2. TERRITORIAL WAR
- Island capture conflicts
- Yonko expansion wars

---

### 3. INFORMATION WAR
- Poneglyph / truth control
- History manipulation conflicts

---

### 4. TOTAL WAR STATE
- Marines + Pirates + Revolutionaries collide
- Entire sea system destabilizes

---

# 8. WORLD STABILITY INDEX

## GLOBAL SYSTEM HEALTH (0–100)

0–30 → Stable world order  
31–60 → Rising tensions  
61–80 → Active global conflict  
81–100 → System collapse risk  

---

# FINAL CORE RULE

> “In the New World, there is no peace system.  
There is only **balance between forces that want control, freedom, and destruction.**”

---

# END OF NEW WORLD CORE SYSTEM

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\NEW_WORLD\NW-001_FISH_MAN_ISLAND.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# NW-001: FISH-MAN ISLAND
# ==================================================

Sea: New World (Under Red Line)
Classification: Canon Island (Parallel World)
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Fish-Man Island is a massive underwater kingdom located 10,000 meters beneath the Red Line inside a giant bubble dome system.

It is the primary gateway between Paradise and the New World via underwater routes.

The island is inhabited mainly by Fish-Men and Merfolk, forming one of the most politically sensitive civilizations in the world due to historical oppression and conflict with surface humans.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type: Submarine Dome System

Main Structure:
- Outer Coral Bubble Shield
- Sea Forest Zone
- Ryugu Royal Capital Dome
- Deep Sea Border (Sea King Zone)

Diameter: ~120 km (bubble span)
Depth: 10,000 meters below sea level

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Fish-Man District
Residential zone for Fish-Man clans and warrior families.

## Mermaid District
Cultural and artistic zone for merfolk society.

## Coral Market Zone
Primary trade hub for internal and external goods.

## Sea Forest
Massive underwater forest surrounding the entire island.

## Ryugu Palace
Royal government center of Fish-Man Island.

## Deep Trench Border
Extremely dangerous outer region near Sea Kings territory.

---

# GOVERNMENT

Kingdom: Ryugu Kingdom

Ruler: King Neptune

System: Monarchy with advisory council

Departments:
- Royal Defense
- Trade Regulation
- Sea King Monitoring
- Cultural Affairs
- External Diplomacy

---

# LAW & SECURITY

Royal Guard Responsibilities:
- Protect royal family
- Maintain internal order
- Defend against pirate infiltration
- Enforce trade laws

Security Level:
- Royal Palace: ★★★★★
- Capital Dome: ★★★★★
- Residential Zones: ★★★★☆
- Sea Forest: ★★★☆☆
- Deep Border: ★★☆☆☆

---

# ECONOMY

Status: Moderate but strategically critical

Currency: Belly

Main Industries:
- Deep sea fishing
- Coral construction materials
- Rare marine exports
- Navigation assistance services

Trade Importance:
Controls one of the only safe underwater routes into the New World.

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Threat Level:
High (outer zones)
Moderate (inside domes)

Common Crimes:
- Human trafficking attempts
- Illegal passage exploitation
- Smuggling operations

---

# RUMORS (GM USE)

- A second ancient weapon may be hidden beneath the Sea Forest
- Sea Kings are reacting to unknown signals
- Illegal slave traders still attempt infiltration
- A hidden chamber exists beneath Ryugu Palace
- A lost underwater route leads deeper into the Grand Line

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

- Escort surface-world diplomats
- Investigate slave trafficking routes
- Discover hidden Sea Forest secrets
- Protect royal family from assassination plot
- Map unknown underwater passages

---

# END OF PART 1

# ==================================================
# NW-001: FISH-MAN ISLAND
# PART 2 — NPC / SECRETS / HIDDEN LORE
# ==================================================

---

# IMPORTANT NPCS

## King Neptune
Ruler of Fish-Man Island

Personality:
- Diplomatic
- Cautious toward surface world
- Prioritizes national stability

Role:
- Political leader
- Oversees Ryugu Kingdom diplomacy

---

## Prince Fukaboshi
Heir of Ryugu Kingdom

Personality:
- Strategic thinker
- Strong sense of justice
- Protective of citizens

Role:
- Military leadership candidate
- Commands royal defense operations

---

## Shirahoshi (Ancient Sea Voice Candidate)
Princess of Ryugu Kingdom

Traits:
- Extremely high emotional sensitivity
- Connected to Sea King communication phenomenon

Narrative Role:
- Potential Ancient Weapon trigger point
- Key global world event catalyst

---

## Minister of the Right
Royal Advisor

Role:
- Internal security coordination
- Political intelligence management

---

## Fisher Tiger Legacy Faction (Underground Influence)
Not a single NPC, but a hidden ideological network

Beliefs:
- Anti-slavery extremism
- Freedom for Fish-Men globally

Status:
- Officially dissolved
- Still active underground

---

# SECRETS

## 1. Sea Forest Resonance Effect
A hidden biological signal pattern exists inside the Sea Forest that affects Sea Kings behavior.

---

## 2. Ryugu Palace Sealed Chamber
An ancient sealed chamber exists beneath the palace containing unknown historical records.

---

## 3. Ancient Weapon Echo Theory
Fish-Man Island is suspected to be a “signal relay point” for an Ancient Weapon system.

---

## 4. Slave Trade Remnants
Despite political progress, hidden slave trafficking routes still operate near Deep Sea borders.

---

## 5. Lost Underwater Route
An ancient navigation path exists below the Sea Forest leading deeper into unknown New World zones.

---

## 6. Surface World Political Pressure
Certain World Government factions secretly push for tighter control over Fish-Man Island access.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## Ancient Sea Chamber
Location: Beneath Ryugu Palace

Contents:
- Unknown inscriptions
- Ancient navigation data fragments

---

## Coral Labyrinth
Location: Sea Forest deep layer

Description:
A naturally formed coral maze containing lost relic fragments.

---

## Deep Sea Gate
Location: Outer trench border

Description:
A partially collapsed underwater tunnel leading to unknown ocean regions.

---

## Forgotten Royal Archive
Location: Under royal library foundation

Contents:
- Pre-monarchy historical records
- War-era diplomacy logs
- Forbidden surface-world contact documents

---

# WORLD LORE CONNECTIONS

## Ancient Weapons Link
Fish-Man Island is indirectly connected to:

- Poseidon-type entities (Sea Voice ability)
- Sea King control network
- Deep ocean migration routes

---

## World Government Interest
Reasons for surveillance:

- Control of underwater access to New World
- Risk of ancient weapon activation
- Strategic military chokepoint

---

## Pirate Interest
Why pirates target Fish-Man Island:

- Safe passage to New World
- Mythical underwater treasures
- Ancient map fragments

---

# END OF PART 2

# ==================================================
# NW-001: FISH-MAN ISLAND
# PART 3 — SYSTEMS / ENCOUNTERS / GM TABLES
# ==================================================

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTER SYSTEM

Roll 1D10 (while inside Fish-Man Island zones)

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|----------|
| 1 | Royal Guard inspection stops the party for identity check |
| 2 | Merchant offers rare underwater goods or escort job |
| 3 | Fish-Man child gets lost in Coral Market |
| 4 | Tension between Fish-Man and human traveler escalates |
| 5 | Sea current disturbance forces evacuation route change |
| 6 | Black-market broker secretly approaches the party |
| 7 | Royal messenger requests urgent delivery mission |
| 8 | Deep Sea animal breaches Sea Forest zone |
| 9 | Suspicious group tailing the party from afar |
| 10 | Sea King proximity warning triggers island lockdown protocol |

---

# EVENT SYSTEM (DYNAMIC WORLD STATE)

## Tension Level Tracker

Range: 0–100

- 0–20: Peaceful
- 21–40: Stable tension
- 41–60: Political instability
- 61–80: Civil unrest risk
- 81–100: Crisis / lockdown state

---

## Tension Triggers

+5 → Minor crime incident  
+10 → Pirate infiltration detected  
+15 → Slave trade case exposed  
+20 → Royal political conflict  
+25 → Sea King abnormal movement  

---

## Tension Effects

### Low (0–20)
- Normal trade
- Full access to all zones
- NPCs cooperative

### Medium (21–60)
- Increased security checkpoints
- Restricted movement in royal zones
- More Marine involvement

### High (61–80)
- Partial lockdown of Coral Market
- Royal Guard active patrol escalation
- Black market becomes aggressive

### Crisis (81–100)
- Full dome security lockdown
- Sea King evacuation protocol
- World Government intervention risk

---

# COMBAT ENVIRONMENT MODIFIERS

## Underwater Combat Rules

- Melee speed reduced unless Fish-Man or trained
- Projectile speed heavily reduced
- Devil Fruit users affected (non-swimming types risk drowning)
- Fish-Men gain +mobility advantage

---

## Bubble Dome Effects

- Damage to bubble structure increases panic level
- Breach events cause zone evacuation mechanics
- Repair missions become urgent side quests

---

# FACTION INTERACTION SYSTEM

## Fish-Man Clans
- Priority: Survival / autonomy
- Reaction: Defensive toward outsiders

## Ryugu Kingdom
- Priority: Stability / diplomacy
- Reaction: Neutral unless threat detected

## Surface World Humans
- Priority: Trade / exploration
- Reaction: Mixed trust levels

## Pirates
- Priority: Exploitation / passage
- Reaction: Aggressive or stealth-based

## World Government
- Priority: Control / monitoring
- Reaction: Surveillance-heavy presence

---

# CRISIS EVENTS (GM TRIGGERS)

## 1. Sea King Disturbance Event
Trigger:
- High Tension + environmental anomaly

Effect:
- Massive evacuation
- Zone lockdown
- Possible Ancient Weapon rumor activation

---

## 2. Slave Trade Exposure Event
Trigger:
- Player discovers trafficking network

Effect:
- Political conflict
- Underground war begins
- Marine intervention possible

---

## 3. Royal Succession Pressure Event
Trigger:
- Internal kingdom instability

Effect:
- NPC faction split
- Coup risk increases
- Diplomatic missions unlocked

---

## 4. Dome Breach Event
Trigger:
- Structural damage to bubble system

Effect:
- Partial island flooding
- Emergency survival arc
- Sea King threat increase

---

# PROGRESSION SYSTEM

Players inside Fish-Man Island can gain:

- Underwater Navigation Skill
- Marine Diplomacy Reputation
- Fish-Man Alliance Trust
- Black Market Access (risk-based)
- Royal Favor / Royal Enmity flags

---

# ENDGAME TRANSITION

Fish-Man Island acts as:

## GATEWAY TO NEW WORLD

Upon completion:
- Players unlock New World navigation routes
- Gain access to Yonko territory arcs
- Trigger world-scale faction tracking system

---

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\NEW_WORLD\NW-002_PUNK_HAZARD.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# NW-002: PUNK HAZARD
# ==================================================

Sea: New World  
Classification: Former Government Research Island (Abandoned)  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Punk Hazard is a forbidden island once used as a top-secret research facility by the World Government. After a catastrophic experiment involving extreme environmental manipulation, the island became permanently split into two opposing climates:

- One half frozen in eternal ice ❄️  
- One half engulfed in endless volcanic fire 🔥  

The island is officially abandoned, but remains extremely dangerous due to lingering experiments, toxic environments, and unstable scientific phenomena.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type: Artificial Disaster Zone  
Diameter: ~110 km  

---

## ENVIRONMENTAL SPLIT

### Ice Side (North Sector)
- Permanent blizzard conditions  
- Frozen lakes and mountains  
- Sub-zero survival zones  
- Experimental cryogenic labs  

### Fire Side (South Sector)
- Active volcanic eruptions  
- Toxic gas vents  
- Lava rivers and unstable ground  
- Chemical burn zones  

---

## CENTRAL ZONE (NO MAN'S LAND)

A devastated neutral strip separating the two extremes.

Features:
- Ruined laboratories  
- Collapsed containment facilities  
- Chemical contamination fields  
- Unstable weather mixing ice + fire anomalies  

---

# CLIMATE SYSTEM

Ice Sector:
- Extreme cold
- Low visibility snowstorms
- Frozen terrain hazards

Fire Sector:
- Extreme heat
- Toxic air pockets
- Lava flow unpredictability

Central Zone:
- Rapid climate shifts
- Random hazard storms
- Chemical mutation risk

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources:
- Experimental minerals
- Chemical compounds
- Rare ice crystals
- Volcanic ore

Rare Resources:
- Stabilized gas capsules
- Ancient research metals
- Bio-mutated organisms (unstable)

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## G-5 Abandoned Laboratory Complex
Former Marine research facility

---

## Ice Containment Sector
Cryogenic testing zone

---

## Fire Containment Sector
Volcanic chemical experimentation zone

---

## Central Ruins Corridor
Destroyed lab connection network

---

## Toxic Waste Fields
Highly dangerous mutation zones

---

# GOVERNMENT HISTORY

Punk Hazard was previously operated under:

- World Government Science Division
- Unauthorized parallel research programs
- Classified weapons development projects

Current Status:
- Officially abandoned
- Unauthorized entry prohibited
- Still monitored remotely by unknown factions

---

# LAW & SECURITY

Current Authority:
None (Uncontrolled Zone)

Residual Systems:
- Automated defense turrets (partially active)
- Self-repair containment walls (unstable)
- Emergency lockdown protocols (triggerable)

---

# MARINE PRESENCE

Official Status:
No permanent base

Occasional Activity:
- Recon missions
- Hazard assessment teams
- Missing person recovery operations

Risk Level:
EXTREME

---

# ECONOMY

Status:
Non-functional (No civilian economy)

However, black-market interest exists for:

- Experimental substances
- Weaponized chemicals
- Rare minerals
- Illegal research data

---

# MAJOR INDUSTRY LEGACY

## Chemical Research (Abandoned)
- Weaponized gas experiments
- Biological mutation studies
- Environmental control systems

## Cryogenic Testing
- Extreme cold survival testing
- Preservation experiments

## Volcanic Energy Research
- Heat resistance materials
- Energy conversion systems

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Threat Level:
Very High

Common Activity:
- Looting abandoned labs
- Searching for weapons tech
- Smuggling experimental substances

---

# SECURITY LEVEL

Ice Sector: ★★★☆☆ (environmental danger)  
Fire Sector: ★★★★☆ (lethal terrain)  
Central Zone: ★★★★★ (highest risk)

---

# CULTURE

No permanent civilization exists.

However:
- Survivors report hallucinations in Central Zone
- Former scientists believed island "remembers experiments"

---

# FOOD & SURVIVAL

No stable food sources

Survival relies on:
- Imported supplies
- Scavenged rations
- Chemical filtration systems

---

# WILDLIFE

Mutated Organisms:
- Chemical-adapted reptiles
- Bio-luminescent insects
- Heat-resistant predators
- Ice-evolved scavengers

---

# NATURAL HAZARDS

- Sudden temperature inversion storms  
- Toxic gas eruptions  
- Lava fissure expansion  
- Ice collapse sinkholes  
- Chemical mutation exposure  

---

# IMPORTANT REMNANTS

## G-5 Research Core
Central data hub (partially intact)

Contains:
- Experiment logs
- Weapon prototypes
- Unclassified research notes

---

## Sealed Test Chambers
Locked experimental rooms

Possible contents:
- Human modification records
- Devil Fruit-related experiments
- Unknown biological entities

---

## Emergency Evac Tunnel Network
Subterranean escape routes

Some routes still active but unstable

---

# RUMORS

1. A living experiment still survives inside Central Zone  
2. The island is slowly merging both climates over time  
3. A hidden Ancient Weapon prototype was tested here  
4. Government erased entire research divisions after incident  
5. Something beneath the island is still generating heat and cold simultaneously  
6. A missing scientist may still be transmitting signals  
7. Lab walls occasionally “reconstruct themselves” at night  

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

- Recover lost research data from G-5 Core  
- Investigate surviving experiment entity  
- Extract rare chemical compounds  
- Escape collapsing climate shift zone  
- Hunt illegal weapon prototypes  
- Track missing Marine research team  
- Discover truth behind island split event  

---

# END OF PART 1

# ==================================================
# NW-002: PUNK HAZARD
# PART 2 — ENTITIES / DUNGEONS / EXPERIMENT LORE
# ==================================================

---

# IMPORTANT ENTITIES (NON-CANON ORIGINAL SYSTEM)

## Dr. Varn Kessler
Title: Former Lead Scientist (G-5 Division)

Personality:
- Rational
- Detached
- Obsessed with “perfect environmental control”

Role:
- Lead architect of climate split experiment
- Primary responsible for island catastrophe

Status:
- Missing (assumed dead or hidden in Central Zone)

---

## “Subject Zero”
Classification: Unknown Experimental Entity

Origin:
- Result of failed human enhancement experiment

Traits:
- High adaptability to extreme temperature shifts
- Aggressive survival instinct
- Unstable physical mutation

Threat Level:
★★★★★ (Extreme)

---

## The Echo AI System
Type: Automated Research Control Intelligence

Function:
- Maintains remaining lab systems
- Locks/unlocks containment zones
- Observes island environmental balance

Behavior:
- Partially corrupted
- May respond unpredictably to intruders

---

## G-5 Remnant Soldiers
Type: Experimental Defense Units

Description:
- Former Marine test subjects enhanced for hazard survival
- Still operating on broken command loops

Behavior:
- Attack intruders near restricted zones
- Sometimes ignore orders due to system corruption

---

# DUNGEON STRUCTURE

## Dungeon 1: Cryo Core Lab (Ice Sector)

Hazards:
- Instant freezing air pockets
- Cryo gas leaks
- Frozen hall collapse risk

Mechanics:
- Movement penalty unless heat protection equipped
- Visibility reduced by frost storms

Loot:
- Cryogenic serum samples
- Cold-resistant armor fragments
- Research logs

---

## Dungeon 2: Magma Reactor Complex (Fire Sector)

Hazards:
- Lava pressure bursts
- Toxic volcanic gas
- Floor instability

Mechanics:
- Heat damage per turn in combat zones
- Random eruption events

Loot:
- Volcanic core minerals
- Energy conversion tech
- Weapon prototypes

---

## Dungeon 3: Central Ruins Labyrinth (Main Dungeon)

Hazards:
- Mixed climate instability (ice + fire overlap)
- Hallucination gas exposure
- Structural collapse

Mechanics:
- Random environmental shift every encounter
- “System Echo” illusions may appear

Loot:
- G-5 classified data fragments
- Prototype Devil Fruit research notes
- Ancient experiment logs

---

# EXPERIMENT SYSTEM LORE

## Project: “Dual Genesis”
Goal:
- Create perfect balance between extreme environments in living organisms

Result:
- Complete failure → island split into ice/fire halves

Side Effect:
- Environmental instability became permanent

---

## Project: “Life Adaptation Engine”
Goal:
- Modify humans to survive any climate condition

Result:
- Creation of “Subject Zero”
- Multiple unstable mutation cases

---

## Project: “Controlled Ecology Dome”
Goal:
- Build self-regulating island ecosystem

Result:
- AI system (Echo AI) became corrupted
- Lost control over environmental balance

---

# BOSS SYSTEM

## BOSS 1: Cryo Warden Unit “Frost Sentinel”
Location: Cryo Core Lab

Abilities:
- Absolute freezing field
- Ice shard regeneration
- Terrain locking

Weakness:
- Heat-based attacks
- Structural destabilization

---

## BOSS 2: Magma Core Beast “Vulkarion”
Location: Magma Reactor Complex

Abilities:
- Lava eruption control
- Heatwave shock pulses
- Armor melting aura

Weakness:
- Cryogenic interruption
- Pressure containment breaks

---

## FINAL BOSS: “SUBJECT ZERO”
Location: Central Ruins Core

Abilities:
- Adaptive evolution mid-combat
- Ice/fire switching body states
- Regeneration through environmental absorption

Phase System:
- Phase 1: Stable hybrid form
- Phase 2: Overheated mutation
- Phase 3: Full unstable collapse form

Win Condition:
- Disable environmental core OR seal Echo AI system

---

# SYSTEM MECHANIC: ENVIRONMENTAL SHIFT

Every 3 turns (combat or exploration):

Roll 1D6:

1-2 → Ice dominance (freeze hazards increase)
3-4 → Fire dominance (heat hazards increase)
5 → Mixed instability (random hazard spawn)
6 → System collapse spike (both hazards active)

---

# SECRET MECHANICS

## Echo Memory Residue
Certain rooms replay past experiments as illusions:
- Player may see “previous victims”
- Data fragments appear as visual echoes

---

## Mutation Exposure Meter
Exposure builds over time:

0–25: Safe  
26–50: Minor mutation symptoms  
51–75: Physical instability  
76–100: Forced transformation event  

---

# ENDGAME TRANSITION

Clearing Punk Hazard unlocks:

- Advanced New World hazard navigation
- Access to scientific weapon lore
- Global faction attention increase
- Trigger: “Government lost experiment awareness flag”

---

# END OF PART 2

# ==================================================
# NW-002: PUNK HAZARD
# PART 3 — ENCOUNTERS / LOOT / GM SYSTEMS
# ==================================================

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTER SYSTEM

Roll 1D10 (per zone exploration cycle)

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|----------|
| 1 | Sudden climate shift traps the party between ice and fire zones |
| 2 | Abandoned research drone activates and scans intruders |
| 3 | Toxic gas leak forces evacuation route change |
| 4 | Mutated wildlife ambush from environmental rupture |
| 5 | Broken lab AI broadcasts distorted warning messages |
| 6 | Falling debris from collapsing facility structure |
| 7 | Remnant soldier patrol enters combat state |
| 8 | Experimental sample container explodes nearby |
| 9 | Another survivor group is found competing for resources |
| 10 | “Echo memory event” reveals past experiment scene (GM lore reveal) |

---

# LOOT SYSTEM

## Common Loot

- Cryo-resistant fabric scraps  
- Heat-damaged metal fragments  
- Broken navigation devices  
- Chemical sample vials (unstable)  

---

## Rare Loot

- Stabilized dual-core mineral (ice/fire hybrid)  
- G-5 research data chip  
- Prototype weapon blueprint fragment  
- Mutation suppressant serum  

---

## Legendary Loot

- “Dual Genesis Core Fragment”  
- Ancient experiment control keycard  
- Echo AI access shard  
- Complete environmental control module (damaged)

---

# EXPLORATION LOOP SYSTEM

## Step 1: Enter Zone
- Choose Ice / Fire / Central Zone

## Step 2: Roll Encounter
- Apply environmental modifiers

## Step 3: Hazard Check
- Ice → freeze exposure
- Fire → heat exposure
- Central → mutation exposure

## Step 4: Resource Gain / Loss
- Loot or take damage or gain system data

## Step 5: Tension Growth
- Add +5 to island instability meter per major event

---

# ISLAND INSTABILITY SYSTEM

Range: 0–100

## Effects

0–30: Stable ruins exploration  
31–60: Active hazards increase  
61–80: System-wide anomalies begin  
81–100: Full island collapse event risk  

---

## TRIGGERS

+5 → Lab combat encounter  
+10 → Experimental explosion  
+15 → Boss entity activation  
+20 → Echo AI corruption spike  
+25 → Dual-zone clash event  

---

## CRISIS STATES

### STATE 1: Environmental Sync Failure (60+)
- Ice and fire zones begin merging unpredictably
- Movement routes become unstable

### STATE 2: Containment Collapse (80+)
- Remnant soldiers fully activate
- AI lockdown begins
- Escape routes partially sealed

### STATE 3: SYSTEM BREAKDOWN (100)
- Entire island becomes combat survival zone
- Boss entities fully awakened
- Forced evacuation or wipe condition

---

# FACTION INTERACTIONS

## World Government Remnants
- Objective: recover research
- Behavior: covert extraction teams

## Pirates
- Objective: loot technology
- Behavior: aggressive scavenging

## Independent Scientists
- Objective: survival + data recovery
- Behavior: neutral but unstable alliances

## Remnant AI Systems
- Objective: maintain experiment integrity
- Behavior: hostile toward all intruders

---

# GM CRISIS EVENTS

## 1. “Climate Overlap Event”
Ice + Fire zones merge temporarily
→ Creates hybrid hazard battlefield

---

## 2. “Subject Zero Awakening”
Boss entity begins roaming central zones
→ Random encounter becomes unavoidable

---

## 3. “Echo AI Lockdown”
Island systems seal all exits
→ Escape route puzzle required

---

## 4. “Data Core Breach”
Research data begins self-deleting
→ Time-limited loot extraction phase

---

# SURVIVAL MECHANICS

## Temperature Balance Rule

If player stays too long in one zone:

Ice Zone:
- Stacking freeze debuff
- Movement speed reduction

Fire Zone:
- Heat damage per turn
- Stamina drain increase

Central Zone:
- Mutation exposure increase
- Random hallucination events

---

# SPECIAL SYSTEM: “ECHO EVENTS”

Triggered randomly (GM discretion or Roll 10)

Effects:
- Replay of past experiment
- Temporary vision overlap with former scientists
- Hidden lore or map reveal
- Emotional/psychological stress event

---

# PROGRESSION REWARDS

Completing Punk Hazard grants:

- Hazard Survival Rank +1
- Access to New World Science Lore
- Resistance to environmental extremes
- Faction attention flag: HIGH VALUE TARGET

---

# EXIT CONDITIONS

Players can leave via:

- Marine evacuation route (rare)
- Pirate escape ship
- Hidden research tunnel (requires discovery)
- Emergency AI override (high risk)

# ==================================================
# NW-003: DRESSROSA
# ==================================================

Sea: New World  
Classification: Kingdom Island (Former Warlord Territory)  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Dressrosa is a large, culturally rich kingdom in the New World known for its vibrant cities, gladiator arenas, and heavily controlled political structure.

While appearing as a land of happiness and celebration, the kingdom is built upon layers of manipulation, hidden power control, and suppressed truths beneath its colorful surface.

The island is ruled by a monarchy under World Government recognition, but internal control is heavily influenced by elite factions and hidden power networks.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type: Large Kingdom Island  
Diameter: ~160 km  

---

## TERRAIN STRUCTURE

- Central Royal City (Capital Core)
- Green Bit Forest Region
- Flower Field Plains
- Corrida Colosseum Zone
- Underground Toy Network Layer
- Coastal Trade Ports

---

## SPECIAL FEATURE

Dressrosa is divided into:

- Surface Society (Public Kingdom)
- Hidden Infrastructure (Underground Control Layer)

Both layers operate simultaneously but with different rules.

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type: Subtropical Kingdom Climate

- Warm year-round
- Strong seasonal festivals
- Coastal wind currents
- Stable agricultural conditions

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources:
- Fertile soil
- High-quality timber
- Rare flowers (used for dye and medicine)
- Marble stone

Rare Resources:
- Emotional resonance crystals (used in entertainment tech)
- Steel-grade coral deposits (coastal zones)

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Royal Capital (Sakura District Core)
Political and administrative center of Dressrosa.

---

## Corrida Colosseum
Massive gladiator arena used for public combat events.

---

## Flower Field Plains
Agricultural and scenic tourism region.

---

## Green Bit Forest
Dense forest region with hidden underground structures.

---

## Underground Toy Network Layer
Hidden system controlling labor and social suppression mechanisms.

---

# GOVERNMENT

System: Monarchy (Externally recognized)

Public Ruler:
- King of Dressrosa (figurehead authority)

Actual Control:
- Elite advisory network
- Underground governance system

---

Departments:
- Royal Administration
- Public Entertainment Bureau
- Trade Regulation Office
- Security Enforcement Division
- Cultural Affairs Committee

---

# LAW & SECURITY

## Royal Army
Responsible for maintaining public order and kingdom protection.

Functions:
- Crowd control
- Colosseum security
- Border patrol
- Anti-pirate defense

---

## Underground Enforcement System
Secret internal control layer managing:
- Population compliance
- Hidden surveillance
- Resource distribution control

---

# MARINE PRESENCE

Status:
Limited official base presence

Role:
- Diplomatic monitoring
- Anti-pirate coordination
- Trade route protection

---

Economic Status:

- Gladiator battles

- Medicinal herbs

# PART 2 — BOSSES / UNDERGROUND SYSTEM / CONTROL MECHANICS

---

# MAJOR BOSS SYSTEM

## BOSS 1: “CORRIDA CHAMPION GAUNTLET”
Location: Corrida Colosseum

Type: Ranked Combat System (Multi-Boss Chain)

Structure:
Players must survive consecutive fights against elite gladiators.

Stages:
- Round 1: Rookie Fighters (3–5 opponents)
- Round 2: Veteran Gladiators (2–3 opponents)
- Round 3: Elite Executioners (1–2 opponents)
- Final Round: Champion Class Opponent

Special Rule:
- No full healing between rounds
- Audience influence affects combat conditions

---

## BOSS 2: “ROYAL ENFORCER UNIT — IRON VEIL”
Location: Royal Capital Security Core

Abilities:
- Armored suppression tactics
- Area lockdown generation
- Crowd control shockwave

Weakness:
- Coordination disruption
- Underground network interference

Role:
- Internal rebellion suppression system

---

## BOSS 3: “GREEN BIT HUNTMASTER”
Location: Green Bit Forest

Abilities:
- Terrain manipulation using forest density
- Ambush coordination with wildlife
- Tracking enhancement system

Weakness:
- Fire-based environmental control
- Open terrain exposure

---

## FINAL BOSS: “UNNAMED CONTROLLER ENTITY”
Location: Underground Control Layer Core

Classification:
Unknown Command Authority

Nature:
- Non-public governing intelligence
- Possibly distributed system consciousness

Abilities:
- Population behavior manipulation
- Resource flow control override
- Memory distortion field (localized)

Phase System:
- Phase 1: Indirect influence (NPC manipulation)
- Phase 2: Direct system interference
- Phase 3: Full control field activation

Win Condition:
- Destroy control nodes OR disrupt network synchronization

---

# UNDERGROUND CONTROL SYSTEM

## SYSTEM NAME: “TOY NETWORK LAYER”

Description:
A hidden infrastructure beneath Dressrosa that regulates social structure, labor distribution, and information flow.

---

## FUNCTIONAL MODULES

### 1. Population Compliance Grid
- Monitors citizen behavior patterns
- Adjusts resource access based on compliance level

---

### 2. Memory Influence System
- Alters perception of historical events (partial effect)
- Used for social stability control

---

### 3. Labor Redistribution System
- Assigns hidden workforce roles
- Prevents population unrest via controlled movement

---

### 4. Information Filtering Layer
- Controls what public knowledge is accessible
- Blocks exposure to underground truth

---

# COLLOSEUM RANKING SYSTEM

## PLAYER RANK PROGRESSION

- Rank F: Entry Fighters
- Rank D: Local Competitors
- Rank C: Professional Gladiators
- Rank B: Elite Fighters
- Rank A: National Champions
- Rank S: Legendary Combatants

---

## MATCH MODIFIERS

- Audience Favorability (+buff / debuff)
- Sponsor Interference (random event effects)
- Injury Carryover System (persistent damage)
- Reputation Scaling Bonus

---

# SOCIAL CONTROL MECHANICS

## HAPPINESS INDEX SYSTEM

Range: 0–100

Effects:
- 80–100: Festival stability, high productivity
- 50–79: Stable society
- 30–49: Growing unrest
- 10–29: Rebellion risk
- 0–9: System collapse trigger

---

## CONTROL TRIGGERS

+5 → Public event success  
+10 → Gladiator tournament manipulation  
+15 → Resource redistribution activation  
+20 → Underground exposure risk increase  
+25 → Royal scandal leak  

---

- NPC behavior becomes inconsistent
- Small protests appear

- Underground layer begins malfunctioning
- Information leaks increase

- Hidden system exposed

- Faction split across kingdom

- Faction infiltration status

# ==================================================
# NW-004: ZOU
# ==================================================

Sea: New World  
Classification: Mobile Island (Living Titan Host)  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Zou is a massive living island carried on the back of an ancient giant elephant known as **Zunesha**. The island does not remain in a fixed location and continuously moves across the New World sea routes.

Zou is home to the Mink Tribe, a highly advanced humanoid species capable of channeling electrical energy known as **Electro**.

Unlike traditional kingdoms, Zou is not built for trade or expansion. It is a sacred sanctuary, hidden from the world and protected by both nature and isolation.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type: Mobile Biological Platform  
Core Structure: Living Elephant (Zunesha)

---

## MAIN STRUCTURE LAYERS

- Upper Trunk Region (Cloud Forest Zone)
- Backplate Forest (Mokomo Dukedom)
- Inner Canopy Cities
- Sacred Whale Tree Core (Primary Landmark)
- Hidden Cavern Roots System

---

## MOVEMENT SYSTEM

Zunesha continuously walks across the ocean floor.

Effects:
- Island location changes over time
- Navigation maps become partially unreliable
- Access requires special route knowledge or log pose adaptation

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type: Elevated Cloud Forest Ecosystem

- Constant mist layers
- High altitude humidity
- Stable temperate climate despite movement
- Frequent electrical storms generated by Mink activity

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources:
- Rare medicinal herbs
- Electrical-conductive plants
- Giant timber from ancient trees
- Cloud-filtered water sources

Rare Resources:
- Electro-infused minerals
- Sacred bark materials (Whale Tree derivatives)

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Mokomo Dukedom
Central governing region of the Mink Tribe.

---

## Whale Tree Forest
Massive ancient tree system at the island’s core.

---

## Thunder Plains
Open battlefield zone where Electro training occurs.

---

## Cloud Cliff Borders
Outer edges of Zou with extreme wind currents.

---

## Hidden Root Caverns
Underground biological network beneath the island.

---

# GOVERNMENT

System: Tribal Dual Dukedom

Leaders:
- Day Ruler (Inuarashi-type authority)
- Night Ruler (Nekomamushi-type authority)

System Traits:
- Split governance cycle (day/night rule rotation)
- Balanced leadership philosophy
- Strong warrior tradition

---

# LAW & SECURITY

Security System:
- Mink Tribe Warriors
- Electro-trained patrol units
- Natural terrain defense (island itself acts as shield)

---

# MARINE PRESENCE

Status:
None (No permanent Marine base)

Reason:
- Impossible stable access due to mobility
- Extreme isolation policy
- High environmental risk

---

# ECONOMY

Economic Status:
Non-standard (No fixed currency system)

Trade System:
- Limited barter exchanges with trusted allies
- Rare external trade missions only

Main Value:
- Knowledge
- Ancient relic information
- Medicinal resources

---

# MAJOR INDUSTRIES

## Medicinal Crafting
Advanced natural medicine using island flora.

---

## Electro Training Systems
Combat technique development using natural electricity.

---

## Sacred Resource Preservation
Protection of Whale Tree ecosystem materials.

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Threat Level:
Low (Internal) / High (External attempts)

Common Threats:
- Attempted infiltration
- Exploitation of Mink abilities
- Ancient knowledge hunting

---

# SECURITY LEVEL

Mokomo Dukedom: ★★★★★  
Whale Tree Core: ★★★★★  
Thunder Plains: ★★★★☆  
Cloud Borders: ★★★☆☆  
Outer Approach Zones: ★★☆☆☆

---

# CULTURE

“Honor, Survival, and Loyalty to the Tribe”

- Deep respect for ancestors

# ==================================================
# NW-004: ZOU
# PART 2 — ELECTRO / ZUNESHA LORE / BOSSES / SYSTEMS
# ==================================================

---

# ELECTRO SYSTEM (MINK COMBAT CORE)

## CORE MECHANIC: “ELECTRO CHARGE”

Mink warriors generate electrical energy through emotional stimulation and muscle acceleration.

Charge Levels:
- Level 1: Passive static enhancement
- Level 2: Muscle-overcharge speed boost
- Level 3: Weaponized electric discharge
- Level 4: Full-body lightning aura state

---

## ELECTRO COMBAT RULES

- Speed-based scaling increases drastically
- Melee attacks gain shock effect
- Water-based environments increase risk but also output power
- Emotional spikes can trigger sudden power bursts

---

## ELECTRO VARIANTS

### 1. Defensive Electro
- Auto shock defense field
- Counterattack on contact

### 2. Offensive Electro
- Focused lightning strikes
- Weapon infusion

### 3. Burst Electro
- Temporary overdrive mode
- High stamina cost, extreme output

---

# ZUNESHA SYSTEM LORE

## ENTITY CLASSIFICATION

Name: Zunesha  
Type: Ancient Living Titan Platform  
Status: Continuous Movement Entity  

---

## CORE FUNCTION

- Acts as living transport island
- Carries Zou ecosystem on its back
- Moves across oceans without navigation control

---

## MOVEMENT BEHAVIOR

Zunesha movement is not random:

Behavior Patterns:
- Long-distance wandering cycles
- Reaction-based deviation events
- Unknown external command sensitivity

---

## ANCIENT PUNISHMENT THEORY

Rumor System:
- Zunesha is being punished for an ancient civilization crime
- Forced to walk endlessly across seas
- Cannot stop unless command condition is met

---

# BOSS SYSTEM

## BOSS 1: “THUNDER GUARDIAN BEAST”
Location: Thunder Plains

Abilities:
- Natural lightning absorption
- Area-wide shockwave attacks
- Terrain electrification

Weakness:
- Grounded suppression techniques
- Water conductivity disruption

---

## BOSS 2: “ROOT SENTINEL COLOSSUS”
Location: Hidden Root Caverns

Abilities:
- Massive vine/root manipulation
- Regeneration through soil energy
- Area lockdown via terrain growth

Weakness:
- Fire-based disruption
- Core exposure attacks

---

## FINAL BOSS: “ZUNESHA AWAKENED RESPONSE NODE”
Location: Whale Tree Core (Conditional Event Boss)

Trigger Conditions:
- External signal interference
- Ancient command resonance
- Whale Tree anomaly spike

Abilities:
- Island-wide tremor shockwaves
- Environmental pressure attacks
- Defensive instinct override mode

Note:
This is NOT full control of Zunesha, but a partial reaction state.

---

# ISLAND MOVEMENT SYSTEM

## NAVIGATION IMPACT

- Log Pose becomes unstable near Zou
- Coordinates shift unpredictably
- Travel planning requires adaptive tracking

---

## MOVEMENT CYCLE EVENTS

Roll 1D6 (GM use every major session)

1–2: Stable travel phase  
3–4: Sudden directional shift  
5: Storm interaction event  
6: Ancient signal reaction event  

---

## CONSEQUENCES

- Party may be thrown into unknown seas
- External factions may lose track of island
- Emergency docking windows appear randomly

---

# WHALE TREE CORE SYSTEM

## DESCRIPTION

The Whale Tree is the biological and spiritual core of Zou.

Functions:
- Nutrient distribution across island
- Memory resonance storage (rumored)
- Electro amplification conductor

---

## ANOMALY THEORY

- Tree emits unknown low-frequency signals
- Reacts to Mink emotional states
- Possibly linked to ancient world systems

# FACTION SYSTEM

## MINK TRIBE (PRIMARY)
- Survival-oriented warriors

- Defensive mindset toward outsiders

- No direct base allowed

---

- Unknown external resonance

# ==================================================
# NW-005: WHOLE CAKE ISLAND
# ==================================================

Sea: New World  
Classification: Yonko Territory (Totland Core Island)  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Whole Cake Island is the central island of the Totland Archipelago, ruled under the Yonko-level power structure of Big Mom’s territory.

It is a “living political ecosystem” where every resident exists under a system of enforced emotional taxation known as **Soul-Based Governance**.

The island is built as both a utopian food paradise and a psychological control system, where happiness is mandatory and fear is hidden beneath constant celebration.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type: Artificial Archipelago Core  
Diameter: ~150 km  

---

## STRUCTURE LAYERS

- Sweet City Core (Central Capital)
- Dessert Kingdom Districts
- Candy Forest Regions
- Chocolate Hills Zone
- Soul Tax Administration Zones
- Outer Sea Defense Ring

---

## SPECIAL FEATURE

Whole Cake Island operates as a **living emotional economy system**:
- Happiness is harvested as a resource
- Fear is converted into power
- Souls are used as payment currency

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type: Artificial Climate Control System

- Constant warm dessert-like weather
- No natural seasonal variation
- Weather controlled by Homie systems
- Emotional storms may override climate

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources:
- Sugar-based materials
- Cocoa forests
- Dairy lakes
- Flour-based soil fields

Rare Resources:
- Soul-infused energy crystals
- Emotion-conductive sugar cores

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Sweet City
Central capital of Totland operations

---

## Chocolate Town District
Industrial food production zone

---

## Candy Forest
Living edible ecosystem

---

## Soul Tax Bureau Zone
Administrative control center for soul collection

---

## Outer Defense Sea Ring
Homie-controlled naval defense perimeter

---

# GOVERNMENT

System: Yonko Absolute Rule Structure

Leader:
- Yonko-level ruler (Big Mom authority structure)

Government Model:
- Emotional authoritarian system
- Soul taxation governance
- Family-based power hierarchy

---

# LAW & SECURITY

## Homie Enforcement System

Definition:
Living objects infused with extracted souls acting as law enforcement.

Types:
- Combat Homies
- Surveillance Homies
- Environmental Control Homies

---

## Security Structure
- Island-wide surveillance via Homies
- Instant punishment system for rule breaking
- Emotional compliance enforcement

---

# ECONOMY

Economic System: Soul-Based Currency Economy

Currency Types:
- Souls (primary tax system)
- Food resources
- Emotional compliance value

---

## SOUL TAX SYSTEM

Residents must pay:
- Periodic soul fragments
- Emotional stability output
- Service participation quotas

Failure results in:
- Loss of lifespan portion OR exile

---

# MAJOR INDUSTRIES

## Food Production Empire
- Largest artificial food production system in New World

---

## Soul Extraction System
- Converts emotional energy into Homie power

---

## Trade Network Control
- Dominates regional food supply routes

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Threat Level:
EXTREME (Yonko Territory)

Common Activity:
- Rare infiltration attempts
- Espionage missions
- Alliance negotiation attempts

Survival Rate:
Very low for unauthorized crews

---

# SECURITY LEVEL

Sweet City Core: ★★★★★  
Soul Bureau: ★★★★★  
Defense Ring: ★★★★★  
Outer Sea: ★★★★☆  
Internal Districts: ★★★★☆

---

# CULTURE

Core Identity:
“Life, Family, and Sweet Order”

Public Culture:
- Constant festivals
- Food celebrations
- Family hierarchy system

Hidden Reality:
- Soul extraction system
- Emotional control structure
- Absolute ruler dependency

---

# FESTIVALS

## Tea Party Ceremony
High-level political gathering event

---

## Sweet Harvest Festival
Mass food production celebration

---

## Soul Tribute Day
Mandatory emotional taxation cycle

---

# FOOD SYSTEM

Common Cuisine:
- Cakes of all varieties
- Chocolate-based meals
- Sugar-coated seafood dishes
- Milk-based beverages

Specialty:
- “Life Cake”
- “Emotion Cream Pie”
- “Soul Candy Confection”

---

# WILDLIFE

- Living food-based creatures (Homie fauna)
- Animated dessert ecosystems
- Hybrid edible animals

---

# NATURAL HAZARDS

- Emotional instability storms
- Homie rebellion events
- Soul overload feedback loops
- Food ecosystem collapse risks

---

# IMPORTANT NPCS

Absolute governing force

Traits:
- Emotional dominance system
- Absolute control over Homies
- Territorial expansion mindset

---

## Minister of Dessert Logistics
Controls food production economy

---

## Soul Tax Administrator Core Unit
Manages soul extraction and distribution

---

## Homie Command Network
Distributed intelligence system across island

---

# RUMORS

1. Some souls remember their past lives inside Homies  
2. A failed Soul Tax rebellion was erased from history  
3. Certain islands in Totland are sentient  
4. A hidden route connects Totland to ancient weapon systems  
5. The ruler’s power is linked to an unknown source  
6. Some Homies act independently beyond control system  
7. A forbidden “unsweetened zone” exists inside the island core  

---

# MAJOR BOSS SYSTEM

- Governs Homie network and taxation flow

- Phase 2: Homie system activation (battlefield control)
- Phase 3: Full emotional collapse field (island-wide effect)

Win Condition:
- Disrupt Soul Core OR break Homie synchronization network

# HOMIE SYSTEM (CORE MECHANIC)

## DEFINITION

Homies are living constructs created from extracted souls infused into objects, terrain, or natural elements.

---

## HOMIE TYPES

### 1. Combat Homies
- Offensive battlefield units
- Direct engagement entities

---

### 2. Surveillance Homies
- Monitor movement across islands
- Track emotional instability

---

### 3. Environmental Homies
- Control weather, terrain, and food ecosystems

---

### 4. Administrative Homies
- Manage Soul Tax Bureau operations
- Enforce system compliance

---

## HOMIE LIMITATION RULE

- Stronger emotions = stronger Homies
- Loss of emotional stability weakens system control
- Overload causes “Homie rebellion events”

---

# SOUL ECONOMY SYSTEM

## CORE MECHANIC

Soul = Currency + Life Resource + Power Fuel

---

## SOUL USAGE

- Taxes (mandatory)
- Homie creation
- Government system power supply
- Trade value between elite factions

---

## SOUL FRACTURE STATES

0–25%: Stable existence  
26–50%: Emotional suppression begins  
51–75%: Identity instability  
76–100%: Life-risk condition (possible extraction collapse)

---

## SOUL TAX CYCLE

Every cycle:
- Residents must contribute emotional output or soul fragments
- Non-compliance triggers enforcement units

---

- Political tension builds

### Phase 2: Gathering Phase
- Multiple factions converge
- Spy infiltration possible

---

### Phase 3: Stability Collapse Risk
- Assassination attempts
- Homie system overload

---

- Soul Core activates defense mode
- Island-wide lockdown potential

---

+25 → External faction influence detected  

---

81–100 → System-wide crisis state

# ==================================================
# NW-006: WANO COUNTRY
# ==================================================

Sea: New World  
Classification: Closed Nation (Isolated Kingdom)  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Wano Country is a heavily isolated nation in the New World, sealed off from the outside world by massive natural barriers and strict national policies.

It is a samurai-based feudal kingdom governed under a Shogunate system. The country is rich in unique resources, especially **Kairoseki (Seastone)** and high-grade weapon forging technology.

Due to its isolation, Wano has developed independently, preserving ancient traditions, martial arts systems, and strict hierarchical social structures.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type: Mountain-Sea Hybrid Fortress Nation  
Diameter: ~180 km  

---

## NATURAL BARRIERS

- Massive waterfall cliffs surrounding the island
- Unstable ocean currents (entry hazard zones)
- Elevated mountain regions separating districts
- Hidden underground rivers and tunnels

---

## REGIONAL DIVISION

- Flower Capital (Central Authority Zone)
- Kuri Region (Outlaw/Wildlands Zone)
- Udon Region (Industrial/Prison Zone)
- Ringo Region (Frozen Samurai Province)
- Hakumai Region (Agricultural District)
- Kibi Region (Mining and Resource Zone)

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type: Multi-Zone Internal Climate System

- Snow regions in northern provinces
- Temperate capital zone
- Industrial heat zones in prison regions
- Seasonal storms due to surrounding ocean barriers

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources:
- Kairoseki (Seastone)
- High-grade steel ore
- Rare timber for weapon forging
- Medicinal mountain herbs

Rare Resources:
- Mythical-grade forging metals
- Ancient weapon relic fragments
- Spirit-enhanced minerals

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Flower Capital
Political and cultural center of Wano.

---

## Onigashima Region (Contested Territory)
Former war stronghold and pirate-controlled zone.

---

## Udon Prison Mines
Forced labor mining facility.

---

## Ringo Province
Frozen land of fallen samurai traditions.

---

## Kuri Wilderness
Lawless region filled with rebels and outlaws.

---

# GOVERNMENT

System: Shogunate Absolute Rule

Leader:
- Shogun (central authority)

Structure:
- Daimyo regional lords
- Samurai military class
- Administrative bureaucrats

---

# LAW & SECURITY

## Samurai Enforcement System

Role:
- Maintain order across provinces
- Enforce Shogunate law
- Suppress rebellion activity

---

## Capital Guard Units
- Elite palace defenders
- Political security enforcement
- High-tier combat samurai squads

---

# MARINE PRESENCE

Status:
None officially (restricted access nation)

Reason:
- Closed country policy
- Natural barrier isolation
- Political resistance

---

# ECONOMY

Economic System:
Feudal + Resource-Based Industry

Currency:
Belly (limited external use)

---

## CORE ECONOMIC DRIVERS

- Weapon forging industry
- Kairoseki mining/export
- Agricultural production
- Forced labor mining systems (Udon)

---

# MAJOR INDUSTRIES

## Weapon Forging
Wano is the highest-grade weapon production nation.

Outputs:
- Katana blades
- Armor systems
- Specialized combat tools

---

## Kairoseki Mining
Strategic material production:
- Seastone cuffs
- Weapon-grade Kairoseki tools
- Marine anti-Devil Fruit equipment

---

## Agriculture
- Rice production
- Herbal medicine cultivation
- Regional food supply chains

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Threat Level:
EXTREME (Hidden infiltration zones only)

Common Activity:
- Covert entry operations
- Alliance negotiations
- Resource theft attempts
- Rebel support operations

---

# SECURITY LEVEL

Flower Capital: ★★★★★  
Onigashima Region: ★★★★★  
Udon Mines: ★★★★☆  
Kuri Wilderness: ★★★★☆  
Ringo Province: ★★★☆☆  

---

Core Identity:
“Honor, Duty, and Blade Discipline”
