# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\NORTH BLUE\NB-003_WHITECLIFF.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# WHITECLIFF
# ==================================================

Sea: North Blue  
Classification: Natural Hazard Island  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Whitecliff is a massive coastal island dominated by towering white limestone cliffs that encircle nearly the entire landmass.

The island is notorious among sailors as one of the most dangerous navigation zones in North Blue due to unpredictable winds, vertical currents, and unstable cliff collapses that can destroy ships before they reach shore.

Most ships avoid the island entirely unless forced by storms or navigation errors.

---

# CORE IDENTITY

Type

Natural Fortress Island

Function

Navigation Hazard Zone / Ship Graveyard Edge

Global Reputation

Extremely Dangerous / Uncharted Risk Area

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Total Size

Medium-Large Island

Dominant Feature

Vertical White Limestone Cliffs

Coastal Shape

Circular cliff ring surrounding inner basin

---

## STRUCTURE OF THE ISLAND

Whitecliff is divided into 3 major layers:

### 1. Outer Cliff Ring

- 300–800 meter vertical cliffs
- Constant erosion from sea wind
- Falling rock zones

### 2. Mid Slope Forest

- Dense forest growing on unstable terrain
- Hidden caves and sinkholes
- Limited safe paths

### 3. Inner Basin

- Calm valley-like zone
- Small freshwater lake
- Ancient ruins scattered

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Extreme Coastal Wind System

Weather Patterns

- Sudden wind shear
- Heavy fog formations
- Rapid storm cycles

Season Stability

Very Low

---

# NATURAL HAZARDS

## Primary Dangers

- Cliff collapses
- Sudden vertical wind currents
- Hidden underwater rocks
- Magnetic navigation interference
- Dense fog blindness

---

## Sea Danger Level

★★★★★ EXTREME

Ships entering too close to Whitecliff often:

- Lose navigation control
- Break hulls on submerged rock
- Are pushed vertically by wind walls

---

# NAVIGATION SYSTEM FAILURE ZONE

Whitecliff is classified as:

“Dead Compass Zone”

Effects:

- Log Pose instability
- Magnetic field distortion
- Eternal drift confusion

---

# RESOURCES

Despite danger, Whitecliff contains rare resources:

## Rare Materials

- White Limestone (high purity)
- Cliff Crystal (navigation resonance stone)
- Wind Ore (used for ship stability tech)

## Biological Resources

- Cliff herbs (medicinal plants)
- Fog moss (alchemical ingredient)

---

# FAUNA

## Surface Wildlife

- Cliff goats
- White seabirds
- Cave foxes

## Dangerous Species

- Rock Serpents (burrow in cliffs)
- Wind Hawks (attack in storms)
- Abyss Crabs (live in underwater caves)

---

# HUMAN ACTIVITY

## Population

Extremely Low

Estimated Inhabitants

< 500 individuals

---

## Settlement Type

Scattered survival villages hidden in cliff caves

---

## Occupations

- Cliff miners
- Herbal gatherers
- Lost sailors (survivors)
- Hermit navigators

---

# MAIN AREAS

## Cracked Horizon Cliffs

Largest cliff wall facing open sea

Known for:

- Shipwreck clusters
- Natural wind tunnels

---

## Whispering Cave Network

Massive cave system inside cliffs

Known for:

- Echo-based navigation
- Hidden survivor routes

---

## Inner Basin Ruins

Ancient civilization remains located in central valley

Believed to contain:

- Old navigation systems
- Pre-world government structures

---

# LOST CIVILIZATION THEORY

Many scholars believe Whitecliff was once:

- A navigation research hub
- Or ancient lighthouse network system

Evidence:

- Stone compass ruins
- Artificial wind channels
- Geometric cliff formations

---

# ECONOMY

Very limited local economy.

Main exchanges:

- Rare minerals trade
- Survival goods barter
- Illegal salvage from shipwrecks

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Pirate Presence

Low but highly dangerous

Common Behavior:

- Shipwreck scavenging
- Hidden treasure hunting
- Avoiding Marines entirely

---

# MARINE PRESENCE

Official stance:

Whitecliff is classified as:

“Unrecoverable Hazard Zone”

Marine activity:

- Occasional reconnaissance only
- No permanent base

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS (WHITECLIFF ZONE)

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|-----------|
|1|Sudden cliff collapse near path|
|2|Lost shipwreck survivor appears|
|3|Navigation compass completely fails|
|4|Wind wall forces ship upward|
|5|Cave entrance revealed after landslide|
|6|Rock Serpent attack from cliff|
|7|Fog blinds entire area|
|8|Ancient ruin structure discovered|
|9|Cliff avalanche blocks escape route|
|10|Unknown signal from deep cave|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

- Survive forced landing on Whitecliff
- Explore ancient ruins in inner basin
- Recover lost ship cargo from cliff wrecks
- Investigate strange magnetic interference
- Rescue trapped expedition team
- Discover origin of wind anomalies

---

# SECRET LORE

- Whitecliff may be artificially shaped by ancient civilization
- Wind patterns appear engineered, not natural
- Underground structures suggest pre-modern technology
- Some caves lead to unknown deeper tunnels below sea level

---

# GM NOTES

Whitecliff should feel like:

- Survival + exploration horror zone
- Navigation punishment area
- Mystery-heavy lore location
- Transition gate between safe seas and unknown zones

Recommended Use

- Travel hazard between arcs
- Exploration side arc
- Ancient lore discovery zone

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\NORTH BLUE\NB-004_HOWLING_BAY.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# HOWLING BAY
# ==================================================

Sea: North Blue  
Classification: Pirate Harbor Zone / Lawless Trade Bay  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Howling Bay is a massive semi-natural harbor surrounded by jagged cliffs and deep sea caves. The name comes from the constant “howling sound” produced by wind passing through the cliff tunnels and broken shipwreck structures.

It is one of the most chaotic maritime hubs in North Blue, functioning as a neutral ground where pirates, smugglers, mercenaries, and illegal merchants trade freely under unstable local control.

Unlike official ports, Howling Bay has no unified authority.

---

# CORE IDENTITY

Type

Lawless Maritime Trading Zone

Function

Pirate Harbor / Black Market Port / Smuggling Hub

Global Reputation

Extremely Dangerous / Unstable / High Profit Zone

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Total Size

Medium Island Bay System

Structure

- Outer Cliff Ring
- Central Harbor Basin
- Hidden Cave Ports
- Floating Dock Ruins

---

## NATURAL FORMATION

Howling Bay was formed by:

- Ancient volcanic collapse
- Sea erosion over centuries
- Submerged cave expansion

---

## BAY STRUCTURE

### 1. Outer Ring Cliffs

- Sharp stone walls surrounding entire bay
- Natural wind amplification system

### 2. Inner Harbor Waters

- Deep but unstable currents
- Frequent whirlpool formations

### 3. Hidden Cave Ports

- Secret docking points inside cliffs
- Used by smugglers and pirates

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Storm-Influenced Coastal Zone

Weather Behavior

- Sudden storms
- High wind bursts
- Rain walls moving across sea surface

---

# NATURAL HAZARDS

## Sea Hazards

★★★★★ EXTREME

- Whirlpool traps
- Sudden wave spikes
- Underwater rock spikes
- Navigation echo distortion

---

## Atmospheric Hazards

- Sound distortion winds
- Fog storms
- Lightning strike clusters

---

# PORT SYSTEM

## Main Harbor: “Broken Crown Port”

Description

The largest open docking zone in Howling Bay.

Function

- Pirate ship docking
- Smuggler exchange
- Illegal cargo trade

---

## Secondary Ports

### Rust Dock

- Old broken naval port
- Used for scrap trading

### Black Tide Pier

- Hidden dock used by high-level criminals

### Whisper Caverns

- Fully hidden underwater docking tunnels

---

# GOVERNANCE

There is no official government.

Instead, control is divided among:

## Pirate Syndicates

- Control docking fees
- Enforce “territory rules”

## Smuggler Guilds

- Manage illegal trade flow

## Mercenary Groups

- Provide protection services

---

# POWER STRUCTURE

## “Bay Council” (Unofficial)

A rotating power system formed by strongest groups:

- Pirate Captains
- Smuggling Lords
- Mercenary Leaders

No permanent leader exists.

---

# ECONOMY

## Economic Nature

Fully black-market based economy

Main Currency

- Belly (standard)
- Barter goods
- Weapon exchange credits

---

## Main Trades

- Illegal weapons
- Stolen cargo
- Slave-free labor contracts
- Rare navigation maps
- Devil Fruit rumors (low reliability)

---

# PIRATE ACTIVITY

Pirate Density

★★★★★ VERY HIGH

Common Crew Sizes

- Small crews (5–20)
- Mid crews (20–80)
- Syndicate fleets

---

## Pirate Behavior

- Constant territorial conflict
- Temporary alliances
- Betrayals common
- No permanent peace

---

# MARINE PRESENCE

Official Status

UNCONTROLLED ZONE

Marine Activity

- Occasional infiltration
- No permanent base
- High casualty rate for missions

---

# BLACK MARKET

## Market Type

Open Illegal Exchange Zone

Location

- Hidden docks
- Floating ships
- Cliff caves

---

## Contraband Types

# ==================================================
# STEELPORT
# ==================================================

Sea: North Blue  
Classification: Industrial Mega Port City

# OVERVIEW

Steelport is the largest industrial port city in North Blue, built around massive steel shipyards, weapon forges, and logistics networks.

Unlike typical port cities focused on trade, Steelport is a production powerhouse that fuels maritime economies across multiple seas.

It is known as the “Heart of Iron Trade Routes.”

# CORE IDENTITY

Type

Industrial Maritime Megacity

Function

# ==================================================
# MISTWOOD
# ==================================================

Sea: North Blue  
Classification: Fog Forest Island  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Mistwood is a vast forest island permanently covered in dense, shifting fog. Visibility is extremely limited, and even experienced navigators often lose direction within minutes of entering the forest.

The island is considered a “Living Navigation Trap” due to unpredictable terrain shifts and unnatural fog behavior that interferes with all known navigation systems.

Many who enter Mistwood never return.

---

# CORE IDENTITY

Type

Mystery Survival Forest Zone

Function

Exploration Hazard / Lost Civilization Zone

Global Reputation

Extremely Dangerous / Unstable Navigation / Unknown Lore

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Total Size

Large Forest Island

Structure

- Outer Fog Ring
- Dense Central Forest
- Hidden Elevation Zones
- Underground Root Systems

---

## TERRAIN LAYERS

### 1. Fog Boundary Zone

- Thick white-gray fog wall
- Navigation signals completely fail
- Sound distortion effects

### 2. Main Forest Core

- Ancient towering trees
- Constant low visibility
- Shifting paths

### 3. Deep Root Underground

- Natural tunnel systems
- Bioluminescent plant life
- Hidden ruins and caverns

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Permanent Fog Ecosystem

Weather Behavior

- No clear day/night cycle
- Fog density shifts unpredictably
- Sudden temperature drops

< 200 individuals

Central zone with highest fog density

Ruins of unknown civilization beneath forest roots

- Stone navigation pillars
- Broken mechanical structures
- Unknown writing systems

“Total Compass Collapse Area”

- Log Pose useless

# OVERVIEW

Crow Island is a hidden intelligence hub shrouded in permanent twilight fog, known only through fragmented maps and pirate rumors.

Unlike conventional islands, Crow Island does not appear consistently on navigation charts. Its location seems to shift slightly depending on weather, tides, and unknown environmental factors.

It is widely believed to be the central meeting point for illegal information brokers across North Blue.

# WINTER HEART
# ==================================================

Sea: North Blue  
Classification: Frozen Capital Region  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Winter Heart is a massive frozen continental region located in the far north of North Blue. Unlike typical winter islands, this area is permanently locked in a deep freeze that never thaws, regardless of seasonal changes.

The region is considered one of the most stable yet hostile cold environments in the world, combining extreme survival conditions with high political and military importance.

It is often referred to as “The Frozen Crown of the North Blue.”

---

# ==================================================

Sea: North Blue

The Spire is surrounded by frozen wastelands and impossible weather systems, making approach extremely dangerous.

Many believe it is a “sealed structure” hiding something at its core.

# NORTH BLUE SEA INFORMATION

## Overview

North Blue is a semi-hostile, semi-developed sea with strong kingdoms, industrial economies, and rising political tension.

---

## Sea Characteristics

- Navigation Difficulty: Medium
- Weather Stability: Medium-Low
- Sea Kings: Rare but dangerous
- Political Conflict: High
- Industrial Activity: Very High

---

## Key Features

- Kingdom-based world structure
- Industrial mega-cities exist
- Intelligence networks active
- Pirate syndicates organized
- Black market deeply integrated

---

## GM Core Identity

North Blue is NOT a beginner sea.

It is:

- Mid-tier campaign zone
- Political + industrial sandbox
- Espionage-heavy environment
- Preparation zone for Grand Line escalation

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\PARADISE\PA-000_PARADISE_CONNECTOR.md
# =====================================================

# PARADISE CONNECTOR SYSTEM

## 🌊 Purpose
This file connects Paradise (Grand Line First Half) with East Blue systems and defines how global world data transitions into Paradise logic.

It does NOT replace East Blue data.
It ONLY extends it.

---

## 🔗 Global Transition Rule

### From EAST BLUE → PARADISE

When a crew enters Reverse Mountain:

- All East Blue systems remain valid references
- BUT scaling rules change immediately:

| System | Change |
|---|---|
| Bounty Scale | ×10 multiplier baseline |
| Threat Evaluation | Global tier system activated |
| Navigation | Log Pose becomes mandatory |
| Marine Response | Multi-base coordination enabled |
| Pirate Behavior | Regional → Strategic |

---

## 🌐 World Integration Rule

East Blue and Paradise are NOT separate worlds.

They are:

> One world with different physics layers.

---

## 📊 SYSTEM TRANSFORMATION

### 🟦 BOUNTY SYSTEM SHIFT
East Blue logic:
- Local threat evaluation

Paradise logic:
- Cross-regional threat evaluation

Example:
- East Blue “10M Pirate” → Paradise “Low Tier Rookie”

---

### 🌊 ECONOMY SHIFT
- East Blue = Supply region
- Paradise = Conflict + trade disruption region

Trade routes become:
- unstable
- pirate-controlled
- Marine-protected corridors

---

### 📜 HISTORY IMPACT
Past East Blue events affect Paradise via:

- Reputation carry-over
- Government classification
- Hidden bounty modifiers

---

### 🪖 MARINE SYSTEM UPGRADE
Marine behavior expands from:

- Local patrol → Strategic fleet network

Paradise enables:

- Cross-island pursuit
- Multi-base coordination
- High-priority bounty tracking

---

### 🏴 PIRATE EVOLUTION RULE
Pirates entering Paradise:

- Gain survival adaptation bonus
- Increase faction awareness
- Become “named entities” faster

---

## 🧭 ROUTE INTEGRATION

East Blue route system ends at:

Loguetown → Reverse Mountain

Then transitions into:

Paradise Route Graph System (PA-ROUTES.md)

---

## ⚙️ GM CORE RULE

Never treat Paradise as “new content”.

Treat it as:

> “Upgraded simulation layer of the same world”

---

## 🔥 FINAL RULE

All East Blue files remain active references.

Paradise does NOT overwrite them.

It expands them.

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\PARADISE\PA-000_PARADISE_OVERVIEW.md
# =====================================================

# PARADISE (GRAND LINE – FIRST HALF)

## 🌊 Overview
Paradise is the first half of the Grand Line, a sea defined by unstable physics, extreme weather, and fragmented geopolitical control.

Unlike East Blue, Paradise is not a linear world.
It is a **network of islands (Island Nodes)** connected by probability-based navigation.

---

## 🧭 Core World Rule

Travel is not fixed.

Instead, movement is determined by:

- Log Pose synchronization
- Magnetic field shifts between islands
- Weather distortion zones
- Faction interference (Marines / Pirates / Revolutionaries)
- Narrative pressure (GM-driven world response)

---

## 🧠 World Structure (Paradise Layer Model)

Paradise is divided into 5 macro-layers:

### 1. 🚪 Entry Layer
- Reverse Mountain
- First exposure to Grand Line instability

### 2. ⚔️ Survival Layer
- Whisky Peak
- Little Garden
- Drum Island
> Focus: survival, resources, first conflicts

### 3. 👑 Kingdom Layer
- Alabasta
> Focus: political war, civil conflict, large-scale stakes

### 4. ⬆️ Vertical Layer
- Jaya
- Skypeia (Sky Route)
> Focus: unknown physics, vertical navigation, myth layers

### 5. 🏙️ Civilization Collapse Layer
- Water 7
- Enies Lobby
- Thriller Bark
- Sabaody Archipelago
> Focus: world system pressure, government escalation

---

## 🌐 Island System Rule

Each island is treated as a **NODE**, not a location.

Every node contains:

- Entry conditions
- Exit conditions
- Faction influence level
- Hidden route triggers
- Log Pose stability rating

---

## ⚖️ World Behavior Rule

The world reacts dynamically to:

- Player reputation
- Marine activity level
- Pirate expansion
- Trade disruption
- Major story events

---

## 🎯 GM Principle

Paradise must feel like:

> “A living system that moves even when players do nothing.”

- Marines patrol and shift routes
- Pirates relocate based on pressure
- Trade routes collapse or evolve
- Islands change importance over time

---

## 🧩 Design Philosophy

- No fixed progression path
- No guaranteed next island
- Exploration is probabilistic
- Narrative drives geography

---

## 🔥 Core Identity of Paradise

Paradise is not a map.

Paradise is a **living network of unstable worlds.**

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\PARADISE\PA-001_REVERSE_MOUNTAIN.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# REVERSE MOUNTAIN
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Reverse Mountain is the only known natural gateway that allows ships from the Four Blues to enter the Grand Line.

Rather than functioning as a traditional island with large civilian populations, Reverse Mountain is a massive continental mountain system located at the intersection of the Red Line and the Grand Line.

Powerful ocean currents flow upward from all four seas before merging at the summit and descending into Paradise.

Because every ship entering the Grand Line must pass through this location, Reverse Mountain has become one of the busiest maritime choke points in the world.

The surrounding region is constantly monitored by the World Government, Marine observers, independent navigators, merchants, bounty hunters, and pirates.

While no permanent kingdom exists here, temporary settlements, maintenance stations, rescue outposts, and supply facilities have gradually formed around the mountain.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Gigantic

Approximate Diameter

Over 300 km

Highest Elevation

Reverse Summit

Terrain Distribution

55% Mountain

20% Cliffs

15% Rivers

5% Harbors

5% Settlements

Coastline

Northern Entrance
Gateway from North Blue.

Eastern Entrance
Gateway from East Blue.

Southern Entrance
Gateway from South Blue.

Western Entrance
Gateway from West Blue.

Grand Line Exit

Massive waterfall-like current descending toward Paradise.

---

# CLIMATE

Heavy mist.

Cool upper elevations.

---

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## East Entrance

Receives ships arriving from East Blue.

The calmest approach among the four entrances.

Navigation beacons assist inexperienced crews.

---

## North Entrance

Steepest water current.

Dangerous whirlpools frequently appear.

Marine rescue vessels remain nearby.

---

## South Entrance

Known for unstable weather.

Strong crosswinds make steering difficult.

---

## West Entrance

Rock formations create numerous hidden caves.

Smugglers occasionally use these coves.

---

## Reverse Summit

Where all four currents merge.

The current becomes extremely violent.

No ship may safely stop here.

---

## Paradise Descent

The famous downward river leading into Paradise.

The current accelerates dramatically.

Failure to steer correctly often results in shipwreck.

---

# NATURAL PHENOMENA

Reverse Current

Water flows uphill against gravity.

No scientific explanation has ever been confirmed.

Grand Convergence

Four ocean currents merge into one.

The resulting pressure creates enormous waves.

Perpetual Mist

Warm and cold air collide constantly.

Visibility changes within minutes.

Echo Cliffs

Voices may echo across entire valleys.

Navigators sometimes mistake echoes for distress calls.

---

# SETTLEMENTS

Unlike most islands, Reverse Mountain contains only small operational facilities.

---

# SECRETS

Reverse Mountain contains enormous natural cave systems still unexplored.

Several Government facilities exist deep inside the mountain.

Ancient inscriptions suggest Reverse Mountain existed long before the current World Government.

Not every rescue mission is recorded officially.

Some missing ships never entered Paradise despite eyewitness reports.

---

Recommended Player Level

Early Paradise

Core Themes

Navigation

Survival

Discovery

Maritime Danger

Beginning of the Grand Line

Reverse Mountain should feel like the gateway separating the familiar world from the unpredictable dangers of Paradise.

Every arriving crew should immediately realize that life inside the Grand Line follows completely different rules.

# ==================================================
# WHISKY PEAK
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Whisky Peak is the first major settlement encountered by many crews after entering Paradise.

To outsiders, the island appears peaceful and welcoming. Music fills the streets, restaurants remain open throughout the night, and visitors are greeted with celebrations. Behind this cheerful façade, however, Whisky Peak has earned a notorious reputation as one of the Grand Line's largest bounty-hunting communities.

Almost every resident has received some form of combat training. Families pass down techniques for tracking, surveillance, and capturing dangerous criminals. Because of this, the island has developed a unique culture where hospitality and suspicion exist side by side.

Although bounty hunting remains the island's primary profession, legal commerce, tourism, ship repair, and information brokerage have also become important industries.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\PARADISE\PA-003_LITTLE_GARDEN.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# LITTLE GARDEN
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Little Garden is one of the most dangerous prehistoric islands in Paradise.

Unlike civilized islands, Little Garden has remained almost untouched for centuries. Massive volcanoes, ancient forests, gigantic rivers and countless prehistoric creatures dominate the landscape.

The island's ecosystem follows the laws of survival rather than civilization. Predators roam freely, enormous herbivores migrate across open plains, and violent volcanic activity constantly reshapes the terrain.

Few permanent residents exist. Most visitors are explorers, hunters, researchers, Marines conducting reconnaissance, or pirates seeking glory.

Because the Log Pose requires an exceptionally long time to record the island's magnetic field, many crews are forced to remain far longer than expected, greatly increasing their chances of encountering danger.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Large

Approximate Diameter

145 km

Highest Elevation

Mount Primordia

35% Primeval Forest

20% Volcanoes

15% Swamps

15% Plains

10% Rivers

5% Coastline

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\PARADISE\PA-004_DRUM_ISLAND.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# DRUM ISLAND
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Drum Island is a winter kingdom located deep within Paradise and is recognized throughout the Grand Line as one of the world's greatest centers of medical knowledge.

Towering snow-covered mountains dominate the island, while scattered villages survive within valleys protected from freezing winds. Nearly every family has some understanding of medicine, herbal treatment, or survival in extreme climates.

Although life is harsh, the people of Drum Island possess remarkable resilience. Visitors often arrive seeking doctors, rare medicines, or treatment for illnesses that cannot be cured elsewhere.

The island's environment is beautiful but unforgiving. Heavy snowfall, avalanches, blizzards, and dangerous wildlife constantly threaten travelers who venture beyond established roads.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Large

Approximate Diameter

125 km

Highest Elevation

15% Forest

10% Frozen Lakes

10% Settlements

5% Rivers

5% Coastline

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\PARADISE\PA-005_ALABASTA.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# ALABASTA KINGDOM
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Canon Kingdom
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Alabasta Kingdom is one of the oldest and largest nations affiliated with the World Government. Situated within Paradise, the kingdom spans an enormous desert continent where only a handful of fertile regions support permanent settlements.

Despite its harsh climate, Alabasta has flourished through centuries of engineering, trade, agriculture, and river management. Cities have been constructed around rivers, underground reservoirs, and ancient oasis systems, allowing civilization to thrive where survival should have been impossible.

Caravan routes connect distant settlements across endless dunes, while merchant ships arrive daily through western ports carrying goods from every corner of Paradise.

The kingdom is respected for its political stability, military discipline, and rich history, though maintaining order across such a vast desert remains a constant challenge.

Travelers often underestimate the dangers beyond the city walls. Sandstorms, giant wildlife, bandits, dehydration, and the immense scale of the desert claim countless lives every year.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Kingdom Size

Massive

Approximate Diameter

1,200 km

Highest Elevation

Mount Kestrel

Terrain Distribution

65% Desert

10% Rocky Highlands

8% Rivers

7% Oasis

5% Forest

5% Cities

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Subtropical Desert

Spring

Warm days.

Cool nights.

Strong seasonal winds.

---

Summer

Extremely hot.

Temperatures frequently exceed 45°C.

Travel becomes dangerous during daylight.

---

Autumn

Dry.

Stable weather.

Ideal for caravans.

---

Winter

Cool evenings.

Occasional rainfall.

Morning fog near rivers.

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources

---

Rare Resources

Blue Desert Crystal

Rare Oasis Flowers

High-Quality Glass Sand

Sea Prism Stone Fragments

Underground Mineral Veins

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Central Desert

The largest continuous desert within Alabasta.

Towering dunes shift constantly due to powerful winds.

Navigation without experienced guides is extremely dangerous.

Few permanent landmarks remain visible for long.

---

## Sandora River Basin

The kingdom's largest freshwater system.

Most agriculture depends upon its seasonal flooding.

Several major cities have developed along its banks.

---

## Eastern Highlands

Rocky mountains rich in minerals.

Mining communities operate throughout the region.

Hidden caves remain largely unexplored.

---

## Southern Oasis Belt

Chain of fertile oasis settlements connected by caravan roads.

Produces much of the kingdom's fruit and vegetables.

---

## Western Coast

Home to Alabasta's largest commercial ports.

Merchant fleets from Paradise arrive daily.

Fishing villages line the coastline.

---

## Northern Wastes

One of the least populated areas.

Violent sandstorms occur frequently.

Ancient ruins occasionally emerge from beneath the dunes before disappearing once again.

---

# RIVERS

## Sandora River

The largest river in Alabasta.

Provides water for millions of residents.

Supports agriculture, transportation, and freshwater fisheries.

---

## East Branch

Supplies eastern farming communities.

Flows throughout the year.

---

## Oasis Stream

Seasonal tributary connecting several oasis settlements.

Often dries during severe droughts.

---

# DESERT ECOSYSTEM

Although often described as empty, Alabasta's desert supports an enormous variety of life specially adapted to extreme conditions.

Water determines every aspect of survival.

Most wildlife becomes active after sunset.

Large predators remain hidden beneath sand until prey approaches.

Travelers rarely move during midday unless absolutely necessary.

Experienced caravan leaders navigate using stars, wind direction, rock formations, and ancient road markers rather than relying solely on maps.

---

# NATURAL PHENOMENA

## Great Sandstorms

Massive storms capable of reducing visibility to only a few meters.

Entire dunes may shift overnight.

Old ruins are frequently buried or uncovered.

---

## Mirage Fields

Extreme heat produces convincing optical illusions.

Inexperienced travelers often mistake mirages for real settlements.

---

## Singing Dunes

Certain dunes emit deep humming sounds when wind passes across their surfaces.

Local legends claim the sounds are voices from forgotten civilizations.

---

## Oasis Bloom

Following rare rainfall, dormant desert plants bloom simultaneously across hundreds of kilometers, transforming portions of the desert into fields of flowers for only a few days.

---

# NATURAL HAZARDS

Extreme Heat

Dehydration

Nighttime Cold

---

# SETTLEMENTS

Alabasta is one of the most populated kingdoms within Paradise.

Rather than concentrating its population in a single capital, the kingdom has developed numerous cities connected through caravan roads, river transportation, and coastal shipping routes.

Every settlement fulfills a specialized role within the kingdom's economy.

---

## Alubarna

Type

Royal Capital

Population

Approximately 95,000

Description

Alubarna serves as the political, administrative, and cultural center of Alabasta Kingdom.

Built upon elevated sandstone cliffs overlooking the Sandora River Basin, the capital is protected by massive defensive walls and centuries of architectural planning.

Wide boulevards divide the city into organized districts containing government offices, noble residences, military headquarters, universities, hospitals, libraries, and commercial markets.

Unlike many capitals across Paradise, Alubarna emphasizes public infrastructure, clean water distribution, and defensive preparedness against both natural disasters and military threats.

Nanohana is the kingdom's largest international harbor.

Merchant vessels from throughout Paradise arrive daily carrying luxury goods, industrial materials, food, books, navigation equipment, and foreign technologies.

The city rarely sleeps.

Warehouses, markets, inns, taverns and repair docks operate almost twenty-four hours a day.

Crime Rate

Low within cities.

Moderate across remote caravan routes.

Population Growth

Stable

Life Expectancy

Above Average for Paradise

---

# GOVERNMENT

## Political System

Alabasta is a hereditary constitutional monarchy officially recognized by the World Government.

The Royal Family serves as the head of state, while day-to-day administration is handled by ministers, provincial governors, military commanders, and civil officials.

The kingdom has maintained diplomatic relations with neighboring nations for centuries and is regarded as one of the most politically stable kingdoms within Paradise.

National priorities include:

- Public Safety
- Water Management
- Agriculture
- International Trade
- Scientific Development
- Medical Care
- Infrastructure
- Border Security

---

## Royal Family

The Royal Family has ruled Alabasta for hundreds of years.

Although succession follows bloodline traditions, heirs begin public administration training from an early age.

Members of the Royal Family rarely interfere with local government unless national emergencies occur.

Royal Responsibilities

- Foreign Diplomacy
- Military Authorization
- National Budget Approval
- Emergency Powers
- Appointment of Ministers
- Disaster Coordination

---

## Royal Council

The Royal Council functions as the kingdom's executive administration.

Departments

Ministry of Finance

Ministry of Agriculture

Ministry of Water Resources

Ministry of Commerce

Ministry of Transportation

Ministry of Justice

Ministry of Public Health

Ministry of Education

Ministry of Defense

Ministry of Archaeology

Every minister is supported by professional civil servants rather than hereditary nobles.

---

## Provincial Administration

Each city is governed by a Provincial Governor.

Responsibilities include

- Tax Collection
- Civil Registration
- Public Works
- Caravan Safety
- Water Distribution
- Local Courts
- Emergency Response

Village leaders report directly to provincial offices.

---

# LAW ENFORCEMENT

## Royal Guard

The Royal Guard protects government buildings, public officials and national infrastructure.

Primary Duties

- City Patrols
- Palace Security
- Criminal Arrests
- Crowd Control
- Escort Operations

Personnel

Approximately 6,000

Influence

The bureau frequently cooperates with Marine investigators.

---

# ROYAL ARMY

## Overview

The Royal Army serves as Alabasta's primary military force.

Because of the kingdom's enormous territory, units are stationed throughout every province.

Military doctrine emphasizes mobility, logistics and civilian protection over territorial conquest.

# MARINE PRESENCE

Internal matters remain under Royal jurisdiction.

# CULTURE

## General Culture

The people of Alabasta have adapted to one of the harshest environments in Paradise.

Life in the desert has taught generations that cooperation is more valuable than wealth, and that water is more precious than gold.

Hospitality is considered a sacred tradition. Refusing water to a traveler in genuine need is regarded as one of the gravest social disgraces.

Communities celebrate endurance, discipline, craftsmanship, and loyalty to one's family and hometown.

---

## Hospitality

Guests are traditionally welcomed with:

- Fresh Water
- Date Fruits
- Herbal Tea
- Shade
- Warm Meals

Foreign merchants are generally treated with respect, provided they obey local laws and customs.

---

## Social Classes

### Royal Family

Serves as the symbolic heart of the kingdom.

Responsible for national unity and diplomacy.

---

### Nobility

Own estates, oversee infrastructure projects and contribute to education and public works.

Many noble families sponsor hospitals, libraries and archaeological expeditions.

---

### Merchants

One of the most influential groups in Alabasta.

Large merchant houses finance caravan routes, ports and trade agreements throughout Paradise.

---

### Scholars

Highly respected.

Researchers, engineers, navigators and physicians enjoy considerable social status.

---

### Craftsmen

Stone masons, blacksmiths, glassmakers and carpenters are considered essential to desert civilization.

---

### Farmers

Responsible for maintaining oasis agriculture.

Efficient irrigation techniques are passed down across generations.

---

### Caravan Workers

Camel handlers, scouts, guards and navigators spend months traveling between settlements.

Their knowledge of the desert is unmatched.

---

# EDUCATION

Education is publicly supported by the kingdom.

Primary Subjects

Reading

Writing

Law

---

## Universities

Advanced education is available in major cities.

Common Fields

Engineering

Medicine

Architecture

Economics

Military Science

Botany

Geology

Navigation

---

## Libraries

Every provincial capital maintains public libraries.

The Royal Library houses thousands of historical documents and engineering records.

---

# RELIGION

Alabasta has no official state religion.

Instead, local traditions emphasize gratitude toward nature and respect for ancestors.

Common beliefs include:

Respect for Water

Respect for the Desert

Respect for Family

Protection of Ancient Ruins

Seasonal Celebrations

Many remote communities maintain shrines dedicated to local guardian spirits.

---

# FESTIVALS

## River Festival

Celebrates the annual flooding of the Sandora River.

Activities

Public Performances

Fireworks

---

## Desert Moon Festival

Held during the coolest nights of autumn.

Families gather beneath the stars to celebrate successful caravan journeys.

---

## Harvest Celebration

Occurs after major agricultural seasons.

Communities exchange food and gifts.

Musicians travel between villages performing traditional songs.

---

## Founding Day

Commemorates the establishment of the kingdom.

Military parades, public ceremonies and cultural exhibitions take place throughout Alabasta.

---

## Caravan Blessing

Before long expeditions depart, local priests and elders perform ceremonies wishing travelers safe passage across the desert.

# RUMORS

Game Masters may introduce these naturally.

1. An enormous buried city has recently been uncovered after a massive sandstorm.

2. Someone is purchasing extraordinary quantities of fresh water without explanation.

3. A forgotten underground river may still exist beneath the Central Desert.

4. Several caravans vanished despite leaving no signs of attack.

5. Strange blue lights appear near ancient ruins during full moons.

6. Desert Rangers recently discovered ruins older than the kingdom itself.

7. Smugglers have established a hidden market beneath abandoned mines.

8. An unknown noble family secretly finances organized bandits.

9. Rare flowers capable of producing powerful medicine bloom somewhere deep inside the desert.

10. A mysterious traveler has been collecting ancient maps from every major city.

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS

Roll 1D10 while traveling.

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|-----------|
|1|A merchant caravan requests armed protection.|
|2|A violent sandstorm approaches rapidly.|
|3|Royal Army patrol inspects travelers.|
|4|A lost camel wanders across the road carrying valuable cargo.|
|5|A wounded Desert Ranger asks for assistance.|
|6|Travelers discover an abandoned oasis.|
|7|A merchant offers a suspiciously cheap ancient relic.|
|8|Wild giant scorpions emerge after sunset.|
|9|A collapsed ruin reveals a hidden underground chamber.|
|10|A mysterious cloaked traveler quietly follows the party.|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

Escort a royal caravan across the Central Desert.

Investigate disappearing water shipments.

Protect engineers repairing a damaged aqueduct.

Discover who finances organized desert bandits.

Locate an ancient city uncovered by shifting sands.

Recover historical artifacts before smugglers steal them.

Escort doctors delivering medicine to isolated oasis settlements.

Investigate mysterious lights appearing beneath ruined temples.

Stop counterfeit merchants distributing fake medicine.

Map an unexplored section of the Northern Wastes.

Recover a priceless royal artifact stolen during a sandstorm.

Investigate reports of enormous creatures beneath the dunes.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## The Buried Observatory

Completely hidden beneath centuries of accumulated sand.

Contains ancient astronomical records and forgotten navigation charts.

---

## Crystal Cavern

Deep beneath the Eastern Highlands.

Rare blue crystals naturally illuminate the cavern.

Many sections remain unexplored.

---

## Forgotten Oasis

Hidden between massive dunes.

Unknown to modern maps.

Contains unusually fertile land and ancient stone ruins.

---

## Underground Aqueduct

A gigantic abandoned water distribution system built by an unknown civilization.

Some passages remain flooded.

Others lead toward forgotten chambers.

---

## The Silent Temple

Located beneath collapsed sandstone cliffs.

No inscriptions identify its builders.

The interior remains remarkably preserved despite its age.

---

## Desert Catacombs

A network of tunnels extending beneath multiple ruined settlements.

Many entrances have been buried by shifting sands.

Treasure hunters rarely return.

---

# SECRETS

The kingdom possesses engineering records describing underground water systems that no longer appear on modern maps.

Several ancient ruins were intentionally sealed by previous generations to prevent dangerous discoveries from becoming public.

Not every archaeological expedition reported to the government is officially documented.

Certain merchant families secretly finance illegal excavations throughout the desert.

Some underground chambers contain construction techniques that modern engineers still cannot reproduce.

The deepest desert continues to reveal forgotten structures after major sandstorms, suggesting that much of Alabasta's true history remains buried.

Several remote oasis communities preserve oral traditions describing civilizations older than the current kingdom.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

10–20 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Mid Paradise

Core Themes

- Survival
- Exploration
- Politics
- Ancient History
- Desert Adventure
- Trade
- Engineering
- Justice
- Resource Management

Alabasta should feel enormous.

Travel between cities should require planning, supplies and reliable navigation.

Every settlement should possess its own economy, traditions, problems and influential figures.

Water should be treated as one of the kingdom's most valuable strategic resources.

Player decisions may permanently affect:

- Caravan Safety
- Trade Prices
- Public Opinion
- Water Distribution
- Political Stability
- Merchant Relationships
- Crime Rates
- Military Readiness
- Archaeological Discoveries

Every journey across the desert should remind players that the environment itself is one of the greatest challenges in the Grand Line.

# ==================================================
# JAYA
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Jaya is one of the most unpredictable islands in Paradise.

Unlike kingdoms governed by centralized authority, Jaya is divided between civilized settlements, lawless pirate towns, dense tropical forests, ancient ruins, and unexplored highlands.

Its strategic position makes it a gathering point for pirates, bounty hunters, explorers, archaeologists, merchants, and adventurers preparing to continue deeper into the Grand Line.

The island is famous for stories of lost civilizations, hidden treasure, mysterious knock-up streams, and legends surrounding the Sky Islands.

Because no single government controls the island, every district has developed according to its own rules.

Violence is common in some regions, while others remain surprisingly peaceful.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Large

Approximate Diameter

95 km

Terrain Distribution

35% Tropical Forest

20% Rocky Highlands

15% Grasslands

10% Ancient Ruins

10% Settlements

10% Coastline

Highest Elevation

Mt. Bell Peak

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Mock Town

The island's most infamous settlement.

Pirates, bounty hunters, smugglers and mercenaries gather here.

Violence is common.

Despite its reputation, numerous legitimate businesses operate openly.

---

## South Jungle

Dense tropical rainforest.

Filled with dangerous wildlife.

Several forgotten ruins remain hidden beneath centuries of vegetation.

---

## Bell Highlands

Rocky mountains overlooking the island.

Excellent observation points.

Contains abandoned temples and collapsed structures.

---

## Eastern Coast

Fishing villages and merchant docks.

Relatively peaceful compared to Mock Town.

---

## Ancient Ruin Zone

Scattered remains of an unknown civilization.

Many archaeological expeditions have disappeared here.

# ==================================================
# SKYPIEA
# ==================================================

Sea: White Sea / White-White Sea
Classification: Sky Kingdom
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Skypiea is one of the largest civilizations that exists above the Grand Line.

Located thousands of meters above sea level, the kingdom rests upon enormous cloud formations known collectively as the White Sea.

Unlike the oceans below, transportation depends upon cloud currents, Wind Dial technology, aerial vessels and trained Sky Creatures capable of navigating the ever-changing atmosphere.

The people of Skypiea have developed an entirely different civilization from the Blue Sea, adapting to a world where clouds replace oceans, islands float freely, and weather changes with astonishing speed.

Although isolated from the surface for centuries, Skypiea has become an important center of Dial technology, cloud engineering, weather research and aerial navigation.

Visitors from the Blue Sea are uncommon but not unknown. Most arrive accidentally through Knock Up Streams or other rare atmospheric phenomena.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Kingdom Size

Large

Approximate Diameter

820 km

Highest Elevation

Upper White-White Sea

Terrain Distribution

40% Island Clouds

20% Cloud Ocean

15% Sacred Forest

10% Heavenly Rivers

8% Cloud Mountains

7% Settlements

---

# SKY LAYERS

## White Sea

Located approximately 7,000 meters above sea level.

Functions similarly to an ordinary ocean.

Most civilian transportation occurs here.

Contains countless cloud islands.

---

## White-White Sea

Approximately 10,000 meters above sea level.

Contains denser clouds capable of supporting entire cities.

Weather becomes significantly more unstable.

Rare creatures inhabit this region.

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Subtropical Sky Climate

Spring

Stable cloud currents.

Light rainfall.

Excellent visibility.

---

Summer

Warm temperatures.

Frequent Cloud Thunderstorms.

Powerful upward winds.

---

Autumn

Dense fog.

Strong crosswinds.

Ideal season for cloud harvesting.

---

Winter

Cold upper atmosphere.

Occasional Ice Clouds.

Reduced visibility.

---

Dials

Rare Resources

Ancient Dials

Sea Prism Fragments

Lightning Stones

Pure Milky Cloud

Sacred Giant Trees

Sky Crystals

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Angel Plateau

The political heart of Skypiea.

Large cloud plains support farms, government buildings and residential districts.

The majority of the kingdom's population lives here.

---

## Sacred Cloud Forest

A massive forest growing upon ancient Island Clouds.

Home to numerous rare animals and medicinal plants.

Ancient ruins remain hidden beneath dense vegetation.

---

## Thunder Highlands

A mountainous cloud region constantly surrounded by electrical storms.

Mining settlements harvest Lightning Stones and rare minerals.

Travel without experienced guides is extremely dangerous.

---

## Milky Ocean

A vast open region of dense cloud seas.

Primary route for commercial transportation.

Cloud Whales and Sky Kings are occasionally spotted here.

---

## Upper Mist Frontier

Northern frontier.

Thin cloud formations create unstable terrain.

Frequently used by explorers and weather researchers.

---

## Floating Archipelago

A chain of drifting islands slowly moving through seasonal wind currents.

Many small villages survive through fishing and Dial production.

---

# CLOUD RIVERS

## Heavenly Current

The largest navigable cloud river.

Connects nearly every major settlement.

Commercial vessels travel continuously throughout the year.

---

## Silver Stream

Flows through Angel Plateau.

Provides freshwater for agriculture.

---

## Mist Channel

A narrow cloud passage connecting remote villages.

Frequently obscured by heavy fog.

---

# SKY ECOSYSTEM

Life above the clouds has evolved differently from the Blue Sea.

Most animals possess lightweight skeletons, wide wings or natural buoyancy.

Cloud Fish swim through dense cloud currents as though they were water.

Vegetation anchors itself into Island Clouds using specialized root systems.

The ecosystem depends heavily upon weather cycles and the seasonal movement of cloud masses.

---

# NATURAL PHENOMENA

## Cloud Storms

Massive electrical storms capable of reshaping entire cloud formations.

Navigation becomes nearly impossible.

---

## Rainbow Bridges

Temporary cloud formations strengthened by moisture and sunlight.

Often remain stable for only a few hours.

---

## Cloud Bloom

Certain Island Clouds produce enormous flowering fields after extended rainfall.

The event attracts rare wildlife from across Skypiea.

---

## Wind Columns

Powerful vertical air currents capable of lifting ships hundreds of meters.

Experienced navigators use them to travel rapidly.

---

# NATURAL HAZARDS

Lightning Storms

Cloud Collapse

Extreme Winds

Fog Banks

Atmospheric Pressure

Air Turbulence

Sky Predator Attacks

Falling Cloud Cliffs

# SETTLEMENTS

The population of Skypiea is concentrated upon stable Island Clouds connected by cloud rivers and aerial routes.

Every settlement specializes in a different aspect of sky civilization.

---

## Angel City

Type

Royal Capital

Population

Approximately 48,000

Description

The political and cultural center of Skypiea.

Constructed upon one of the oldest stable Island Clouds, Angel City contains government institutions, public plazas, universities, markets and major Dial workshops.

Wide cloud bridges connect every district while artificial waterways distribute fresh rainwater across the city.

Major Facilities

Royal Palace

Sky Council Hall

Central Market

---

Population

Famous for skilled Dial Engineers and Cloud Ship builders.

Exports advanced navigation equipment across the White Sea.

---

# GOVERNMENT

## Political System

Skypiea is governed by a constitutional monarchy supported by a representative Sky Council.

The Monarch serves as Head of State while executive authority is shared with ministers, provincial governors and elected representatives from the major settlements.

Because survival above the clouds depends heavily upon cooperation, government policy emphasizes public safety, weather management and transportation infrastructure.

National Priorities

- Public Safety
- Weather Observation
- Dial Research
- Transportation
- Trade
- Environmental Protection
- Medical Care
- Scientific Development

---

## Royal Family

The Royal Family has ruled Skypiea for centuries.

Although respected as symbols of unity, members of the Royal Family rarely interfere with local administration unless national emergencies occur.

Royal Responsibilities

- Foreign Diplomacy
- Military Authorization
- Disaster Response
- National Budget
- Appointment of Ministers
- Emergency Declarations

---

## Sky Council

The Sky Council serves as the executive administration.

Departments

Ministry of Transportation

Ministry of Weather

Ministry of Trade

Ministry of Science

Ministry of Health

Ministry of Agriculture

Ministry of Defense

Ministry of Justice

Ministry of Infrastructure

Ministry of Education

---

## Provincial Administration

Each settlement is governed by a Sky Governor.

Responsibilities

- Public Safety
- Civil Registration
- Transportation
- Weather Emergency Response
- Trade Regulation
- Infrastructure Maintenance
- Local Courts

Village Elders report directly to provincial governors.

---

# CULTURE

## General Culture

Life above the clouds revolves around harmony with nature.

The people of Skypiea believe survival depends upon cooperation rather than conquest.

Hospitality, craftsmanship and respect for the sky are considered the foundation of civilized life.

Music is deeply embedded within everyday culture.

Many celebrations include wind instruments, drums and Tone Dials capable of recording performances.

Communities place enormous value on environmental preservation and technological innovation.

---

# RUMORS

Game Masters may introduce these naturally during exploration.

1. A floating island has recently appeared beyond the Upper Mist Frontier but disappears every sunrise.

2. Several merchant ships have vanished without signs of storms or attacks.

3. Ancient Dials recovered from forgotten ruins have begun activating on their own.

4. Explorers claim to have discovered enormous ruins hidden beneath the Sacred Cloud Forest.

5. Strange lights have been observed inside thunderclouds where no lightning should exist.

6. Rare Cloud Whales have altered their annual migration routes for unknown reasons.

7. Smugglers are secretly transporting military-grade Dials through abandoned cloud tunnels.

8. An isolated village possesses technology capable of creating artificial Island Clouds.

9. A mysterious traveler from the Blue Sea has been purchasing every ancient map available.

10. Several weather stations have reported impossible atmospheric readings from the White-White Sea.

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS

Roll 1D10 while traveling across the White Sea.

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|-----------|
|1|A merchant sky ship requests escort through unstable weather.|
|2|A sudden lightning storm blocks the planned route.|
|3|Sky Guard inspectors stop the party for identification.|
|4|A damaged cloud bridge begins collapsing beneath nearby travelers.|
|5|Researchers request assistance investigating strange weather activity.|
|6|A drifting island slowly approaches before disappearing into heavy fog.|
|7|An engineer offers to trade a rare experimental Dial.|
|8|A flock of aggressive Storm Hawks attacks passing vessels.|
|9|A hidden ancient shrine is revealed after part of a cloud collapses.|
|10|An unknown sky ship silently follows the party before vanishing into the mist.|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

Escort a merchant convoy through dangerous thunderclouds.

Investigate the disappearance of several White Sea cargo vessels.

Protect engineers repairing a collapsing cloud bridge.

Recover stolen military Dials before they reach the black market.

Explore newly discovered ruins beneath the Sacred Cloud Forest.

Escort scientists researching unstable atmospheric currents.

Track mysterious smugglers using abandoned cloud passages.

Locate an island that only appears during violent storms.

Map unexplored regions of the White-White Sea.

Protect a Weather Observatory threatened by increasingly violent storms.

Investigate reports of giant creatures living beneath dense cloud layers.

Discover why ancient Dials have begun activating after centuries of silence.

Recover lost navigation records from an abandoned floating observatory.

Escort diplomats traveling between isolated sky settlements.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## The Forgotten Sky Temple

Hidden deep inside the Sacred Cloud Forest.

The temple predates the current kingdom and contains enormous stone mechanisms powered by forgotten Dials.

---

## Endless Thunder Basin

A massive storm permanently trapped within a ring of cloud mountains.

Lightning never ceases.

Researchers believe unknown minerals deep inside the clouds generate the phenomenon.

---

## The Silent Observatory

An abandoned astronomical station built upon an isolated Island Cloud.

Ancient weather records remain remarkably well preserved.

---

## Crystal Cloud Cavern

Hidden beneath the White-White Sea.

Natural crystal formations illuminate the cavern without fire or sunlight.

Rare medicinal plants grow nowhere else.

---

## The Drifting Sanctuary

A sacred island that slowly circles Skypiea every few years.

Its location changes constantly, making reliable maps impossible.

---

## Ancient Dial Vault

An underground storage complex sealed centuries ago.

Thousands of experimental Dials remain untouched.

Many have never been identified.

---

## Mist Labyrinth

A maze of dense fog and unstable cloud formations.

Navigation instruments become unreliable.

Many explorers wander for days before escaping.

---

# SECRETS

Several government archives describe civilizations that existed in the sky long before the current kingdom was founded.

Not every ancient Dial discovered by archaeologists is publicly documented.

Certain experimental Dials possess functions unknown even to modern engineers.

Hidden cloud tunnels connect remote regions of Skypiea without appearing on official maps.

The Weather Observatory secretly monitors atmospheric phenomena that cannot be explained by modern science.

Some floating islands slowly migrate around the Grand Line over periods lasting decades.

Deep beneath the White-White Sea exist cloud formations dense enough to support enormous underground ecosystems.

Several noble families quietly finance expeditions searching for forgotten Dial technology capable of transforming the balance of power across the sky.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

10–20 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Mid Paradise

Core Themes

- Exploration
- Discovery
- Technology
- Adventure
- Weather
- Navigation
- Ancient Civilization
- Scientific Research
- Aerial Survival

Skypiea should feel completely different from every Blue Sea island.

Travel should emphasize three-dimensional movement through cloud oceans, floating islands and changing wind currents rather than ordinary sailing.

Weather is not simply background scenery.

Storms, cloud currents and atmospheric pressure should actively influence travel, combat, trade and exploration.

Dial technology should be present throughout everyday life, making the kingdom feel technologically unique while remaining faithful to the One Piece world.

Every settlement should possess its own identity, economy and traditions centered around life above the clouds.

Player decisions may permanently affect

- Trade Routes
- Weather Safety
- Public Opinion
- Scientific Discoveries
- Dial Technology
- Government Stability
- Merchant Relationships
- Crime Levels
- Transportation Infrastructure

The White Sea should always inspire wonder.

Players should constantly feel that they are exploring a civilization unlike anything found below the clouds, where the sky itself is both the greatest opportunity and the greatest danger.

# END OF FILE

# ==================================================
# LONG RING LONG LAND
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Grassland Archipelago
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Long Ring Long Land is a unique archipelago composed of numerous small islands connected only during periods of extremely low tide.

The islands are famous for their endless grasslands, gentle climate, and unusual wildlife whose bodies have adapted over countless generations to the island's extraordinary environment.

Because the sea periodically recedes, local residents traditionally travel between islands on foot, allowing trade, festivals and cultural exchange to flourish.

Although peaceful compared to many Grand Line islands, travelers should never underestimate the dangers of sudden tidal changes, wild animals and isolated grassland regions.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type

Large Archipelago

470 km

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Central Prairie

The largest grassland in the archipelago.

Huge herds of wildlife roam freely.

---

## Eastern Highlands

Rolling hills overlooking the surrounding sea.

Windmills and ranches dominate the landscape.

---

## Western Woodland

Dense forests rich in medicinal plants and wildlife.

Several unexplored ruins remain hidden beneath the trees.

---

## Southern Coast

Fishing villages and small harbors line the coastline.

Trade vessels arrive during calm seasons.

---

## Northern Marsh

Wetlands filled with rare birds and medicinal plants.

Travel is difficult after rainfall.

---

# NATURAL PHENOMENA

## Great Low Tide

Several times each year, the sea retreats dramatically.

Temporary land bridges appear between islands.

Entire trade routes become accessible on foot.

---

## Endless Wind

Strong ocean winds constantly sweep across the plains.

Windmills provide energy for many villages.

---

## Golden Bloom

Every spring, enormous fields of wildflowers cover the grasslands.

The event attracts merchants and travelers from nearby islands.

---

# ==================================================
# WATER 7
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Maritime City-State
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Water 7 is the greatest shipbuilding city in Paradise and one of the most prosperous maritime centers anywhere in the Grand Line.

Built upon a vast network of canals, waterways and artificial islands, the city has adapted to life surrounded by the sea for centuries.

Every district is connected by bridges, locks, water elevators and canals where transportation never truly stops.

The city attracts merchants, engineers, navigators, inventors and adventurers from every corner of the world.

Its reputation rests upon master shipwrights capable of constructing vessels that can survive even the most dangerous seas of the Grand Line.

Despite its wealth and technological advancement, Water 7 constantly struggles against one unstoppable enemy:

The sea itself.

Every year the city prepares for Aqua Laguna, a catastrophic tidal disaster that threatens to destroy everything built by generations before.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

City Type

Artificial Maritime Metropolis

Approximate Diameter

38 km

Terrain Distribution

45% Urban Districts

30% Canals

10% Harbor Facilities

8% Shipyards

5% Parks

2% Elevated Structures

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Humid Maritime

Spring

Warm

Frequent rain

Stable tides

---

Summer

Hot

Humid

Heavy rainfall

---

Autumn

Mild

Ideal sailing conditions

---

Winter

Cool

Windy

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources

Fresh Water

Timber Imports

Steel Imports

Stone

Fish

Seafood

Industrial Materials

---

Rare Resources

Ancient Blueprints

Experimental Ship Components

Sea Prism Stone Fragments

High-grade Navigation Equipment

---

# NATURAL PHENOMENA

## Aqua Laguna

The greatest natural disaster affecting Water 7.

Once every year, enormous tidal waves generated somewhere within the Grand Line strike the city with devastating force.

Water levels rise dramatically.

Entire districts may flood.

Transportation completely changes.

Emergency flood barriers are activated throughout the city.

Citizens begin preparations weeks before the event.

Shipyards suspend construction.

Government offices coordinate evacuations and emergency shelters.

Every resident respects Aqua Laguna.

No one underestimates it.

---

## High Tide Canals

The city's canals constantly change depth depending upon tides.

Special locks regulate water flow throughout the districts.

---

## Floating Markets

Certain commercial districts operate entirely upon floating platforms.

As water levels change, entire marketplaces rise and fall with the canals.

---

# MAJOR DISTRICTS

## Central District

The administrative and commercial heart of Water 7.

Government offices, financial institutions and public squares dominate the area.

Large bridges connect every surrounding district.

---

## Grand Shipyard District

Home to the world's most respected shipbuilders.

Massive dry docks line the waterfront.

Construction continues day and night.

Visitors from across Paradise arrive seeking new vessels.

---

## Merchant Quarter

The busiest commercial district.

Warehouses, banks, inns, restaurants and trading companies operate continuously.

International merchants are a common sight.

---

## Harbor District

Contains passenger terminals, cargo ports and customs facilities.

Hundreds of ships arrive every week.

Marine inspections occur regularly.

---

## Residential Canals

Quiet neighborhoods connected by narrow waterways.

Most residents travel using small canal boats rather than walking.

Schools, hospitals and public gardens are concentrated here.

---

## Old Water District

One of the oldest surviving sections of the city.

Ancient stone buildings overlook narrow canals.

Many structures preserve traditional architecture despite repeated flooding.

---

## Northern Dry Dock

Specialized industrial district.

Large-scale military and commercial vessels are assembled here.

Heavy engineering equipment operates continuously.

---

## Eastern Locks

Controls the city's complex water management system.

Engineers monitor canal levels twenty-four hours a day.

Failure of these facilities would endanger the entire city.

---

# WATERWAYS

## Grand Canal

The primary transportation route.

Connects every major district.

Large cargo vessels travel throughout the day.

---

## Merchant Canal

Supports commercial traffic.

Warehouses line both banks.

---

## Residential Waterways

Smaller canals serving neighborhoods.

Most civilian transportation occurs here.

---

## Engineering Channel

Restricted industrial route connecting shipyards with dry docks.

Heavy construction vessels operate continuously.

---

# TRANSPORTATION

Common Methods

Canal Boat

Water Taxi

Cargo Vessel

Walking

Drawbridge Transit

Horse Wagon

Travel throughout Water 7 depends almost entirely upon its canal network.

Private boats are common among residents.

Commercial transportation operates day and night.

---

# CITY INFRASTRUCTURE

Water 7 possesses one of the most advanced urban infrastructures anywhere in Paradise.

Major Systems

Canal Network

Flood Barriers

Water Locks

Ship Elevators

Public Bridges

Drainage Systems

Emergency Flood Gates

Cargo Rail Platforms

Engineering maintenance continues every day to ensure the city remains operational despite constant exposure to the sea.

---
# GOVERNMENT

## Political System

Water 7 is governed as an autonomous City-State officially recognized by the World Government.

Rather than a hereditary monarchy, the city is administered by a Mayor supported by a Maritime Council composed of representatives from industry, commerce, engineering, finance and public administration.

Because nearly every aspect of the city depends upon its waterways, government policy prioritizes infrastructure maintenance, flood prevention and maritime commerce.

National Priorities

- Shipbuilding
- Flood Prevention
- Maritime Trade
- Public Infrastructure
- Scientific Innovation
- Economic Stability
- Public Safety
- International Diplomacy

---

## Mayor

The Mayor serves as both Head of Government and Chief Administrator.

Responsibilities

- National Budget
- Infrastructure Planning
- Emergency Authority
- Foreign Relations
- Economic Development
- Disaster Response

---

## Maritime Council

The Maritime Council advises the Mayor on city administration.

Departments

# CULTURE

## General Culture

Water 7 has developed a culture centered around craftsmanship, cooperation and life upon the water.

Every citizen grows up surrounded by canals, bridges and ships.

Engineering is not viewed simply as a profession, but as an art passed from one generation to the next.

Citizens take enormous pride in the city's reputation as the greatest shipbuilding center in Paradise.

Visitors quickly notice that conversations about ships, weather and Aqua Laguna are part of everyday life.

Because international merchants constantly arrive from across the Grand Line, Water 7 has become one of the most culturally diverse cities in Paradise.

---

## Hospitality

Guests are traditionally welcomed with

Fresh Seafood

Warm Bread

Coffee

Fruit Juice

Local Wine

Fresh Fish Soup

Foreign merchants are treated respectfully as long as they obey local law and harbor regulations.

---

## Daily Life

Life begins early.

Fishing boats leave before sunrise.

Shipyards become active shortly after dawn.

Markets remain busy throughout the day while restaurants and taverns become crowded after sunset.

Canal traffic rarely stops, even late at night.

Most citizens travel by boat instead of walking whenever possible.

---

## Social Classes

### Government Officials

Responsible for administration, infrastructure and disaster preparation.

Highly respected for maintaining one of the world's most complicated canal systems.

---

### Master Shipwrights

The highest respected craftsmen in Water 7.

Receiving certification as a Master Shipwright is considered one of the greatest professional achievements.

---

### Engineers

Responsible for bridges, locks, flood barriers and mechanical innovation.

Many spend decades perfecting specialized fields.

---

### Merchants

International commerce gives wealthy merchants considerable influence.

Many operate trading companies across Paradise.

---

### Sailors

Thousands of sailors pass through Water 7 every month.

Many eventually settle permanently within the city.

---

### Fishermen

Continue centuries-old traditions.

Fresh seafood remains one of Water 7's largest food industries.

---

### Craftsmen

Carpenters

Blacksmiths

Mechanics

Furniture Makers

Rope Makers

Sail Weavers

All are essential to the city's economy.

---

---

## Public Libraries

Every district maintains libraries.

The National Maritime Archive contains thousands of navigation charts, engineering documents and historical ship designs.

---

# RELIGION

Water 7 has no official religion.

Most citizens instead place their faith in tradition, craftsmanship and community.

Help Neighbors During Disaster

Many neighborhoods maintain small shrines dedicated to sailors lost at sea.

# RUMORS

Game Masters may introduce these naturally.

1. An abandoned dry dock beneath the city contains the remains of an unfinished legendary vessel.

2. Several engineers have disappeared after accepting confidential construction contracts.

3. Strange sounds echo through forgotten canals late at night.

4. Someone has begun stealing rare shipbuilding blueprints from private workshops.

5. Divers discovered enormous stone structures beneath the oldest district.

6. An unknown craftsman has been producing ship components far beyond modern technology.

7. Smugglers are using hidden flood tunnels beneath the city.

8. Aqua Laguna has become slightly stronger every year for reasons no scientist can explain.

9. A merchant recently purchased an ancient blueprint for an unbelievable price.

10. Old maintenance maps describe sealed sections of Water 7 that no longer appear on official records.

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS

Roll 1D10 while exploring Water 7.

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|-----------|
|1|A cargo ship accidentally blocks a major canal, causing citywide traffic delays.|
|2|The Water Guard requests assistance chasing a smuggling boat.|
|3|A famous shipwright is looking for rare construction materials.|
|4|A bridge temporarily closes due to emergency maintenance.|
|5|A merchant offers an old navigation chart recovered from a wreck.|
|6|Unexpected heavy rain rapidly raises canal water levels.|
|7|Workers uncover an unknown underground passage beneath a construction site.|
|8|A damaged cargo vessel requests emergency repairs before Aqua Laguna arrives.|
|9|A mysterious inventor demonstrates an experimental machine that immediately malfunctions.|
|10|A child discovers an old ship component bearing the emblem of a forgotten shipyard.|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

Escort valuable shipbuilding materials across the city.

Investigate the disappearance of several master shipwrights.

Protect engineers repairing the Eastern Flood Gates before Aqua Laguna.

Recover stolen blueprints before they are sold overseas.

Explore forgotten tunnels beneath the Old Water District.

Escort a newly completed luxury vessel during its maiden voyage.

Investigate mysterious sabotage occurring inside the Grand Shipyard.

Search for an abandoned dry dock mentioned only in historical records.

Protect a foreign diplomat visiting Water 7 during the Maritime Trade Fair.

Recover priceless engineering documents from a flooded archive.

Escort researchers investigating unusual tidal patterns beneath the city.

Track smugglers using abandoned maintenance canals.

Discover who has been secretly purchasing obsolete shipbuilding technology.

Investigate rumors of an ancient vessel buried beneath the foundations of Water 7.

Prevent organized criminals from sabotaging the city's flood defense system.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## Forgotten Dry Dock

Hidden beneath the oldest section of the city.

An enormous underground dock abandoned centuries ago.

Several unfinished vessels remain untouched.

---

## The Flood Tunnels

A massive maintenance network built beneath Water 7.

Originally constructed to redirect floodwater during Aqua Laguna.

Many passages have long been sealed.

---

## Ancient Foundation Chamber

Below the Central District lies a forgotten stone complex predating the modern city.

Its builders remain unknown.

---

## The Silent Workshop

An abandoned shipyard where experimental construction techniques were once developed.

Most tools remain exactly where they were left.

---

## Deep Canal Vault

A reinforced chamber beneath the Engineering Bureau.

Contains historical engineering records and emergency flood blueprints.

Access is heavily restricted.

---

## Sunken Warehouse

A commercial warehouse lost beneath rising sea levels decades ago.

Still contains intact cargo protected by sealed storage rooms.

---

## Observatory Tower

An old navigation tower overlooking the entire city.

Modern equipment has replaced it, but ancient maritime records remain inside.

---

# SECRETS

Historical records suggest Water 7 has been rebuilt numerous times after catastrophic flooding.

Several sections of the city's oldest foundations are far older than the current government admits.

Some engineering techniques used by the Shipwright Guild cannot be reproduced by modern craftsmen.

Hidden emergency flood gates exist beneath the city that appear on no official map.

Certain wealthy merchants secretly compete to obtain forgotten shipbuilding blueprints from across the Grand Line.

Engineers have recorded subtle changes in Aqua Laguna for decades, yet no one understands why the tides continue to grow stronger.

Legends claim an unfinished masterpiece vessel still rests somewhere beneath the city, waiting for the right shipwright to complete it.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

12–24 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Mid Paradise

Core Themes

- Maritime Adventure
- Engineering
- Urban Exploration
- Political Intrigue
- Trade
- Shipbuilding
- Investigation
- Disaster Survival
- Innovation

Water 7 should feel alive every hour of the day.

Ships constantly arrive and depart.

Construction never truly stops.

Markets remain busy, bridges rise and lower, and canals are always filled with traffic.

The city itself should feel like a living machine powered by thousands of workers.

Aqua Laguna is not simply an annual disaster.

It should shape architecture, economy, politics and the daily lives of every citizen.

Shipbuilding should be presented as both an industry and an art.

Master Shipwrights are celebrities whose work can influence commerce across the Grand Line.

Player decisions may permanently affect

- Harbor Security
- International Trade
- Shipbuilding Reputation
- Merchant Relationships
- Engineering Development
- Public Opinion
- Canal Infrastructure
- Crime Levels
- Flood Defense Readiness
- Economic Stability

Every visit to Water 7 should remind players that this city was built by human ingenuity against the overwhelming power of the sea.

Its greatest strength is not its walls or its wealth—

but the determination of the people who rebuild it, year after year.

# END OF FILE

# ==================================================
# ENIES LOBBY
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: World Government Judicial Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Enies Lobby serves as the primary judicial center of the World Government within Paradise.

Unlike ordinary islands, Enies Lobby functions as a massive governmental complex dedicated to law, criminal prosecution, intelligence coordination and high-security detention transfer.

Every individual arriving at the island is subject to strict inspection and identification procedures.

The island receives judges, prosecutors, investigators, Marine officers and government officials from every region under World Government authority.

Because of its political significance, Enies Lobby maintains some of the highest security standards anywhere in Paradise.

To ordinary citizens it symbolizes justice.

To criminals it represents the final destination before imprisonment.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type

Artificial Fortress Island

Approximate Diameter

26 km

Terrain Distribution

35% Government Buildings

25% Defensive Structures

15% Military Facilities

10% Administrative Districts

8% Courtyards

5% Bridges

2% Harbor

---

# CLIMATE

Temperate Maritime

Cool

Stable

---

Warm

Clear Skies

---

---
