# MAJOR DISTRICTS

## Central Judicial Plaza

The symbolic center of Enies Lobby.

Government ceremonies, official announcements and public hearings take place here.

Large stone plazas connect every major government building.

---

## Supreme Courthouse

The largest judicial facility on the island.

Contains numerous courtrooms, evidence vaults and judicial archives.

Thousands of legal cases are processed every year.

---

## Administrative Quarter

Houses government ministries, record offices and civil administration.

Only authorized personnel may access certain sections.

---

## Security District

Military barracks, armories and training grounds.

Home to elite government security personnel.

Access is heavily restricted.

---

## Intelligence Wing

Contains offices responsible for intelligence analysis, classified investigations and secure communications.

Most facilities remain closed to civilians.

---

## Government Harbor

The only official harbor on Enies Lobby.

Every arriving vessel undergoes strict inspection.

Civilian traffic is extremely limited.

---

## Judicial Archives

One of the largest collections of legal records maintained by the World Government.

Historical cases dating back centuries are preserved here.

---

## Bridge of Conviction

A heavily fortified bridge connecting the courthouse with prisoner transportation facilities.

Constantly guarded.

Only authorized transfers are permitted.

---

# INFRASTRUCTURE

Major Systems

Government Archives

Military Barracks

Emergency Shelters

Communication Network

Secure Transport Routes

Armories

Evidence Vaults

Prisoner Processing Centers

The island has been designed for security before convenience.

Nearly every building connects through controlled checkpoints.

---

# DAILY LIFE

Unlike ordinary cities, Enies Lobby never truly sleeps.

Court proceedings begin early every morning.

Government officials work throughout the day processing investigations, legal documents and administrative matters.

Military patrols operate continuously.

Large numbers of government messengers travel between departments delivering classified information.

The atmosphere is disciplined, orderly and highly structured.

Citizens and employees alike are expected to follow regulations precisely.

---

★★★★★

Visitors quickly realize that almost every section of the island is monitored.

Unauthorized access rarely goes unnoticed.
# GOVERNMENT

## Administrative System

Enies Lobby is administered directly by the World Government.

Unlike ordinary kingdoms, the island possesses no independent ruler or local parliament.

Every department ultimately answers to the Judicial Administration Bureau, which coordinates legal procedures, inter-agency cooperation and government operations throughout the island.

Primary Responsibilities

- Judicial Administration
- Criminal Prosecution
- Legal Documentation
- Intelligence Coordination
- Prisoner Processing
- National Security
- Government Logistics
- International Legal Affairs

---

## Chief Judicial Administrator

The highest-ranking civilian official stationed on Enies Lobby.

Responsibilities

Approve major legal proceedings

Coordinate government agencies

Authorize prisoner transfers

Supervise judicial administration

Manage emergency operations

Represent the World Government during international legal affairs

# CULTURE

## General Culture

Although Enies Lobby is not a traditional civilian city, it possesses a distinct institutional culture built upon discipline, order and absolute professionalism.

Life on the island revolves around schedules, regulations and official responsibilities.

Employees are expected to maintain punctuality, confidentiality and impartiality regardless of their position.

Unlike commercial cities, social status is determined primarily by experience, competence and public service rather than wealth.

---

## Daily Life

Government offices begin operating shortly after sunrise.

Court hearings occupy most of the day.

Administrative departments continue processing reports and legal documents well into the evening.

Marine patrols rotate continuously.

Evidence laboratories, archives and communication centers operate twenty-four hours a day.

Nighttime is noticeably quieter, though security activity never decreases.

---

## Hospitality

Visitors granted official access are welcomed professionally.

Government Guest Houses provide

Clean Accommodation

Medical Assistance

Dining Facilities

Meeting Rooms

Escort Services

Every visitor is accompanied while inside restricted areas.

---

## Social Structure

### Judicial Officials

Judges, prosecutors and senior legal advisors.

Responsible for interpreting and applying national law.

---

### Government Administrators

Coordinate documentation, finance, logistics and personnel.

Form the administrative backbone of Enies Lobby.

---

### Investigators

Collect evidence and prepare criminal cases.

Often cooperate with Marine investigators.

---

### Marines

Protect the island and support judicial operations.

Visible throughout every district.

---

### Engineers

Maintain bridges, communication systems and security infrastructure.

Essential during emergencies.

---

### Medical Personnel

Operate hospitals, emergency clinics and forensic laboratories.

---

### Civilian Workers

Teachers

Maintenance Staff

Archivists

Chefs

Cleaners

Dock Workers

Technical Specialists

Support daily government operations.

---

# RUMORS

Game Masters may introduce these naturally.

1. A forgotten courtroom beneath the island still contains sealed evidence from centuries ago.

2. Several classified case files have recently disappeared from the National Archive.

3. Unknown individuals have been forging official government documents.

4. Hidden maintenance tunnels connect buildings never shown on official maps.

5. An abandoned evidence vault has recently been rediscovered.

6. A retired judge secretly preserved records from a controversial historical trial.

7. Strange sounds echo beneath the Bridge of Conviction during quiet nights.

8. Government engineers recently discovered ancient foundations beneath the courthouse.

9. Someone has attempted to bribe officials responsible for prisoner transfers.

10. Certain classified records are believed to exist only in handwritten form.

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|-----------|
|1|Judicial Security officers perform a routine identification inspection.|
|2|A prosecutor urgently requests additional witnesses for an ongoing trial.|
|3|Government messengers accidentally deliver confidential documents to the wrong office.|
|4|Marine patrols temporarily seal a district during a security exercise.|
|5|Archivists uncover forgotten legal records hidden behind old shelves.|
|6|An emergency prisoner transfer passes through the area under heavy escort.|
|7|Engineers inspect structural damage beneath a government bridge.|
|8|Officials investigate reports of forged identification documents.|
|9|A government courier asks for protection while transporting classified evidence.|
|10|A restricted archive is briefly opened for authorized research.|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

Escort classified legal documents across the island.

Investigate missing evidence from a major criminal case.

Protect an important witness before trial.

Expose corruption within a government department.

Locate stolen judicial archives before they leave Enies Lobby.

Investigate hidden tunnels beneath the courthouse.

Escort engineers repairing critical security infrastructure.

Recover historical legal documents lost during a fire decades ago.

Investigate forged government identification papers.

Protect international delegates attending the National Justice Conference.

Uncover the truth behind an abandoned courtroom sealed for generations.

Investigate unexplained activity beneath the Bridge of Conviction.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## The Forgotten Court

A courtroom abandoned long before the current judicial system.

Its records remain sealed.

---

## Underground Archive Vault

Contains damaged legal records considered too fragile for public access.

---

## Emergency Command Center

Hidden beneath the Administrative Quarter.

Activated only during national emergencies.

---

## Old Security Tunnel

A forgotten maintenance passage connecting several government buildings.

Only fragments of official maps still acknowledge its existence.

---

## Evidence Vault Zero

An extremely secure storage facility containing artifacts and evidence from cases of exceptional importance.

---

## Foundation Chamber

Ancient stone structures discovered beneath modern government buildings.

Their original purpose remains unknown.

---

# SECRETS

Several areas beneath Enies Lobby predate the establishment of the current judicial complex.

Some historical trials remain permanently classified despite their age.

Hidden emergency evacuation routes exist beneath nearly every government building.

Not every confiscated artifact stored within Evidence Vault Zero has ever been publicly documented.

A number of forgotten investigations were quietly closed without official explanation.

Certain handwritten legal records contain references to government institutions that no longer officially exist.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

8–16 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Mid Paradise

Core Themes

- Justice
- Investigation
- Political Intrigue
- Espionage
- Government
- Law
- Security
- Mystery

Enies Lobby should feel fundamentally different from every other island.

The greatest challenge is not survival against nature, but navigating bureaucracy, uncovering hidden truths and operating within one of the most secure government facilities in the world.

Player decisions may permanently affect

- Government Reputation
- Judicial Integrity
- Public Trust
- Security Readiness
- International Relations
- Criminal Investigations
- Intelligence Operations
- Administrative Stability

Every visit to Enies Lobby should remind players that laws, records and information can shape the world just as powerfully as fleets or armies.

# ==================================================
# THRILLER BARK
# ==================================================

Sea: Florian Triangle
Classification: Mobile Ghost Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Thriller Bark is not a natural island.

It is an enormous mobile fortress constructed upon one of the largest ships ever built, drifting silently through the mysterious waters of the Florian Triangle.

Unlike ordinary islands, Thriller Bark constantly changes its position, making navigation nearly impossible without experienced navigators or exceptional luck.

The island has earned a terrifying reputation throughout Paradise.

Merchant crews avoid it.

Marine patrols rarely enter its surrounding waters.

Even experienced pirates often choose longer routes rather than risk sailing through the perpetual darkness surrounding the island.

Although countless ghost stories circulate across the Grand Line, very few people truly know what exists within Thriller Bark.

Many ships enter.

Few are ever seen again.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type

Mobile Fortress Island

Approximate Diameter

32 km

Terrain Distribution

25% Haunted Forest

20% Graveyards

18% Abandoned Town

12% Central Mansion

10% Swamp

8% Rocky Coast

7% Shipyard

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Perpetual Dark Maritime

Spring

# NATURAL RESOURCES

---

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

## Haunted Forest

A dense woodland where towering dead trees block nearly all sunlight.

Visibility rarely exceeds a few dozen meters.

Travelers frequently report hearing voices despite seeing no one nearby.

---

## Central Mansion

An enormous gothic manor overlooking the island.

Built centuries ago using dark stone and reinforced timber.

Its countless halls, towers and underground chambers remain largely unexplored.

---

## Cemetery Fields

Thousands of graves stretch across rolling hills.

Many monuments have become impossible to identify due to age and neglect.

Some graves appear far newer than they should.

---

## Forgotten Village

An abandoned settlement slowly reclaimed by nature.

Buildings remain structurally intact despite decades of apparent abandonment.

Doors occasionally open without explanation.

---

## Black Swamp

A marshland filled with poisonous plants and unstable ground.

Travel becomes extremely dangerous after rainfall.

---

## Western Cliffs

Jagged cliffs overlooking the Florian Triangle.

Violent waves constantly batter the shoreline.

Hidden sea caves exist beneath the rock formations.

---

## Old Shipyard

The remains of an enormous dockyard once used to repair vessels.

Rusted cranes and broken dry docks dominate the landscape.

Many underground workshops remain sealed.

---

# NATURAL PHENOMENA

## Eternal Fog

A supernatural fog surrounds Thriller Bark throughout the year.

Visibility may suddenly fall below five meters.

Sound travels strangely through the mist.

---

## Ghost Lights

Small floating lights appear after sunset.

Most disappear when approached.

Some appear to guide travelers.

Others lead them deeper into danger.

---

## Shadow Mist

Certain areas become unnaturally cold.

Shadows seem darker than normal.

Many explorers describe feelings of being watched.

---

## Midnight Bell

On rare nights, enormous bells echo across the island despite no visible bell towers.

No official explanation exists.

---

# GOVERNMENT

## Administrative System

Unlike ordinary kingdoms, Thriller Bark possesses no unified central government.

Authority is exercised through local settlement councils, influential guilds and community leaders.

Because communication between settlements is difficult, each community maintains significant independence while cooperating during emergencies.

Primary Priorities

- Community Survival
- Monster Suppression
- Resource Management
- Salvage Operations
- Maritime Safety
- Infrastructure Repair

---

## Settlement Councils

Each major settlement elects or appoints respected elders to oversee daily administration.

Construction

Emergency Planning

# CULTURE

## General Culture

Life on Thriller Bark is defined by resilience.

Generations of isolation have taught its people to value practical skills above wealth or social status.

Every resident learns basic survival, navigation and emergency medicine from childhood.

Stories, ghost legends and maritime folklore are deeply woven into everyday life.

Rather than fearing the island itself, locals respect it.

The greatest mistake, they believe, is becoming overconfident.

---

## Hospitality

Visitors are welcomed cautiously.

Common Gifts

Fresh Bread

Warm Blankets

Trust must be earned.

# RUMORS

1. A forgotten ballroom beneath the mansion still contains untouched treasures.

2. Several abandoned houses appear occupied despite showing no signs of life.

3. Strange lights emerge from the cemetery every full moon.

4. Hidden docks beneath the island connect to flooded tunnels.

5. Explorers recently discovered a library untouched for centuries.

6. Salvagers recovered an ancient compass that always points toward the mansion.

7. A massive underground cavern lies beneath the Haunted Forest.

8. Travelers continue disappearing along the western cliffs.

9. An old bell tower rings despite having no visible bell.

10. Some maps suggest portions of Thriller Bark were constructed long before the current fortress.

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|-----------|
|1|A frightened survivor asks for an escort back to Black Hollow.|
|2|Heavy fog reduces visibility to only a few meters.|
|3|Hunters pursue an unusually aggressive predator.|
|4|A collapsing bridge blocks the main road.|
|5|A salvager offers an old artifact recovered from a shipwreck.|
|6|Ghost Lights appear, leading toward unexplored ruins.|
|7|Night Watch patrols question unfamiliar travelers.|
|8|Violent rain floods abandoned streets.|
|9|A forgotten tunnel entrance collapses open.|
|10|Ancient bells echo throughout the island for no apparent reason.|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

Escort salvagers recovering cargo from an abandoned ship.

Investigate disappearances near the cemetery.

Explore forgotten tunnels beneath the mansion.

Protect engineers rebuilding a collapsed bridge.

Recover historical records from an abandoned library.

Escort doctors delivering medicine to isolated settlements.

Investigate unusual activity within the old shipyard.

Map unexplored regions hidden beneath the Haunted Forest.

Recover stolen artifacts before smugglers escape the island.

Discover why Ghost Lights have become increasingly common.

Investigate strange underground vibrations beneath the Central Mansion.

Protect civilians during an unusually violent storm.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## Forgotten Ballroom

A magnificent underground hall preserved beneath the mansion.

Dust covers every surface, yet nothing appears damaged.

---

## Underground Ship Dock

A hidden harbor capable of concealing several ships.

Most entrances remain collapsed.

---

## Library of Echoes

An ancient library containing journals from explorers who vanished centuries ago.

---

## Shadow Cavern

A vast cave beneath the Black Swamp.

Rare glowing minerals illuminate the darkness.

---

## Bell Tower Ruins

An abandoned tower overlooking the island.

Its bells occasionally ring without explanation.

---

## Forgotten Workshop

An old engineering facility hidden beneath Iron Dock.

Several unfinished inventions remain intact.

---

# SECRETS

Historical evidence suggests Thriller Bark has been expanded repeatedly across several centuries.

Large portions of the fortress were built upon structures even older than the ship itself.

Several forgotten tunnels connect distant regions of the island through hidden underground passages.

Ancient journals describe expeditions into the Florian Triangle that encountered phenomena still unexplained today.

Many recovered artifacts originate from ships that officially never existed.

Certain sections of the Central Mansion remain sealed by mechanisms no modern engineer understands.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

8–14 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Mid Paradise

Core Themes

- Gothic Exploration
- Survival
- Mystery
- Horror
- Salvage
- Ancient Ruins
- Isolation
- Maritime Legends

Thriller Bark should feel fundamentally different from every other island in Paradise.

Silence, darkness and uncertainty should be constant companions.

The greatest threats are often psychological as much as physical.

Allow players to question whether strange events are caused by natural phenomena, forgotten technology or simple superstition.

Player decisions may permanently affect

- Settlement Safety
- Salvage Operations
- Public Morale
- Trade Routes
- Exploration Progress
- Crime Activity
- Local Reputation
- Infrastructure Recovery

Every journey through Thriller Bark should leave players wondering whether they truly uncovered the island's secrets—or merely scratched the surface.

# END OF FILE

# ==================================================
# SABAODY ARCHIPELAGO
# ==================================================

Sea: Paradise
Classification: Mangrove Archipelago
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Sabaody Archipelago is the final great crossroads of Paradise and the last major civilization before travelers attempt to enter the New World.

Rather than a single island, Sabaody consists of dozens of interconnected mangrove groves whose enormous roots rise above the sea, creating natural islands.

Every district is built upon the roots of giant Yarukiman Mangrove trees.

These trees continuously produce natural bubbles, allowing unique transportation, architecture, industry and technology unlike anywhere else in the world.

Because every route toward the New World passes nearby, Sabaody attracts nearly every kind of traveler imaginable.

Pirates.

Marines.

Merchants.

Treasure Hunters.

Scientists.

Slave Traders.

World Government Officials.

Foreign Nobles.

Shipwrights.

Bounty Hunters.

Information Brokers.

Criminal Syndicates.

Every day thousands of ships arrive.

Some continue toward the New World.

Many never leave.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type

Mangrove Archipelago

Number of Major Groves

79

Approximate Diameter

58 km

Terrain Distribution

45% Mangrove Roots

25% Urban Districts

15% Commercial Areas

10% Natural Forest

5% Government Facilities

---

# CLIMATE

---

Autumn

Pleasant

---

Winter

Warm

Occasional Storms

Sea Fog During Morning

---

# THE YARUKIMAN MANGROVES

The entire archipelago exists because of enormous Yarukiman Mangrove trees.

Their gigantic roots emerge from the ocean floor and intertwine to create natural islands.

Every Grove is connected through these root systems.

The trees naturally generate bubbles from their resin.

These bubbles have become the foundation of local civilization.

---

## Bubble Characteristics

Naturally Produced

Extremely Light

Transparent

Elastic

Temporary

Sensitive to Sharp Objects

Can support heavy weight depending on size.

Used throughout daily life.

---

## Bubble Applications

Transportation

Housing

Architecture

Cargo

Tourism

Medical Equipment

Entertainment

Industrial Machinery

Scientific Research

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources

Bubble Resin

Mangrove Wood

Fresh Water

Fish

Seafood

Medicinal Plants

Natural Rubber

Rare Flowers

---

Rare Resources

High Purity Bubble Resin

Ancient Mangrove Resin

Sea Prism Stone Fragments

Rare Marine Minerals

Deep Root Crystals

---

# NATURAL PHENOMENA

## Bubble Rain

During certain humid mornings millions of tiny bubbles drift across the archipelago.

Visibility decreases.

Children celebrate it as a seasonal event.

Scientists continue studying its cause.

---

## Root Growth

The mangrove roots slowly expand every year.

Entire districts occasionally require rebuilding.

Roads shift naturally over decades.

---

## Bubble Storm

Rare weather conditions cause unstable bubbles to explode throughout parts of the city.

Transportation temporarily shuts down.

---

## Giant Root Tremors

Massive underwater root movement occasionally causes localized earthquakes.

Buildings are specifically designed to withstand these events.

---

# GROVES 1–79 OVERVIEW SYSTEM

Sabaody Archipelago is divided into 79 Groves.

Each Grove is not just a district but a semi-independent micro-city connected through mangrove root bridges and bubble transport systems.

Below is the structural classification of all Groves.

---

# GROVE CLASSIFICATION SYSTEM

Grove 1–9  
Industrial / Ship Maintenance / Coating Supply

Grove 10–19  
Residential Housing District

Grove 20–29  
Commercial & Entertainment

Grove 30–39  
Tourism & Luxury District

Grove 40–49  
Government Administration

Grove 50–59  
Marine & Security Sector

Grove 60–69  
Science & Research

Grove 70–79  
World Government Restricted Zone

# SABAODY ARCHIPELAGO
# PART 3 (FINAL)

# CULTURE

Sabaody Archipelago is a collision point of the entire world.

Cultures from Paradise, New World routes, and unknown islands merge into one unstable but vibrant society.

Unlike other cities, Sabaody does not have a single identity.

It is defined by arrival and departure.

People come here to leave.

Or to disappear.

---

## GENERAL CULTURE

Core Values

Freedom of Movement

Profit Above All

Information is Currency

Strength Determines Safety

Survival Through Adaptation

---

## DAILY LIFE

Morning

Ship arrivals

Coating operations begin

Market openings

Marine inspections

---

Afternoon

Trade negotiations

Tourist activity

Research operations

Transport congestion

---

Night

Black market expansion

Information trade

Illegal auctions

High-risk transactions

---

## SOCIAL STRUCTURE

World Nobles

Absolute authority within restricted zones

---

Government Officials

Administrative control class

---

Marine Officers

Military enforcement class

---

Merchants

Economic power class

---

Coating Engineers

Highly respected technical class

---

Shadow influence network

---

Workers

Core labor force

---

Underground Population

Illegal traders

Escaped slaves

Criminal syndicates

---

# FESTIVALS

## Arrival Festival

Celebrates ships entering Sabaody.

Entire Groves light up with floating bubbles.

---

## Bubble Storm Night

Artistic festival simulating bubble storms.

Music and light shows across Groves 20–39.

---

## Coating Ceremony

Ships preparing for Fish-Man Island receive blessing-like coating rituals.

Engineers treated like artists.

---

## Market Collapse Day

Historical remembrance of past economic crashes.

Mock auctions and trade games occur.

---

(All original to Parallel World)

Rumor: Controls movements within mangrove root systems

No confirmed identity

Possibly non-human intelligence

---

# RUMORS

1. A hidden Grove exists beyond Grove 79, erased from all maps.

2. Certain bubbles can store human memories.

3. World Nobles travel through invisible routes inside mangrove roots.

4. A slave auction has been operating under Marine protection.

5. Some ships entering Sabaody never leave but are still “seen” at sea.

6. The mangroves may respond to human emotion.

7. A Marine admiral is secretly funding black market auctions.

8. There is a ship coating that can hide a vessel from Haki detection.

9. Information Broker “Silk” is actually multiple people sharing one identity.

10. The Root King may control all transportation bubbles.

---

# RANDOM ENCOUNTERS

Roll 1D10

| Roll | Encounter |
|------|----------|
|1|A bubble transport system collapses mid-air|
|2|Illegal auction invitation delivered to player|
|3|Marine inspection escalates into conflict|
|4|A noble arrives unexpectedly in public zone|
|5|Black market informant offers secret map|
|6|Coating engineer requests urgent escort|
|7|Slave convoy passes through hidden canal|
|8|Bubble storm traps entire district|
|9|Assassination attempt on merchant leader|
|10|Unknown figure appears inside mangrove roots|

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

Infiltrate illegal auctions hidden beneath Groves 20–29

Escort a World Noble through unstable Groves

Investigate disappearing ships after coating process

Expose corruption inside Marine Sabaody division

Track the identity of “Silk” the information broker

Protect engineers developing revolutionary bubble tech

Escape Sabaody while being hunted by multiple factions

Discover the truth behind Grove 79

Stop a slave trade route disguised as tourist transport

Investigate rumors of Root King intelligence

Recover stolen Marine intelligence files

Prevent assassination during Arrival Festival

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## The Forgotten Grove

A Grove erased from official records

Exists between root layers of mangroves

---

## Sub-Bubble Prison

Floating underground detention system

Used for high-value prisoners

---

## Root Network Core

Central control system of mangrove structure

Unknown origin

---

## Silent Auction Depth

Hidden auction hall beneath Groves 23–29

---

## World Noble Passage

Secret transport route inside mangrove roots

Invisible from surface navigation

---

## Coating Abyss

Deep experimental bubble pressure facility

Ships vanish during failed tests

---

# SECRETS

Sabaody is not just a transit point.

It is a filter.

The world passes through it, and only some continue forward.

Some Groves are not physically connected but still accessible.

The World Government does not fully understand the mangroves.

Some bubbles behave as if they are alive.

Certain individuals have “disappeared” but are still recorded as active travelers.

The Root King may not be a person.

It may be the system itself.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Role

Mid to High Paradise Transition Arc

Core Themes

Corruption

Transit Chaos

Identity Loss

Power Hierarchies

Underground Economy

Information Warfare

Survival Pressure

Mystery Systems

---

Sabaody should feel unstable.

Every encounter should carry uncertainty.

Every alliance should feel temporary.

Every escape route should feel incomplete.

This is not a city.

It is a gateway that decides who is worthy to continue the journey.

---

# ==================================================
# BATERILLA
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Baterilla is a peaceful island nation located within South Blue. Though modest in size and population, the island is renowned for its fertile farmland, quiet fishing villages, and unwavering community spirit.

Unlike the bustling trade cities of other Blues, Baterilla values family, craftsmanship, and agriculture above commerce. The island has historically remained politically neutral and has avoided involvement in major conflicts whenever possible.

In the Parallel World, Baterilla has become a favored destination for refugees, retired sailors, and families seeking a peaceful life away from the dangers of piracy.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Medium

Approximate Diameter

88 km

Travel Time by Foot

2 Days

Highest Elevation

Mount Selene

Terrain Distribution

35% Forest

25% Farmland

20% Hills

10% Rivers

10% Coastline

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Temperate Maritime

Spring

Warm rain and blooming fields.

Summer

Sunny with sea breezes.

Autumn

Harvest season.

Winter

Cool with light snowfall in the mountains.

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources

- Fresh Water
- Wheat
- Fruits
- Hardwood
- Fish

Rare Resources

- White Marble
- Healing Herbs

# GOVERNMENT

## Political System

Baterilla is governed by an elected town council supported by village representatives from each region.

Major decisions require approval from both the council and the village assembly, creating a balance between urban and rural interests.

Departments

- Agriculture
- Harbor Administration
- Public Works
- Education
- Public Health
- Trade
- Emergency Services

---

# LAW ENFORCEMENT

## Island Guard

The Island Guard is responsible for maintaining peace across Baterilla.

Responsibilities

- Patrol Villages
- Resolve Civil Disputes
- Protect Trade Routes
- Assist During Storms
- Cooperate with Marines

Because crime is relatively uncommon, guards are well known by local residents.

# CULTURE

## General Culture

Baterilla values family, honesty, and mutual support above personal wealth.

Most residents know each other by name, and strangers are usually welcomed warmly unless they behave suspiciously.

People believe that a peaceful community is stronger than a wealthy one.

---

## Hospitality

Visitors are often invited to share meals with local families.

Travelers staying for several days frequently receive assistance without asking, especially during harvest season.

---

## Social Classes

### Farmers

The backbone of the island's economy.

Highly respected for providing food to the entire population.

---

### Fishermen

Operate both river and coastal fisheries.

Families often pass down boats through generations.

---

### Craftsmen

Known for woodworking, carpentry, and furniture making.

Many shipwrights begin their careers here before moving to larger ports.

---

### Merchants

Responsible for exporting agricultural products throughout South Blue.

---

# EDUCATION

Public education is available in every major settlement.

Core Subjects

- Reading
- Writing
- Mathematics
- Geography
- Agriculture
- Navigation
- History

Many children help their families after school in farms or fishing boats.

---

# RELIGION

No official religion exists.

Residents commonly visit small shrines dedicated to

- Ancestors
- The Sea
- Harvest Spirits

Annual ceremonies are held before planting and harvesting seasons.

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

- Investigate disappearing livestock around Greenfield.
- Escort this year's harvest shipment safely across South Blue.
- Discover who is purchasing enormous food reserves.
- Explore newly uncovered ruins beneath the farmland.
- Recover stolen medicine before an epidemic spreads.
- Rescue missing herbalists from Mount Selene.
- Stop smugglers using abandoned sea caves.
- Search for the legendary Healing Spring.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

## Forgotten Chapel

An abandoned stone chapel hidden inside the forest.

---

## Selene Caverns

Natural caves beneath Mount Selene rich in medicinal plants.

---

## Ancient Irrigation Tunnel

A centuries-old underground water system still partially functional.

---

## Hidden Smuggler Cove

A concealed beach accessible only during low tide.

---

# SECRETS

Several ancient ruins beneath Greenfield predate the current kingdom by hundreds of years.

The Healing Spring truly exists, but its water loses its properties shortly after leaving the source.

One influential merchant secretly finances smugglers to avoid export taxes.

The caves beneath Mount Selene connect to forgotten tunnels extending beneath half the island.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

2–4 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Beginning Characters

Core Themes

- Peaceful Exploration
- Community
- Agriculture
- Family
- Mystery

## GM Guidance

Baterilla should feel like a place worth protecting rather than conquering.

Conflicts here are personal and community-driven instead of world-shaking, making it an excellent location for introducing roleplay, investigation, and emotional storytelling before players enter more dangerous seas.

# ==================================================
# TORINO KINGDOM
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Canon Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Torino Kingdom is a remote island located deep within South Blue, famous for its enormous forests, towering trees, unusual wildlife, and the harmonious relationship between its inhabitants and nature.

Unlike most kingdoms, Torino has never pursued military expansion or commercial dominance. Its greatest treasures are knowledge of medicine, rare plants, and ecological preservation.

In the Parallel World, Torino has become one of the world's leading centers for botanical research. Doctors, herbalists, scholars, and explorers travel here to study plants found nowhere else in the world.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Medium

Approximate Diameter

95 km

Travel Time by Foot

2–3 Days

Highest Elevation

Great Canopy Mountain

Terrain Distribution

55% Forest

20% Mountains

10% Grassland

10% Rivers

5% Settlements

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Humid Tropical

Spring

Warm and rainy.

Summer

Hot with frequent thunderstorms.

Autumn

Comfortable temperatures and abundant harvests.

Winter

Cool mornings with dense fog.

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

- Medicinal Herbs
- Hardwood
- Fresh Water

- Scarlet Moss

# ==================================================
# SUNBURST ISLAND
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Original Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Sunburst Island is a prosperous tropical island famous for its nearly year-round sunshine, fertile volcanic soil, and vast citrus plantations. Nicknamed "The Island of Endless Summer," it supplies fruit, sugar, and tropical products throughout South Blue.

Although peaceful on the surface, competition between merchant companies and fruit exporters creates constant political tension beneath everyday life.

---

# HIDDEN LOCATIONS

---

## Smuggler Tunnel

Ancient irrigation tunnels converted into secret trade routes.

---

# SECRETS

The Fruit Export Guild secretly manipulates market prices across South Blue.

Golden Citrus trees naturally grow only in volcanic soil beneath Mount Solis.

Ancient ruins beneath the volcano belong to a civilization predating the current kingdom.

---

# GM NOTES

Recommended Campaign Length

2–3 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Beginning–Intermediate

Core Themes

- Trade
- Agriculture
- Exploration
- Mystery
- Economic Conflict

## GM Guidance

Sunburst Island provides a balance between peaceful roleplay and commercial intrigue. Most adventures revolve around protecting trade, uncovering corruption, and exploring the dormant volcano that quietly dominates the island.

# ==================================================
# CORALHAVEN
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Original Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Coralhaven is an island built around massive coral reef systems that extend both above and below sea level. The island is famous for its marine biodiversity, underwater settlements, and advanced diving culture.

It is one of the few islands in South Blue where humans, Fish-Men, and other sea-adapted species coexist closely due to the island’s unique semi-aquatic environment.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Medium

Approximate Diameter

85 km

Travel Time by Foot

2 Days (land only)

Highest Elevation

Coral Spire Ridge

Terrain Distribution

30% Coral Reef Structures

25% Coastal Towns

20% Shallow Waters

15% Islands

10% Underwater Caverns

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Warm Oceanic

Year-round Conditions

Stable warm waters with mild surface winds.

Storm Season

Strong underwater currents and surface storms.

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

Primary Resources

- Coral Stone
- Pearls
- Marine Minerals
- Fish
- Sea Plants

Rare Resources

- Blue Coral Crystal
- Deep Pearl
- Luminescent Algae

---

# MAJOR REGIONS

Main hub and trading port.

---

Half-submerged residential area.

Underwater canyon system.

# GM NOTES

2–4 Sessions

Recommended Player Level

Intermediate

Core Themes

- Exploration
- Marine Mystery
- Trade Conflict
- Underwater Survival

## GM Guidance

Coralhaven is ideal for underwater exploration arcs, smuggling investigations, and introducing deep-sea mythology. The environment itself is a major threat as much as enemies.

# ==================================================
# RED LAGOON
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Original Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Red Lagoon is a lawless island formed around a massive blood-red saltwater lagoon surrounded by volcanic cliffs. It is infamous as a haven for pirates, smugglers, bounty hunters, and underground brokers.

Unlike most islands, Red Lagoon has no central government. Instead, it is controlled indirectly by competing criminal syndicates that maintain a fragile balance of power.

The island is often referred to as **"South Blue’s Shadow Market"**.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Medium

Approximate Diameter

92 km

Travel Time by Foot

2–3 Days

Highest Elevation

Crimson Cliffs

Terrain Distribution

30% Volcanic Rock

25% Urban Slums

20% Coastal Caves

15% Lagoon Waters

10% Hidden Facilities

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Volcanic Coastal

Conditions

- Warm air temperature
- High humidity
- Frequent ash winds from dormant vents
- Unstable weather patterns

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

- Salt Crystals
- Volcanic Glass
- Rare Minerals
- Fish (lagoon species)

Rare Resources

- Blood Coral
- Crimson Ore
- Black Salt

# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB-006_AURORA_PORT.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# AURORA PORT
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Original Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Aurora Port is a northern maritime hub famous for its rare phenomenon: glowing sea fog and bioluminescent waters that illuminate the entire coastline at night.

It is one of South Blue’s most important cold-water trade ports, connecting southern routes with northern shipping lanes and acting as a key transfer point for navigation toward the Grand Line approach routes.

The island is known for its disciplined naval presence, advanced navigation science, and strict trade regulation.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Medium–Large

Approximate Diameter

105 km

Travel Time by Foot

3 Days

Highest Elevation

Glacier Crown Ridge

Terrain Distribution

30% Frozen Highlands

25% Coastal Port Cities

20% Boreal Forest

15% Ice Rivers

10% Cliffs

---

# CLIMATE

Climate Type

Cold Maritime

Spring

Meltwater floods and fog.

Summer

Cool and stable.

Autumn

Strong winds and storms.

Winter

Harsh snowstorms and frozen seas.

---

# NATURAL RESOURCES

- Ice Crystals
- Coldwater Fish
- Timber
- Navigation Minerals
- Salt

Rare Resources

- Aurora Ore
- Glow Ice
- Frozen Coral

# ==================================================
# BLOOD MANGROVE
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Forbidden Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Blood Mangrove is a forbidden swamp island covered entirely by massive crimson mangrove forests that bleed red resin when cut.

The island is feared across South Blue due to its toxic environment, extreme disease outbreaks, and the presence of mutated wildlife.

It is officially marked as **“No-Entry Zone”** by multiple Marine divisions.

Rumors claim the island was once used for illegal biological experiments during early World Government expansion.

---

# ==================================================
# WINDSONG ISLE
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Original Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Windsong Isle is a fast-moving trade and travel hub known for its constant strong winds that circle the island year-round. These winds allow ships to accelerate unusually fast, making the island a critical “speed corridor” for South Blue navigation.

It is also famous for its musical culture, where wind patterns are believed to carry “songs of the sea,” inspiring musicians, navigators, and pirates alike.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Medium

Approximate Diameter

90 km

Travel Time by Foot

2 Days

Highest Elevation

25% Coastal Cliffs

15% Forest

15% Port Towns

10% High Altitude Ridges

---

- Constant directional winds
- Sudden gust storms
- Calm “eye zones” between wind cycles
- High sailing efficiency zones

# ==================================================
# SANDGLASS KEY
# ==================================================

Sea: South Blue
Classification: Ancient Mystery Island
World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Sandglass Key is a legendary and heavily restricted island located at the edge of South Blue’s mapped territory.

It is known for its abnormal time-related phenomena, shifting landscapes, and ancient ruins that appear to predate recorded history of the seas.

Most navigation charts label this island as:

> “DO NOT APPROACH – STATIC SPACE ANOMALY”

Only a few Marine expedition logs confirm its existence.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Size

Small–Medium

Approximate Diameter

70 km

1–2 Days (but inconsistent due to spatial distortion)

Highest Elevation

Hourglass Spire

15% Coastal Cliffs

10% Submerged Structures

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_BOUNTIES.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE BOUNTIES SYSTEM
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Bounty systems in South Blue are more complex than East Blue due to:

- Higher presence of syndicates
- More classified threats
- Environmental hazards affecting “danger scoring”
- Marine division specialization per region

Bounties are not only based on combat power but also:

- Economic disruption
- Information sensitivity
- Environmental danger
- Political influence

---

# BASE BOUNTY SCALE (SOUTH BLUE)

| Threat Level | Description | Bounty Range |
|---|---|---:|
| Low Threat | Bandits / small crews | 2M – 8M |
| Rookie Pirates | Early-stage crews | 5M – 15M |
| Established Crews | Regional pirates | 15M – 40M |
| High Threat | Syndicate-level crews | 40M – 120M |
| Disaster Class | Island destabilizers | 120M – 300M |
| Classified Threat | World Government interest | 300M+ (hidden) |

---

# REGION MODIFIERS

## 🌾 Peaceful Zones (Baterilla / Torino)
- -30% bounty reduction
- Crime visibility is low
- Marines prioritize capture over kill

---

## ⚓ Trade Zones (Aurora / Coralhaven / Sunburst)
- Standard bounty
- Higher economic damage weight

---

## ☠️ Lawless Zones (Red Lagoon)
- +50% bounty multiplier
- Syndicate-affiliated crimes included

---

## 🧬 Anomaly Zones (Sandglass Key / Blood Mangrove)
- Bounties may be **classified**
- Some targets have “UNKNOWN VALUE”
- Marine may suppress bounty publication

---

# SPECIAL CLASSIFICATIONS

## 🔴 “BLACK FILE” TARGETS
- No public bounty
- Only Marine HQ + Government records

Examples:
- Sandglass Key anomalies
- Rotmother-type entities
- Chrono research incidents

---

## ☣️ BIOHAZARD TARGETS
(Blood Mangrove category)

- Living mutation threats
- Contagion risk
- Environmental corruption entities

---

## ⚡ FAST ROUTE PIRATES
(Windsong Isle region)

- Bounty adjusted based on ship speed capability
- Pursuit difficulty increases value

---

# DEVIL FRUIT MODIFIER

If user has Devil Fruit:

- Paramecia → +20–50%
- Zoan → +30–70%
- Logia → +100%+

Special Fruits:
- Time / Biological / Wind-related → Classified scaling

---

# MARINE RESPONSE FACTOR

Bounty increases if:

- Marine casualties occur
- Government property destroyed
- Trade routes disrupted
- Classified zones accessed

---

# GM NOTES

This system is designed to:

- Make each island feel economically different
- Link bounty with world systems (not just fighting)
- Allow “story crimes” (information theft, exploration) to matter

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_ECONOMY.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE ECONOMY
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

South Blue Economy is highly fragmented, with strong specialization by island type.

Unlike East Blue which is stable and uniform, South Blue operates as a “cluster economy system”:

- Each island type controls one major resource
- Trade routes are more dangerous but more profitable
- Black markets are more organized and region-based

---

# MAIN ECONOMIC STRUCTURE

## 1. Agricultural Core
(Baterilla, Sunburst Island)

- Food production
- Livestock
- Fruit exports
- Grain supply chains

---

## 2. Maritime Trade Core
(Aurora Port, Coralhaven)

- Shipping logistics
- Navigation services
- Marine infrastructure
- Pearl / mineral trade

---

## 3. Research & Knowledge Core
(Torino Kingdom, Sandglass Key)

- Medicine
- Botany
- Navigation science
- Temporal research (classified)

---

## 4. Shadow Economy Core
(Red Lagoon, Blood Mangrove)

- Smuggling
- Illegal weapons
- Biological trade
- Black market auctions

---

# CURRENCY

Standard Currency

- Belly (Universal)

Secondary Systems

- Trade Credits (Merchant Guild)
- Black Tokens (Illegal market only)

---

# MAJOR EXPORTS

- Fish & seafood
- Citrus & tropical fruit
- Navigation equipment
- Medical herbs
- Pearls & coral materials
- Illegal artifacts (unofficial)

---

# MAJOR IMPORTS

- Steel & weapons
- Medicine
- Luxury goods
- Ship components
- Scientific equipment

---

# TRADE DYNAMICS

- Aurora Port = Main trade hub
- Coralhaven = Underwater trade routes
- Red Lagoon = Illegal redistribution center
- Windsong Isle = High-speed logistics corridor

---

# ECONOMIC RISKS

- Pirate interception
- Syndicate monopolies
- Environmental instability zones
- Government restriction zones (Sandglass Key, Blood Mangrove)

---

# GM NOTES

South Blue economy is designed to create:

- Conflict between legal and illegal trade
- Player-driven supply chain decisions
- Regional economic identity per island cluster

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_HISTORY.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE HISTORY
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

South Blue history is defined by fragmentation, independent island development, and limited centralized control compared to other seas.

Unlike the Grand Line, South Blue never experienced a single world-shaping war—but instead evolved through **localized crises, trade expansion, and hidden government experiments**.

---

# 1. 🌱 EARLY ERA (FOUNDATION AGE)

- Islands developed independently
- Fishing and agriculture were dominant
- Navigation was primitive and coastal-only

Key Event:
- Formation of early island settlements like Baterilla and Torino Kingdom

Result:
👉 Stable but isolated civilizations

---

# 2. ⚓ AGE OF TRADE EXPANSION

- Merchant guilds begin connecting islands
- First structured sea routes established
- Early Marine presence introduced

Key Event:
- Creation of Aurora Port as a central trade hub

Result:
👉 Economic integration begins across South Blue

---

# 3. ☠️ AGE OF PIRATE FRAGMENTATION

- Pirate crews emerge across trade routes
- No large pirate empires form
- Syndicates begin replacing traditional piracy in some regions

Key Event:
- Rise of Red Lagoon black market network

Result:
👉 Crime becomes system-based instead of crew-based

---

# 4. 🧬 AGE OF SECRET EXPERIMENTATION

(World Government classified era)

- Biological research begins in hidden zones
- Environmental experiments conducted
- Early anomaly zones emerge

Key Events:
- Blood Mangrove origin incident
- Sandglass Key temporal distortion event
- Coralhaven underwater expansion tests

Result:
👉 Creation of “forbidden islands”

---

# 5. 🌪️ MODERN ERA (CURRENT TIMELINE)

South Blue becomes:

- A multi-layer economic sea
- A navigation research hub
- A controlled crime ecosystem
- A testing ground for classified World Government projects

---

# MAJOR HISTORICAL INCIDENTS

## 🔴 Red Lagoon Formation Event
- Collapse of old port authority
- Syndicates took control
- Official government withdrawal

---

## 🧬 Blood Mangrove Incident
- Biological contamination outbreak
- Entire research base lost
- Area declared quarantine zone

---

## 🕰️ Sandglass Key Anomaly
- Temporal distortion first recorded
- Multiple expedition disappearances
- Area sealed by Chrono Division

---

## ⚡ Windsong Navigation Revolution
- Discovery of wind-speed travel corridors
- Major increase in trade efficiency
- Pirate mobility drastically increased

---

# WORLD GOVERNMENT ROLE

South Blue was not directly conquered or unified.

Instead, the government operates through:

- Trade regulation hubs
- Marine specialized divisions
- Classified research zones
- Indirect syndicate monitoring

---

# PIRACY EVOLUTION

1. Early Era → Small pirate crews
2. Trade Era → Route-based piracy
3. Modern Era → Syndicate piracy + anomaly exploitation

---

# CURRENT STATE OF SOUTH BLUE

South Blue is considered:

- Stable economically
- Unstable in hidden zones
- Highly valuable strategically
- Dangerous in uncharted regions

---

# GM NOTES

South Blue history is designed to:

- Explain why each island is unique
- Justify anomalies (Blood Mangrove / Sandglass Key)
- Support faction-based storytelling
- Provide long-term campaign evolution hooks

Core idea:
👉 “History is layered, not linear”

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_MARINES.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE MARINES SYSTEM
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

The South Blue Marine structure is more fragmented and specialized than East Blue.

Instead of a single unified force, it operates as a **multi-division adaptive system**, designed to handle:

- Syndicate crime networks
- Environmental anomaly zones
- High-speed piracy routes
- Biological hazard regions
- Temporal instability areas

---

# MAIN STRUCTURE

## 1. SOUTH BLUE HEADQUARTERS
Central command overseeing all operations.

Responsibilities:
- Strategic planning
- Bounty classification approval
- Classified zone authorization

---

## 2. SPECIALIZED DIVISIONS

### ⚓ Trade Protection Fleet
(Sea routes: Aurora / Coralhaven / Sunburst)

- Escort merchant ships
- Protect trade corridors
- Anti-piracy interception

---

### ⚡ FAST RESPONSE UNIT
(Windsong Isle influence)

- High-speed pursuit ships
- Interception of fast-route pirates
- Rapid deployment across islands

---

### 🧬 BIOHAZARD CONTAINMENT UNIT
(Blood Mangrove)

- Quarantine enforcement
- Mutation containment
- Experimental sample retrieval

---

### 🕰️ CHRONOLOGY DIVISION (CLASSIFIED)
(Sandglass Key)

- Temporal anomaly research
- Time distortion containment
- Expedition suppression

---

### ☠️ UNDERCOVER INTELLIGENCE UNIT
(Red Lagoon)

- Syndicate infiltration
- Black market surveillance
- Identity masking operations

---

# MARINE BASE TYPES

## Regional Headquarters
- Large command bases
- Connected to HQ network

## Coastal Bases
- Standard patrol control

## Outposts
- Remote island surveillance

## Black Sites (CLASSIFIED)
- Blood Mangrove
- Sandglass Key

---

# PATROL SYSTEM

| Level | Description |
|---|---|
| I | Harbor security |
| II | Island patrol |
| III | Sea lane patrol |
| IV | Anti-pirate operations |
| V | Emergency / anomaly response |

---

# FLEET STRUCTURE

## Patrol Ship
- Fast interception
- Small crew

## Warship
- Standard combat operations

## Heavy Battleship
- Syndicate / large pirate engagement

## Experimental Vessel
- Used in Sandglass Key operations

---

# JUSTICE SYSTEM TYPES

## ⚖️ PROTECTIVE JUSTICE
- Civilian safety priority
- Common in Baterilla / Torino zones

## ⚖️ BALANCED JUSTICE
- Standard Marine doctrine
- Trade zones

## ⚖️ ABSOLUTE CONTROL
- Applied in anomaly zones
- Sandglass Key / Blood Mangrove

---

# CORRUPTION LEVEL

South Blue Marines are:

- Low corruption in peaceful zones
- Moderate corruption in trade hubs
- High risk infiltration in Red Lagoon border regions

Corruption is treated as:
👉 “Story event generator”, not default behavior

---

# RELATIONSHIP NETWORK

## Civilians
Generally positive

## Merchants
Strong cooperation

## Pirates
Hostile but case-dependent

## Syndicates
Covert warfare / infiltration

## World Government
Direct oversight on classified zones only

---

# GM NOTES

South Blue Marines are designed to:

- Feel like multiple organizations, not one army
- React dynamically to island types
- Create layered conflict (law vs anomaly vs economy)

Key design principle:
👉 “Different justice for different reality zones”

---

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_PIRATES.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE PIRATES SYSTEM
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Piracy in South Blue is not a single unified culture.

Instead, it is divided into **4 Pirate Archetypes**, shaped by geography, economy, and anomaly zones.

Unlike East Blue pirates (mostly small crews), South Blue pirates include:

- Organized syndicates
- Research-based crews
- Speed/navigation specialists
- Mutation survivors

---

# PIRATE CLASSIFICATIONS

## 1. ⚓ TRADITIONAL PIRATES
(Common in Sunburst / Aurora / Coralhaven routes)

- Crew size: 10–40
- Focus: Raiding, treasure hunting
- Weak against Marines

---

## 2. ☠️ SYNDICATE PIRATES
(Red Lagoon influence)

- Crew size: 50–300 (network-based)
- Structure: Mafia-style hierarchy
- Activities:
  - Smuggling
  - Assassination contracts
  - Illegal auctions
- Extremely organized

---

## 3. 🧭 EXPLORER PIRATES
(Torino / Sandglass Key influence)

- Focus: Discovery, ruins, forbidden zones
- Often not hostile unless provoked
- May cooperate with scholars or governments

---

## 4. ⚡ FAST-ROUTE PIRATES
(Windsong Isle influence)

- Specialize in high-speed ships
- Hit-and-run tactics
- Difficult to capture
- Often act as smugglers or escorts

---

## 5. 🧬 MUTATION SURVIVOR PIRATES
(Blood Mangrove influence)

- Physically altered crews
- Unstable abilities
- Often unpredictable behavior
- Sometimes non-human intelligence

---

# DEVIL FRUIT DISTRIBUTION

| Type | Frequency |
|---|---|
| Paramecia | Common |
| Zoan | Uncommon |
| Logia | Rare |
| Special/Anomaly | Extremely Rare |

Special Fruits often appear in:
- Sandglass Key (time-related rumors)
- Blood Mangrove (bio mutations)
- Red Lagoon (illegal trade)

---

# PIRATE ECONOMY ROLE

Pirates are not just fighters:

- Smuggling transporters
- Information brokers
- Illegal explorers
- Syndicate enforcers
- Navigation specialists

---

# RELATIONSHIP WITH MARINES

## Peace Zones
- Capture & release possible
- Negotiation exists

## Trade Zones
- Active pursuit
- Escort conflicts common

## Lawless Zones
- Open warfare possible

## Anomaly Zones
- Containment priority over capture

---

# MAJOR PIRATE BEHAVIOR PATTERNS

- Avoid Aurora Port direct conflict
- Use Windsong Isle for fast escape routes
- Hide in Coralhaven underwater tunnels
- Trade through Red Lagoon networks
- Investigate Sandglass Key rumors

---

# GM NOTES

South Blue pirates are designed to be:

- More “system-based” than brute force
- Integrated into economy and navigation systems
- Capable of becoming allies or enemies depending on arc

This creates:
👉 Dynamic faction storytelling instead of static enemies

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_ROUTES.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE ROUTES SYSTEM
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

South Blue trade routes are significantly more complex than East Blue due to:

- Environmental anomaly zones
- Syndicate-controlled corridors
- High-speed wind routes
- Underwater passage networks
- Classified navigation paths

Routes are divided into **5 major categories**.

---

# 1. 🌾 STANDARD TRADE ROUTE NETWORK

Main civilian and merchant routes.

## Primary Chain Route
Baterilla → Sunburst Island → Aurora Port → Coralhaven → Loguetown Gateway (East Blue connection point)

Purpose:
- Food trade
- Merchant transport
- Civilian travel

---

# 2. ☠️ DANGEROUS ROUTES

High piracy / conflict zones

## Red Corridor Route
Sunburst Island → Red Lagoon → Coralhaven

Risks:
- Syndicate interception
- Illegal taxation
- Ship hijacking

---

## Mangrove Shadow Route
Coralhaven → Blood Mangrove → Unmapped exit points

Risks:
- Biological contamination
- Navigation loss
- Ship destruction

---

# 3. ⚡ FAST WIND ROUTES

(Windsong Isle system)

## Aeolus Speed Corridor
Windsong Isle → Aurora Port → Coralhaven (High-speed loop)

Advantages:
- 2–3x faster travel
- Reduced fuel/time cost

Risks:
- Sudden wind storms
- Ship instability zones

---

# 4. 🧭 RESEARCH / RESTRICTED ROUTES

## Northern Knowledge Path
Torino Kingdom → Sandglass Key → Aurora Port (classified)

Purpose:
- Research expeditions
- Government operations
- Artifact recovery missions

Status:
- Restricted access
- Marine escort required

---

# 5. 🌊 ANOMALY ROUTES (UNKNOWN NAVIGATION)

## Temporal Drift Route
Sandglass Key → Unknown exit points

Effects:
- Time distortion
- Route shifting
- Possible re-entry in different coordinates

---

## Coral Depth Network
Coralhaven → Underwater tunnel systems → unknown sea exits

Effects:
- Submarine navigation required
- Risk of entrapment
- Hidden smuggling access

---

# WORLD GOVERNMENT CONTROL POINTS

- Aurora Port (inspection hub)
- Sandglass Key (black classified zone)
- Blood Mangrove perimeter blockade
- Red Lagoon surveillance border

---

# ROUTE DANGER SCALE

| Level | Meaning |
|---|---|
| 1 | Safe trade route |
| 2 | Minor pirate activity |
| 3 | Active danger zone |
| 4 | High risk survival route |
| 5 | Extreme / classified anomaly |

---

# GM NOTES

South Blue routes are designed to:

- Connect story arcs between islands naturally
- Force player decision-making in navigation
- Create “risk vs reward travel planning”
- Enable hidden world discovery through anomaly routes

Core idea:
👉 “Travel is gameplay, not just transition”

---

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_RUMORS.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE RUMORS SYSTEM
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

Rumors in South Blue are a core narrative engine.

They are used by Game Masters to:
- Trigger story arcs
- Seed hidden factions
- Connect islands indirectly
- Introduce future threats
- Foreshadow world-level events

Unlike factual records, rumors may be:
- True
- Partially true
- Completely false
- Deliberately planted misinformation

---

# 🌾 COMMON RUMORS (LOW LEVEL)

1. A merchant ship vanished near Sunburst Island carrying rare fruit seeds.
2. Aurora Port’s glowing sea is getting brighter every year.
3. Torino Kingdom discovered a plant that can heal fatal injuries.
4. Fishermen in Baterilla saw a “moving island” in the distance.
5. Windsong Isle wind patterns suddenly changed direction for one day.

---

# ⚓ TRADE ROUTE RUMORS

6. A secret route bypasses all Marine checkpoints between Coralhaven and Aurora Port.
7. Ships using Windsong Isle currents arrive before they leave.
8. A hidden merchant guild controls all fruit pricing in South Blue.
9. Illegal maps are being sold that include Sandglass Key.

---

# ☠️ PIRATE & CRIME RUMORS

10. Red Lagoon is planning to unify all syndicates under one ruler.
11. A Devil Fruit is being auctioned inside Coralhaven’s underwater tunnels.
12. Blood Mangrove survivors are immune to Marine weapons.
13. A pirate crew uses wind currents as a weapon system.

---

# 🧬 ANOMALY RUMORS

14. Sandglass Key may not exist in a single timeline.
15. People who enter Blood Mangrove sometimes return… unchanged but not the same.
16. Windsong Isle is slowly drifting across the sea map.
17. Coralhaven reefs are forming patterns that resemble ancient writing.

---

# 🕰️ CLASSIFIED / WORLD GOVERNMENT RUMORS

18. Sandglass Key is a failed World Government experiment.
19. Blood Mangrove was originally a Marine biological weapon project.
20. Chrono Division is hiding evidence of time manipulation.
21. A “forbidden sea route” connects all anomaly zones.

---

# 🔥 HIGH IMPACT RUMORS (WORLD ARC TRIGGERS)

22. A map exists that connects all 9 South Blue islands in a perfect circle.
23. One of the islands is not natural—it was “placed” into the sea.
24. A hidden war between syndicates and World Government is already ongoing.
25. A Devil Fruit user can control entire trade routes.
26. The South Blue sea itself may be artificially stabilized.

---

# 🎭 GM USAGE SYSTEM

Each rumor has 3 layers:

## Layer 1: Surface Info
What players hear casually.

## Layer 2: Investigation Layer
What becomes true after research.

## Layer 3: Truth Layer
Actual world lore or hidden system truth.

---

# 🎯 DESIGN PURPOSE

South Blue rumors are designed to:

- Connect all islands into one narrative ecosystem
- Create long-term mystery arcs
- Allow player-driven investigation
- Bridge into Grand Line escalation

Core idea:
👉 “Nothing is just flavor. Everything is a hook.”

---

# END OF SOUTH BLUE CORE SYSTEM

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\SOUTH_BLUE\SB_SEA_INFORMATION.md
# =====================================================

# ==================================================
# SOUTH BLUE SEA INFORMATION
# ==================================================

World Type: One Piece Parallel World

---

# OVERVIEW

South Blue is a volatile and diverse sea compared to East Blue.

While East Blue is stable and beginner-friendly, South Blue is:

- More politically fragmented
- More biologically diverse
- More crime-prone in certain regions
- More extreme in environmental variation

It is considered a “transition sea” between beginner seas and the Grand Line.

---

# SEA CHARACTERISTICS

Navigation Difficulty

Medium

Weather Stability

Medium–Low (unpredictable zones exist)

Sea King Activity

Moderate

Average Wave Height

2–8 meters

Visibility

Variable (fog zones in multiple regions)

---

# REGIONAL TYPES

South Blue is divided into 4 major environmental categories:

## 1. Trade-Heavy Zones
- Sunburst Island
- Aurora Port
- Coralhaven

Stable economy, strong Marine presence.

---

## 2. Lawless Zones
- Red Lagoon
- Blood Mangrove (restricted)

High piracy, smuggling networks.

---

## 3. Natural/Peaceful Zones
- Baterilla
- Torino Kingdom

Low crime, high agriculture and research.

---

## 4. Anomaly Zones
- Sandglass Key
- Windsong Isle (wind distortion fields)

Unstable physics or extreme environmental effects.

---

# NAVIGATION SYSTEM

South Blue requires:

- Standard Compass
- Sea Charts
- Wind Reading (important in Windsong Isle region)
- Coral Depth Mapping (Coralhaven region)

Log Pose is optional but recommended near anomaly zones.

---

# STRATEGIC ROLE

South Blue functions as:

- 🌾 Food supplier (Baterilla, Sunburst)
- 🔬 Research hub (Torino, Sandglass Key)
- ⚓ Trade corridor (Aurora Port, Coralhaven)
- ☠️ Criminal network hub (Red Lagoon)
- 🌪️ Navigation innovation zone (Windsong Isle)

---

# MILITARY IMPORTANCE

Compared to East Blue:

- More Marine specialization units
- More experimental operations
- More classified zones (Sandglass Key, Blood Mangrove)

---

# PIRACY LEVEL

Overall Threat

Medium–High

Notes:
- Fewer “massive pirate crews”
- More organized syndicates in specific zones
- More hidden operations than open warfare

---

# WORLD GOVERNMENT INTEREST

High Priority Zones:

- Sandglass Key (TOP SECRET)
- Blood Mangrove (BIOHAZARD CLASSIFIED)
- Red Lagoon (CRIMINAL NETWORK MONITORING)
- Aurora Port (STRATEGIC NAVIGATION HUB)

---

# GM NOTES

South Blue is designed for:

- Mid-campaign progression
- Transition from beginner to advanced world understanding
- Introduction of hidden world mechanics (time, biology, wind, smuggling networks)

Player experience should shift from:
“exploration” → “systems awareness of the world”

# END OF FILE

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\WEST_BLUE\WB-001_ILUSIA_KINGDOM.md
# =====================================================

# ILUSIA KINGDOM

Sea: West Blue  
Classification: Kingdom Island  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Ilusia Kingdom is one of the most politically influential nations in West Blue. It is known for its strict governance, advanced bureaucracy, and strong ties with the World Government.

Unlike most kingdoms that rely heavily on military force or trade dominance, Ilusia maintains power through **administrative control, intelligence networks, and economic leverage**.

The kingdom is often described as “quietly absolute” — it does not expand aggressively, but its influence spreads through diplomacy, contracts, and covert agreements.

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Island Type

Large Continental Island

Total Area

~18,000 km²

Terrain Distribution

- 40% Plains (Capital Regions)
- 25% Forest
- 15% Hills
- 10% Farmland
- 10% Coastal Zones

Climate

Temperate Oceanic Climate

- Mild winters
- Stable seasons
- Frequent coastal fog

Key Feature

Central Plateau where the Royal Capital is located

---

# KEY REGIONS

## Royal Capital – “Aurelia”

The political heart of Ilusia Kingdom.

- Royal Palace
- Government Ministries
- Noble District
- Foreign Embassy Zone

---

## East Trade Port – “Lys Harbor”

Primary export/import hub.

- Merchant fleets
- World Government supply ships
- Naval checkpoints

---

## Verdant Farmlands

Agricultural backbone of the kingdom.

Produces:
- Grain
- Livestock
- Medicinal herbs

---

## Blackwood Forest

Dense forest region with limited access.

Rumored to contain:
- Illegal research facilities
- Hidden rebel cells

---

## North Ridge Military Zone

Heavily restricted zone controlled by Royal Guard.

- Training facilities
- Weapon storage
- Strategic command base

---

# GOVERNMENT / CONTROL

System Type

Monarchy under World Government oversight

Ruler

King Regulus V

Power Structure

- Royal Family (symbolic + executive authority)
- Ministry Council (real administrative power)
- World Government Envoys (oversight)

Internal Reality

True power is shared between:
- Nobility houses
- Ministry elites
- World Government liaison office

---

# ECONOMY

Economic Type

Highly centralized planned economy with strong trade sector

Primary Exports

- Grain supplies
- Timber
- Medical herbs
- Manufactured tools

Secondary Exports

- Navigation equipment
- Luxury goods for nobles

Trade Strength

★★★★★ (West Blue Tier 1)

---

# MILITARY / SECURITY

Royal Guard Strength

Approx. 8,000 personnel

Structure

- Capital Defense Corps
- Intelligence Division
- Port Security Force

World Government Presence

- Cipher Bureau observers
- Marine liaison unit stationed at Lys Harbor

---

# CRIME / CONFLICT

Crime Level

Low (Surface) / Medium (Hidden)

Surface Crime:
- Petty theft
- Smuggling attempts at ports

Hidden Crime:
- Political corruption
- Illegal experimentation in Blackwood Forest
- Noble assassination plots

---

# IMPORTANT NPCS

## King Regulus V
Age: 63  
Role: King of Ilusia Kingdom  
Traits:
- Politically cautious
- Strategically passive
- Deeply dependent on council

---

## Chancellor Marius Bell
Age: 52  
Role: Head of Ministry Council  
Traits:
- Real power behind the throne
- Master manipulator
- Controls taxation & trade policy

---

## Captain Elira Dawn
Age: 34  
Role: Commander of Royal Guard  
Traits:
- Strict justice
- Loyal to kingdom (not individuals)
- Investigates internal corruption

---

## Ambassador Harkin Vale
Age: 45  
Role: World Government Liaison  
Traits:
- Calm diplomat
- Hidden CP influence suspected

---

# RUMORS

1. A secret council controls the king’s decisions.
2. Blackwood Forest hides a forbidden research lab.
3. A noble family is funding pirates in West Blue.
4. The Royal Guard commander is investigating the ministry.
5. Ancient weapons are stored beneath the capital.
6. A revolutionary cell exists inside the palace staff.

---

# ADVENTURE HOOKS

- Investigate corruption inside the Ministry Council  
- Escort World Government envoy through Ilusia  
- Discover hidden lab in Blackwood Forest  
- Prevent assassination attempt on royal family  
- Uncover smuggling route through Lys Harbor  
- Investigate disappearance of royal scholars  

---

# SECRETS

- The Ministry Council effectively controls the kingdom
- Royal authority is largely ceremonial in practice
- Blackwood Forest contains early-stage Devil Fruit research
- World Government uses Ilusia as intelligence hub in West Blue

---

# GM NOTES

Ilusia Kingdom is a **political pressure core** of West Blue.

Use it to:
- Introduce political intrigue arcs
- Connect World Government operations
- Seed revolution storyline
- Create long-term faction manipulation plots

Tone: Controlled, elegant, dangerous beneath surface

# =====================================================
# FILE : 01_WORLD\ISLANDS\WEST_BLUE\WB-002_FROSTHAVEN.md
# =====================================================

# FROSTHAVEN

Sea: West Blue  
Classification: Kingdom / Frozen Archipelago  
World Type: One Piece Parallel World  

---

# OVERVIEW

Frosthaven is a massive frozen kingdom located in the far northern reaches of West Blue. Unlike typical winter islands, Frosthaven is permanently covered in ice due to an abnormal oceanic cold current known as the **“White Undertow”**.

The kingdom is both a strategic naval chokepoint and a dangerous scientific anomaly. Ships that pass too close often report navigation failure, frozen compasses, and hallucinations caused by extreme cold magnetic distortion.

Frosthaven is officially a kingdom under World Government oversight, but in reality it is a **semi-autonomous cold-zone fortress civilization**.

---

# ISLAND STRUCTURE

Frosthaven is not a single island but a **cluster of 5 major frozen landmasses**:

- North Spire Island (Capital)
- Iceveil Island (Industrial Zone)
- Glacier Chain (Mining Region)
- Silent Sea Platform (Naval Zone)
- Whitegrave Island (Unknown Restricted Zone)

---

# GEOGRAPHY

Total Area

~22,500 km²

Terrain Distribution

- 70% Ice Sheet
- 15% Frozen Forest
- 10% Rocky Mountains
- 5% Coastal Ice Shelf

Climate

Permanent Sub-Zero Climate

- Temperature: -10°C to -45°C
- Constant snowstorm zones
- Icequake activity in deeper regions

Natural Phenomenon

White Undertow Current  
→ distorts compasses & disrupts navigation routes

---

# MAJOR REGIONS (PART 1)

## NORTH SPIRE ISLAND (CAPITAL CORE)

The administrative heart of Frosthaven.

Features:
- Frosthaven Royal Citadel
- Government Ice Palace
- Research Directorate HQ
- Civil Settlement Domes

Population:
~18,000

---

## ICEVEIL ISLAND (INDUSTRIAL CORE)

Primary production zone.

Industries:
- Ice-forged steel production
- Cold-resistant shipbuilding
- Thermal clothing manufacturing

Special Facility:
- Cryo-Tech Foundry Complex

---

## GLACIER CHAIN (MINING ZONE)

Mountainous ice cliffs rich in rare minerals.

Resources:
- Frozen Iron Ore
- Blue Cryo Crystal
- Sub-zero Quartz

Hazards:
- Ice collapses
- Frozen Sea Kings (rare sightings)

---

# GOVERNMENT

System Type

Military Monarchy under World Government observation

Ruler

Queen Isolde Valkyr

Power Structure

- Royal Ice Court
- Scientific Directorate
- World Government Cold Division

True Control Layer

Scientific Directorate holds **practical operational control**

---

# MILITARY / DEFENSE

Frosthaven Defense Corps

Strength: ~11,500

Divisions:
- Ice Infantry Units
- Cryo Naval Fleet
- Arctic Recon Division

Special Unit:
“White Fang Division” (elite cold-zone assassins)

---

# ECONOMY

Economic Type

Resource + Military Industry Hybrid Economy

Exports:
- Cryo Steel
- Cold-resistant gear
- Navigation stabilizers

Imports:
- Food supplies
- Medical goods
- Fuel

Economic Role in West Blue:
Strategic Military Supplier

---

# CRIME / UNDERWORLD

Surface Crime:
- Low (strict military control)

Hidden Crime:
- Illegal Cryo experiments
- Smuggling of Cryo crystals
- Disappearing research subjects

Rumored Black Site:
“WHITEGRAVE PROJECT”

---

# IMPORTANT NPCS

## Queen Isolde Valkyr
Age: 39  
Role: Ruler of Frosthaven  
Traits:
- Calm but authoritarian
- Obsessed with stability
- Deeply secretive about Whitegrave Island
